{ViPur, 1, 1}
parāśaraṃ munivaraṃ kṛtapūrvāhṇikakriyam | [ViPur, 1, 1 1.1]
maitreyaḥ paripapraccha praṇipatyābhivādya ca | [ViPur, 1, 1 1.2]
tvatto hi vedādhyayanam adhītam akhilaṃ guro | [ViPur, 1, 1 2.1]
dharmaśāstrāṇi sarvāṇi vedāṅgāni yathākramam | [ViPur, 1, 1 2.2]
tvatprasādān muniśreṣṭha mām anye nākṛtaśramam | [ViPur, 1, 1 3.1]
vakṣyanti sarvaśāstreṣu prāyaśo ye 'pi vidviṣaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 3.2]
so 'ham icchāmi dharmajña śrotuṃ tvatto yathā jagat | [ViPur, 1, 1 4.1]
babhūva bhūyaś ca yathā mahābhāga bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 1, 1 4.2]
yanmayaṃ ca jagad brahman yataś caitac carācaram | [ViPur, 1, 1 5.1]
līnam āsīd yathā yatra layam eṣyati yatra ca | [ViPur, 1, 1 5.2]
yatpramāṇāni bhūtāni devādīnāṃ ca saṃbhavam | [ViPur, 1, 1 6.1]
samudraparvatānāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ ca yathā bhuvaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 6.2]
sūryādīnāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ pramāṇaṃ munisattama | [ViPur, 1, 1 7.1]
devādīnāṃ tathā vaṃśān manūn manvantarāṇi ca | [ViPur, 1, 1 7.2]
kalpān kalpavikalpāṃś ca caturyugavikalpitān | [ViPur, 1, 1 8.1]
kalpāntasya svarūpaṃ ca yugadharmāṃś ca kṛtsnaśaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 8.2]
devarṣipārthivānāṃ ca caritaṃ yan mahāmune | [ViPur, 1, 1 9.1]
vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ yathāvad vyāsakartṛkam | [ViPur, 1, 1 9.2]
dharmāṃś ca brāhmaṇādīnāṃ tathā cāśramavāsinām | [ViPur, 1, 1 10.1]
śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ sarvaṃ tvatto vāsiṣṭhanandana | [ViPur, 1, 1 10.2]
brahman prasādapravaṇaṃ kuruṣva mayi mānasam | [ViPur, 1, 1 11.1]
yenāham etaj jānīyāṃ tvatprasādān mahāmune | [ViPur, 1, 1 11.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 1, 1 12.1]
sādhu maitreya dharmajña smārito 'smi purātanam | [ViPur, 1, 1 12.2]
pituḥ pitā me bhagavān vasiṣṭho yad uvāca ha | [ViPur, 1, 1 12.3]
viśvāmitraprayuktena rakṣasā bhakṣito mayā | [ViPur, 1, 1 13.1]
śrutas tātas tataḥ krodho maitreyāsīn mamātulaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 13.2]
tato 'haṃ rakṣasāṃ satraṃ vināśāya samārabham | [ViPur, 1, 1 14.1]
bhasmīkṛtāś ca śataśas tasmin satre niśācarāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 14.2]
tataḥ saṃkṣīyamāṇeṣu teṣu rakṣaḥsv aśeṣataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 15.1]
mām uvāca mahābhāgo vasiṣṭho 'smatpitāmahaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 15.2]
alam atyantakopena tāta manyum imaṃ jahi | [ViPur, 1, 1 16.1]
rākṣasā nāparādhyante pitus te vihitaṃ tathā | [ViPur, 1, 1 16.2]
mūḍhānām eṣa bhavati krodho jñānavatāṃ kutaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 17.1]
hanyate tāta kaḥ kena yataḥ svakṛtabhuk pumān | [ViPur, 1, 1 17.2]
saṃcitasyāpi mahatā vatsa kleśena mānavaiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 18.1]
yaśasas tapasaś caiva krodho nāśakaraḥ paraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 18.2]
svarga apavarga vyāsedha kāraṇam parama ṛṣayaḥ varjayanti sadā krodham tātaiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 499609_1]
mā tad vaśaḥ bhava | [ViPur, 1, 1 499609_2]
alaṃ niśācarair dagdhair dīnair anaparādhibhiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 20.1]
satraṃ te viramatv etat kṣamāsārā hi sādhavaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 20.2]
evaṃ tātena tenāham anunīto mahātmanā | [ViPur, 1, 1 21.1]
upasaṃhṛtavān satraṃ sadyas tadvākyagauravāt | [ViPur, 1, 1 21.2]
tataḥ prītaḥ sa bhagavān vasiṣṭho munisattamaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 22.1]
samprāptaś ca tadā tatra pulastyo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 22.2]
pitāmahena datta arghyaḥ kṛta āsana parigrahaḥ mām uvāca mahābhāgaḥ maitreyaiḥ pulaha agrajaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 499617_1]
pulastya uvāca | [ViPur, 1, 1 24.1]
vaire mahati yad vākyād guror asyāśritā kṣamā | [ViPur, 1, 1 24.2]
tvayā tasmāt samastāni bhavāñchāstrāṇi vetsyati | [ViPur, 1, 1 24.3]
saṃtater na mamocchedaḥ kruddhenāpi yataḥ kṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 25.1]
tvayā tasmān mahābhāga dadāmy anyaṃ mahāvaram | [ViPur, 1, 1 25.2]
purāṇasaṃhitākartā bhavān vatsa bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 1, 1 26.1]
devatāpāramārthyaṃ ca yathāvad vetsyate bhavān | [ViPur, 1, 1 26.2]
pravṛtte ca nivṛtte ca karmaṇy astamalā matiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 27.1]
matprasādād asaṃdigdhā tava vatsa bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 1, 1 27.2]
tataś ca bhagavān prāha vasiṣṭho me pitāmahaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 28.1]
pulastyena yad uktaṃ te sarvam etad bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 1, 1 28.2]
iti pūrvaṃ vasiṣṭhena pulastyena ca dhīmatā | [ViPur, 1, 1 29.1]
yad uktaṃ tat smṛtiṃ yātaṃ tvatpraśnād akhilaṃ mama | [ViPur, 1, 1 29.2]
so 'haṃ vadāmy aśeṣaṃ te maitreya paripṛcchate | [ViPur, 1, 1 30.1]
purāṇasaṃhitāṃ samyak tāṃ nibodha yathātatham | [ViPur, 1, 1 30.2]
viṣṇoḥ sakāśād udbhūtaṃ jagat tatraiva ca sthitam | [ViPur, 1, 1 31.1]
sthitisaṃyamakartāsau jagato 'sya jagac ca saḥ | [ViPur, 1, 1 31.2]
{ViPur, 1, 2}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 1, 2 1.1]
avikārāya śuddhāya nityāya paramātmane | [ViPur, 1, 2 1.2]
sadaikarūparūpāya viṣṇave sarvajiṣṇave | [ViPur, 1, 2 1.3]
namo hiraṇyagarbhāya haraye śaṃkarāya ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 2.1]
vāsudevāya tārāya sargasthityantakāriṇe | [ViPur, 1, 2 2.2]
ekānekasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmātmane namaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 3.1]
avyaktavyaktarūpāya viṣṇave muktihetave | [ViPur, 1, 2 3.2]
sargasthitivināśānāṃ jagato yo jaganmayaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 4.1]
mūlabhūto namas tasmai viṣṇave paramātmane | [ViPur, 1, 2 4.2]
ādhārabhūtaṃ viśvasyāpy aṇīyāṃsam aṇīyasām | [ViPur, 1, 2 5.1]
praṇamya sarvabhūtastham acyutaṃ puruṣottamam | [ViPur, 1, 2 5.2]
jñānasvarūpam atyantanirmalaṃ paramārthataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 6.1]
tam evārthasvarūpeṇa bhrāntidarśanataḥ sthitam | [ViPur, 1, 2 6.2]
viṣṇuṃ grasiṣṇuṃ viśvasya sthitisarge tathā prabhum | [ViPur, 1, 2 7.1]
praṇamya jagatām īśam ajam akṣayam avyayam | [ViPur, 1, 2 7.2]
kathayāmi yathāpūrvaṃ dakṣādyair munisattamaiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 8.1]
pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān abjayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 8.2]
taiś coktaṃ purukutsāya bhūbhuje narmadātaṭe | [ViPur, 1, 2 9.1]
sārasvatāya tenāpi mama sārasvatena ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 9.2]
paraḥ parāṇāṃ paramaḥ paramātmātmasaṃsthitaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 10.1]
rūpavarṇādinirdeśaviśeṣaṇavivarjitaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 10.2]
apakṣayavināśābhyāṃ pariṇāmarddhijanmabhiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 11.1]
varjitaḥ śakyate vaktuṃ yaḥ sadāstīti kevalam | [ViPur, 1, 2 11.2]
sarvatrāsau samastaṃ ca vasaty atreti vai yataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 12.1]
tataḥ sa vāsudeveti vidvadbhiḥ paripaṭhyate | [ViPur, 1, 2 12.2]
tad brahma paramaṃ nityam ajam akṣayam avyayam | [ViPur, 1, 2 13.1]
ekasvarūpaṃ ca sadā heyābhāvāc ca nirmalam | [ViPur, 1, 2 13.2]
tad eva sarvam evaitad vyaktāvyaktasvarūpavat | [ViPur, 1, 2 14.1]
tathā puruṣarūpeṇa kālarūpeṇa ca sthitam | [ViPur, 1, 2 14.2]
parasya brahmaṇo rūpaṃ puruṣaḥ prathamaṃ dvija | [ViPur, 1, 2 15.1]
vyaktāvyakte tathaivānye rūpe kālas tathāparam | [ViPur, 1, 2 15.2]
pradhānapuruṣavyaktakālānāṃ paramaṃ hi yat | [ViPur, 1, 2 16.1]
paśyanti sūrayaḥ śuddhaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam | [ViPur, 1, 2 16.2]
pradhānapuruṣavyaktakālās tu pravibhāgaśaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 17.1]
rūpāṇi sthitisargāntavyaktisadbhāvahetavaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 17.2]
vyaktaṃ viṣṇus tathāvyaktaṃ puruṣaḥ kāla eva ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 18.1]
krīḍato bālakasyeva ceṣṭāṃ tasya niśāmaya | [ViPur, 1, 2 18.2]
avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yat tat pradhānam ṛṣisattamaiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 19.1]
procyate prakṛtiḥ sūkṣmā nityā sadasadātmikā | [ViPur, 1, 2 19.2]
akṣayaṃ nānyadādhāram ameyam ajaraṃ dhruvam | [ViPur, 1, 2 20.1]
śabdasparśavihīnaṃ tad rūpādibhir asaṃhatam | [ViPur, 1, 2 20.2]
triguṇaṃ tajjagadyonir anādiprabhavāvyayam | [ViPur, 1, 2 21.1]
tenāgre sarvam evāsīd vyāptaṃ vai pralayād anu | [ViPur, 1, 2 21.2]
vedavādavido vidvan niyatā brahmavādinaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 22.1]
paṭhanti caitam evārthaṃ pradhānapratipādakam | [ViPur, 1, 2 22.2]
nāho na rātrir na nabho na bhūmir nāsīt tamo jyotir abhūn na cānyat | [ViPur, 1, 2 23.1]
śrotrādibuddhyānupalabhyam ekaṃ prādhānikaṃ brahma pumāṃs tadāsīt | [ViPur, 1, 2 23.2]
viṣṇoḥ svarūpāt parato hi te 'nye rūpe pradhānaṃ puruṣaś ca vipra | [ViPur, 1, 2 24.1]
tasyaiva te 'nyena dhṛte viyukte rūpāntaraṃ tad dvija kālasaṃjñam | [ViPur, 1, 2 24.2]
prakṛtau ca sthitaṃ vyaktam atītapralaye tu yat | [ViPur, 1, 2 25.1]
tasmāt prākṛtasaṃjño 'yam ucyate pratisaṃcaraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 25.2]
anādir bhagavān kālo nānto 'sya dvija vidyate | [ViPur, 1, 2 26.1]
avyucchinnās tatas tvete sargasthityantasaṃyamāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 26.2]
guṇasāmye tatas tasmin pṛthak puṃsi vyavasthite | [ViPur, 1, 2 27.1]
kālasvarūpaṃ tad viṣṇor maitreya parivartate | [ViPur, 1, 2 27.2]
tatas tat paramaṃ brahma paramātmā jaganmayaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 28.1]
sarvagaḥ sarvabhūteśaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 28.2]
pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ cāpi praviśyātmecchayā hariḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 29.1]
kṣobhayāmāsa samprāpte sargakāle vyayāvyayau | [ViPur, 1, 2 29.2]
yathā saṃnidhimātreṇa gandhaḥ kṣobhāya jāyate | [ViPur, 1, 2 30.1]
manaso nopakartṛtvāt tathāsau parameśvaraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 30.2]
sa eva kṣobhako brahman kṣobhyaś ca puruṣottamaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 31.1]
sa saṃkocavikāsābhyāṃ pradhānatve 'pi ca sthitaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 31.2]
vikāsāṇusvarūpaiś ca brahmarūpādibhis tathā | [ViPur, 1, 2 32.1]
vyaktasvarūpaś ca tathā viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 32.2]
guṇasāmyāt tatas tasmāt kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitān mune | [ViPur, 1, 2 33.1]
guṇavyañjanasaṃbhūtiḥ sargakāle dvijottama | [ViPur, 1, 2 33.2]
pradhānatattvam udbhūtaṃ mahāntaṃ tat samāvṛṇot | [ViPur, 1, 2 34.1]
sāttviko rājasaś caiva tāmasaś ca tridhā mahān | [ViPur, 1, 2 34.2]
pradhānatattvena samaṃ tvacā bījam ivāvṛtam | [ViPur, 1, 2 34.3]
vaikārikas taijasaś ca bhūtādiś caiva tāmasaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 35.1]
trividho 'yam ahaṃkāro mahattattvād ajāyata | [ViPur, 1, 2 35.2]
bhūtendriyāṇāṃ hetuḥ sa triguṇatvān mahāmune | [ViPur, 1, 2 36.1]
yathā pradhānena mahān mahatā sa tathāvṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 36.2]
bhūtādis tu vikurvāṇaḥ śabdatanmātrakaṃ tataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 37.1]
sasarja śabdatanmātrād ākāśaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam | [ViPur, 1, 2 37.2]
śabdamātraṃ tathākāśaṃ bhūtādiḥ sa samāvṛṇot | [ViPur, 1, 2 38.1]
ākāśas tu vikurvāṇaḥ sparśamātraṃ sasarja ha | [ViPur, 1, 2 38.2]
balavān abhavad vāyus tasya sparśo guṇo mataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 39.1]
ākāśaṃ śabdamātraṃ tu sparśamātraṃ samāvṛṇot | [ViPur, 1, 2 39.2]
tato vāyur vikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha | [ViPur, 1, 2 40.1]
jyotir utpadyate vāyos tad rūpaguṇam ucyate | [ViPur, 1, 2 40.2]
sparśamātras tato vāyū rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot | [ViPur, 1, 2 41.1]
jyotiś cāpi vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātraṃ sasarja ha | [ViPur, 1, 2 41.2]
sambhavanti tato 'mbhāṃsi rasādhārāṇi tāni ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 42.1]
rasamātrāṇi cāmbhāṃsi rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot | [ViPur, 1, 2 42.2]
vikurvāṇāni cāmbhāṃsi gandhamātraṃ sasarjire | [ViPur, 1, 2 43.1]
saṃghāto jāyate tasmāt tasya gandho guṇo mataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 43.2]
tasmiṃs tasmiṃs tu tanmātrā tena tanmātratā smṛtā | [ViPur, 1, 2 44.1]
tanmātrāṇy aviśeṣāṇi aviśeṣās tato hi te | [ViPur, 1, 2 44.2]
na śāntā nāpi ghorās te na mūḍhāś cāviśeṣiṇaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 45.1]
bhūtatanmātrasargo 'yam ahaṃkārāt tu tāmasāt | [ViPur, 1, 2 45.2]
taijasānīndriyāṇy āhur devā vaikārikā daśa | [ViPur, 1, 2 46.1]
ekādaśaṃ manaś cātra devā vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 46.2]
tvak cakṣur nāsikā jihvā śrotram atra ca pañcamam | [ViPur, 1, 2 47.1]
śabdādīnām avāptyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni vai dvija | [ViPur, 1, 2 47.2]
pāyūpasthau karau pādau vāk ca maitreya pañcamī | [ViPur, 1, 2 48.1]
visargaśilpagatyukti karma teṣāṃ ca kathyate | [ViPur, 1, 2 48.2]
ākāśavāyutejāṃsi salilaṃ pṛthivī tathā | [ViPur, 1, 2 49.1]
śabdādibhir guṇair brahman saṃyuktāny uttarottaraiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 49.2]
śāntā ghorāś ca mūḍhāś ca viśeṣās tena te smṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 50.1]
nānāvīryāḥ pṛthagbhūtās tatas te saṃhatiṃ vinā | [ViPur, 1, 2 51.1]
nāśaknuvan prajāḥ sraṣṭum asamāgamya kṛtsnaśaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 51.2]
sametyānyonyasaṃyogaṃ parasparasamāśrayāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 52.1]
ekasaṃghātalakṣyāś ca samprāpyaikyam aśeṣataḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 52.2]
puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 53.1]
mahadādyā viśeṣāntā hy aṇḍam utpādayanti te | [ViPur, 1, 2 53.2]
tat krameṇa vivṛddhaṃ tu jalabudbudavat samam | [ViPur, 1, 2 54.1]
bhūtebhyo 'ṇḍaṃ mahābuddhe bṛhat tad udakeśayam | [ViPur, 1, 2 54.2]
prākṛtaṃ brahmarūpasya viṣṇoḥ sthānam anuttamam | [ViPur, 1, 2 54.3]
tatrāvyaktasvarūpo 'sau vyaktarūpī jagatpatiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 55.1]
viṣṇur brahmasvarūpeṇa svayam eva vyavasthitaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 55.2]
merur ulbam abhūt tasya jarāyuś ca mahīdharāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 56.1]
garbhodakaṃ samudrāś ca tasyāsan sumahātmanaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 56.2]
sādridvīpasamudrāś ca sajyotir lokasaṃgrahaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 57.1]
tasminn aṇḍe 'bhavad vipra sadevāsuramānuṣaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 57.2]
vārivahnyanilākāśais tato bhūtādinā bahiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 58.1]
vṛtaṃ daśaguṇair aṇḍaṃ bhūtādir mahatā tathā | [ViPur, 1, 2 58.2]
avyaktenāvṛto brahmaṃs taiḥ sarvaiḥ sahito mahān | [ViPur, 1, 2 59.1]
ebhir āvaraṇair aṇḍaṃ saptabhiḥ prākṛtair vṛtam | [ViPur, 1, 2 59.2]
nālikeraphalasyāntar bījaṃ bāhyadalair iva | [ViPur, 1, 2 59.3]
juṣan rajoguṇaṃ tatra svayaṃ viśveśvaro hariḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 60.1]
brahmā bhūtvāsya jagato visṛṣṭau sampravartate | [ViPur, 1, 2 60.2]
sṛṣṭaṃ ca pāty anuyugaṃ yāvat kalpavikalpanā | [ViPur, 1, 2 61.1]
sattvabhṛd bhagavān viṣṇur aprameyaparākramaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 61.2]
tamoudrekī ca kalpānte rudrarūpī janārdanaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 62.1]
maitreyākhilabhūtāni bhakṣayaty atibhīṣaṇaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 62.2]
saṃbhakṣayitvā bhūtāni jagaty ekārṇavīkṛte | [ViPur, 1, 2 63.1]
nāgaparyaṅkaśayane śete 'sau parameśvaraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 63.2]
prabuddhaś ca punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ karoti brahmarūpadhṛk | [ViPur, 1, 2 64.1]
sṛṣṭisthityantakaraṇād brahmaviṣṇuśivātmikām | [ViPur, 1, 2 65.1]
sa saṃjñāṃ yāti bhagavān eka eva janārdanaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 65.2]
sraṣṭā sṛjati cātmānaṃ viṣṇuḥ pālyaṃ ca pāti ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 66.1]
upasaṃharate cānte saṃhartā ca svayaṃ prabhuḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 66.2]
pṛthivy āpas tathā tejo vāyur ākāśam eva ca | [ViPur, 1, 2 67.1]
sarvendriyāntaḥkaraṇaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ hi yajjagat | [ViPur, 1, 2 67.2]
sa eva sarvabhūteśo viśvarūpo yato 'vyayaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 2 68.1]
sargādikaṃ tato 'syaiva bhūtastham upakārakam | [ViPur, 1, 2 68.2]

catvāri trīṇi dve caikaṃ kṛtādiṣu yathākramam | [ViPur, 1, 3 12.1]
divyābdānāṃ sahasrāṇi yugeṣv āhuḥ purāvidaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 3 12.2]

saṃdhyāsaṃdhyāṃśayor antar yaḥ kālo munisattama | [ViPur, 1, 3 14.1]

bhavanti parimāṇaṃ ca teṣāṃ kālakṛtaṃ śṛṇu | [ViPur, 1, 3 16.2]
saptarṣayaḥ surāḥ śakro manus tatsūnavo nṛpāḥ | [ViPur, 1, 3 17.1]
ekakāle hi sṛjyante saṃhriyante ca pūrvavat | [ViPur, 1, 3 17.2]

manvantaraṃ manoḥ kālaḥ surādīnāṃ ca sattama | [ViPur, 1, 3 18.2]

saptaṣaṣṭis tathānyāni niyutāni mahāmune | [ViPur, 1, 3 20.2]
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālo 'yam adhikaṃ vinā | [ViPur, 1, 3 21.1]
manvantarasya saṃkhyeyaṃ mānuṣair vatsarair dvija | [ViPur, 1, 3 21.2]
caturdaśaguṇo hy eṣa kālo brāhmam ahaḥ smṛtam | [ViPur, 1, 3 22.1]
brāhmo naimittiko nāma tasyānte pratisaṃcaraḥ | [ViPur, 1, 3 22.2]
tadā hi dahyate sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ bhūrbhuvādikam | [ViPur, 1, 3 23.1]

ekārṇave tu trailokye brahmā nārāyaṇātmakaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 3 24.1]

janasthair yogibhir devaś cintyamāno 'bjasaṃbhavaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 3 25.1]

{ViPur, 1, 9}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 1, 9 1.1]
idaṃ ca śṛṇu maitreya yat pṛṣṭo 'ham iha tvayā | [ViPur, 1, 9 1.2]
śrīsambaddhaṃ mayāpy etacchrutam āsīn marīcitaḥ | [ViPur, 1, 9 1.3]

prakṣipya tasmāt salilān niścakrāma mahāmatiḥ | [ViPur, 1, 20 6.2]
dṛṣṭvā ca sa jagad bhūyo gaganādyupalakṣaṇam | [ViPur, 1, 20 7.1]
prahlādo 'smīti sasmāra punar ātmānam ātmanā | [ViPur, 1, 20 7.2]

{ViPur, 1, 22}

naro gayasya tanayas tatputro 'bhūd virāṭ tataḥ | [ViPur, 2, 1 37.2]

tair idaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ navabhedam alaṃkṛtam | [ViPur, 2, 1 40.2]

parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 2, 2 4.1]

sahasradvitayocchrāyāstāvadvistāriṇaśca te | [ViPur, 2, 2 12.2]
bhārataṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ tataḥ kiṃpuruṣaṃ smṛtam | [ViPur, 2, 2 13.1]
harivarṣaṃ tathaivānyanmerordakṣiṇato dvija | [ViPur, 2, 2 13.2]

{ViPur, 2, 3}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 2, 3 1.1]

yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu dvīpo 'yaṃ dakṣiṇottarāt | [ViPur, 2, 3 8.1]
pūrve kirātā yasyānte paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 8.2]

āsāṃ nadyupanadyaśca santyanyāśca sahasraśaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 14.2]
tāsvime kurupāñcālā madhyadeśādayo janāḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 15.1]
pūrvadeśādikāścaiva kāmarūpanivāsinaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 15.2]

tathāparāntāḥ saurāṣṭrāḥ śūrābhīrāstathārbudāḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 16.2]
kārūṣā mālavāścaiva pāriyātranivāsinaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 17.1]
sauvīrāḥ saindhavā hūṇāḥ sālvāḥ śākalavāsinaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 3 17.2]

{ViPur, 2, 4}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 2, 4 1.1]
kṣārodena yathā dvīpo jambūsaṃjño 'bhiveṣṭitaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 4 1.2]
saṃveṣṭya kṣāram udadhiṃ plakṣadvīpastathā sthitaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 4 1.3]
jambūdvīpasya vistāraḥ śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 4 2.1]
sa evaṃ dviguṇo brahman plakṣadvīpa udāhṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 2, 4 2.2]
sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpeśvarasya vai | [ViPur, 2, 4 3.1]
jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayo nāma śiśirastadanantaraḥ | [ViPur, 2, 4 3.2]
sukhodayastathānandaḥ śivaḥ kṣemaka eva ca | [ViPur, 2, 4 4.1]
dhruvaśca saptamasteṣāṃ plakṣadvīpeśvarā hi te | [ViPur, 2, 4 4.2]
pūrvaṃ śāntabhayaṃ varṣaṃ śiśiraṃ sukhadaṃ tathā | [ViPur, 2, 4 5.1]
ānandaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva kṣemakaṃ dhruvameva ca | [ViPur, 2, 4 5.2]
maryādākārakāsteṣāṃ tathānye varṣaparvatāḥ | [ViPur, 2, 4 6.1]
saptaiva teṣāṃ nāmāni śṛṇuṣva munisattama | [ViPur, 2, 4 6.2]
gomedaścaiva candraśca nārado dundubhistathā | [ViPur, 2, 4 7.1]

prarohahetusāmagrīmāsādya munisattama | [ViPur, 2, 7 38.2]

{ViPur, 2, 9}

{ViPur, 3, 4}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 4 1.1]
ādyo vedaścatuṣpādaḥ śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 1.2]
tato daśaguṇaḥ kṛtsno yajño 'yaṃ sarvakāmadhuk | [ViPur, 3, 4 1.3]
tato 'tra matsuto vyāso 'ṣṭāviṃśatitame 'ntare | [ViPur, 3, 4 2.1]
vedamekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturdhā vyabhajatprabhuḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 2.2]
yathā tu tena vai vyastā vedavyāsena dhīmatā | [ViPur, 3, 4 3.1]
vedāstathā samastaistairvyastā vyastaistathā mayā | [ViPur, 3, 4 3.2]
tadanenaiva vedānāṃ śākhābhedāndvijottama | [ViPur, 3, 4 4.1]
caturyugeṣu racitānsamasteṣvavadhāraya | [ViPur, 3, 4 4.2]
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ vyāsaṃ viddhi nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum | [ViPur, 3, 4 5.1]
ko 'nyo hi bhuvi maitreya mahābhāratakṛdbhavet | [ViPur, 3, 4 5.2]
tena vyastā yathā vedā matputreṇa mahātmanā | [ViPur, 3, 4 6.1]
dvāpare hyatra maitreya tanme śṛṇu yathārthataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 6.2]
brahmaṇā codito vyāso vedānvyastuṃ pracakrame | [ViPur, 3, 4 7.1]
atha śiṣyānsa jagrāha caturo vedapāragān | [ViPur, 3, 4 7.2]
ṛgvedaśrāvakaṃ pailaṃ jagrāha sa mahāmuniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 8.1]
vaiśampāyananāmānaṃ yajurvedasya cāgrahīt | [ViPur, 3, 4 8.2]
jaiminiṃ sāmavedasya tathaivātharvavedavit | [ViPur, 3, 4 9.1]
sumantustasya śiṣyo 'bhūdvedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 9.2]
romaharṣaṇanāmānaṃ mahābuddhiṃ mahāmuniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 10.1]
sūtaṃ jagrāha śiṣyaṃ sa itihāsapurāṇayoḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 10.2]
eka āsīdyajurvedas taṃ caturdhā vyakalpayat | [ViPur, 3, 4 11.1]
cāturhotram abhūdyasmiṃs tena yajñamathākarot | [ViPur, 3, 4 11.2]
ādhvaryavaṃ yajurbhistu ṛgbhirhotraṃ tathā muniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 12.1]
audgātraṃ sāmabhiścakre brahmatvaṃ cāpyatharvabhiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 12.2]
tataḥ sa ṛca uddhṛtya ṛgvedaṃ kṛtavānmuniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 13.1]
yajūṃṣi ca yajurvedaṃ sāmavedaṃ ca sāmabhiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 13.2]
rājñastvatharvavedena sarvakarmāṇi sa prabhuḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 14.1]
kārayāmāsa maitreya brahmatvaṃ ca yathāsthitiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 14.2]
so 'yameko mahāvedatarustena pṛthakkṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 15.1]
caturdhā tu tato jātaṃ vedapādapakānanam | [ViPur, 3, 4 15.2]
bibheda prathamaṃ vipra paila ṛgvedapādapam | [ViPur, 3, 4 16.1]
indrapramataye prādād bāṣkalāya ca saṃhite | [ViPur, 3, 4 16.2]
caturdhā sa bibhedātha bāṣkalo nijasaṃhitām | [ViPur, 3, 4 17.1]
baudhyādibhyo dadau tāstu śiṣyebhyaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 17.2]
baudhyāgnimāṭharau tadvadyājñavalkyaparāśarau | [ViPur, 3, 4 18.1]
pratiśākhāstu śākhāyāstasyāste jagṛhurmune | [ViPur, 3, 4 18.2]
indrapramatirekāṃ tu saṃhitāṃ svasutaṃ tataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 19.1]
māṇḍukeyaṃ mahātmānaṃ maitreyādhyāpayattadā | [ViPur, 3, 4 19.2]
tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyebhyaḥ putraśiṣyānkramādyayau | [ViPur, 3, 4 20.1]
vedamitrastu śākalyaḥ saṃhitāṃ tāmadhītavān | [ViPur, 3, 4 21.1]
cakāra saṃhitāḥ pañca śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau ca tāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 21.2]
tasya śiṣyāstu ye pañca teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu | [ViPur, 3, 4 22.1]
mudgalo gālavaścaiva vātsyaḥ śālīya eva ca | [ViPur, 3, 4 22.2]
śiśiraḥ pañcamaścāsīt maitreya sumahāmuniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 22.3]
saṃhitātritayaṃ cakre śākapūṇirathetaraḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 23.1]
niruktamakarottadvaccaturthaṃ munisattama | [ViPur, 3, 4 23.2]
krauñco vaitālakistadvadbalākaśca mahāmuniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 24.1]
niruktaśca caturtho 'bhūdvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 24.2]
ityetāḥ pratiśākhābhyo 'pyanuśākhā dvijottama | [ViPur, 3, 4 25.1]
bāṣkalaścāparāstisraḥ saṃhitāḥ kṛtavāndvija | [ViPur, 3, 4 25.2]
śiṣyaḥ kālāyanirgārgyastṛtīyaśca tathā javaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 25.3]
ityete bahvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravartitāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 4 26.1]
{ViPur, 3, 5}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 5 1.1]
yajurvedataroḥ śākhāḥ saptaviṃśanmahāmatiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 1.2]
vaiśampāyananāmāsau vyāsaśiṣyaścakāra vai | [ViPur, 3, 5 1.3]
śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāśca jagṛhuste 'pyanukramāt | [ViPur, 3, 5 2.1]
yājñavalkyastu tasyābhūdbrahmarātasuto dvija | [ViPur, 3, 5 3.1]
śiṣyaḥ paramadharmajño guruvṛttiparaḥ sadā | [ViPur, 3, 5 3.2]
ṛṣiryo 'dya mahāmerau samājenāgamiṣyati | [ViPur, 3, 5 4.1]
tasya vai saptarātrāt tu brahmahatyā bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 3, 5 4.2]
pūrvam evaṃ munigaṇaiḥ samayo 'bhūtkṛto dvija | [ViPur, 3, 5 5.1]
vaiśampāyana ekastu taṃ vyatikrāntavāṃstadā | [ViPur, 3, 5 5.2]
svasrīyaṃ bālakaṃ so 'tha padā spṛṣṭamaghātayat | [ViPur, 3, 5 6.1]
śiṣyānāha ca bhoḥ śiṣyā brahmahatyāpahaṃ vratam | [ViPur, 3, 5 7.1]
caradhvaṃ matkṛte sarve na vicāryamidaṃ tathā | [ViPur, 3, 5 7.2]
athāha yājñavalkyastaṃ kim ebhirbhagavandvijaiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 8.1]
kleśitairalpatejobhiścariṣye 'hamidaṃ vratam | [ViPur, 3, 5 8.2]
tataḥ kruddho guruḥ prāha yājñavalkyaṃ mahāmatiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 9.1]
mucyatāṃ yat tvayādhītaṃ matto viprāvamānaka | [ViPur, 3, 5 9.2]
nistejaso vadasyetānyastvaṃ brāhmaṇapuṃgavān | [ViPur, 3, 5 10.1]
tena śiṣyeṇa nārtho 'sti mamājñābhaṅgakāriṇā | [ViPur, 3, 5 10.2]
yājñavalkyastataḥ prāha bhaktyaitatte mayoditam | [ViPur, 3, 5 11.1]
mamāpyalaṃ tvayādhītaṃ yanmayā tadidaṃ dvija | [ViPur, 3, 5 11.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 5 12.1]
ityuktvā rudhirāktāni sarūpāṇi yajūṃṣi saḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 12.2]
chardayitvā dadau tasmai yayau ca svecchayā muniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 12.3]
yajūṃṣyatha visṛṣṭāni yājñavalkyena vai dvija | [ViPur, 3, 5 13.1]
jagṛhustittirībhūtvā taittirīyāstu te tataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 13.2]
brahmahatyāvrataṃ cīrṇaṃ guruṇā coditaistu yaiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 14.1]
carakādhvaryavaste tu caraṇānmunisattama | [ViPur, 3, 5 14.2]
yājñavalkyo 'pi maitreya prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 15.1]
tuṣṭāva praṇataḥ sūryaṃ yajūṃṣyabhilaṣaṃstataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 15.2]
yājñavalkya uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 5 16.1]
namaḥ savitre dvārāya mukteramitatejase | [ViPur, 3, 5 16.2]
ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūtāya trayīdhāmavate namaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 16.3]
namo 'gnīṣomabhūtāya jagataḥ kāraṇātmane | [ViPur, 3, 5 17.1]
bhāskarāya paraṃ tejaḥ sauṣumṇamuru bibhrate | [ViPur, 3, 5 17.2]
kalākāṣṭhānimeṣādikālajñānātmane namaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 18.1]
dhyeyāya viṣṇurūpāya paramākṣararūpiṇe | [ViPur, 3, 5 18.2]
bibharti yaḥ suragaṇān āpyāyenduṃ svaraśmibhiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 19.1]
svadhāmṛtena ca pitṝṃstasmai tṛptyātmane namaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 19.2]
himāmbugharmavṛṣṭīnāṃ kartā bhartā ca yaḥ prabhuḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 20.1]
tasmai trikālabhūtāya namaḥ sūryāya vedhase | [ViPur, 3, 5 20.2]
apahanti tamo yaśca jagato 'sya jagatpatiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 21.1]
sattvadhāmadharo devo namastasmai vivasvate | [ViPur, 3, 5 21.2]
satkarmayogyo na jano naivāpaḥ śaucakāraṇam | [ViPur, 3, 5 22.1]
yasminnanudite tasmai namo devāya bhāsvate | [ViPur, 3, 5 22.2]
spṛṣṭo yadaṃśubhirlokaḥ kriyāyogyo 'bhijāyate | [ViPur, 3, 5 23.1]
pavitratākāraṇāya tasmai śuddhātmane namaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 23.2]
namaḥ savitre sūryāya bhāskarāya vivasvate | [ViPur, 3, 5 24.1]
ādityāyādibhūtāya devādīnāṃ namo namaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 24.2]
hiraṇmayaṃ rathaṃ yasya ketavo 'mṛtadhāriṇaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 25.1]
vahanti bhuvanālokacakṣuṣas taṃ namāmyaham | [ViPur, 3, 5 25.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 5 26.1]
ityevamādibhistena stūyamānaḥ stavai raviḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 26.2]
vājirūpadharaḥ prāha vrīyatāmiti vāñchitam | [ViPur, 3, 5 26.3]
yājñavalkyastadā prāha praṇipatya divākaram | [ViPur, 3, 5 27.1]
yajūṃṣi tāni me dehi yāni santi na me gurau | [ViPur, 3, 5 27.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 5 28.1]
evamukto dadau tasmai yajūṃṣi bhagavānraviḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 28.2]
ayātayāmasaṃjñāni yāni vetti na tadguruḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 28.3]
yajūṃṣi yairadhītāni tāni viprairdvijottama | [ViPur, 3, 5 29.1]
vājinaste samākhyātāḥ sūryo 'śvaḥ so 'bhavadyataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 29.2]
śākhābhedāstu teṣāṃ vai daśa pañca ca vājinām | [ViPur, 3, 5 30.1]
kaṇvādyāḥ sumahābhāgā yājñavalkyapravartitāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 5 30.2]
{ViPur, 3, 6}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 6 1.1]
sāmavedataroḥ śākhā vyāsaśiṣyaḥ sa jaiminiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 1.2]
krameṇa yena maitreya bibheda śṛṇu tanmama | [ViPur, 3, 6 1.3]
sumantustasya putro 'bhūtsukarmāsyāpyabhūtsutaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 2.1]
adhītavantāvekaikāṃ saṃhitāṃ tau mahāmunī | [ViPur, 3, 6 2.2]
sāhasraṃ saṃhitābhedaṃ sukarmā tatsutastataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 3.1]
cakāra taṃ ca tacchiṣyau jagṛhāte mahāvratau | [ViPur, 3, 6 3.2]
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kausalyaḥ pauṣpiñjiśca dvijottama | [ViPur, 3, 6 4.1]
udīcyāḥ sāmagāḥ śiṣyāstasya pañcadaśa smṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 4.2]
hiraṇyanābhāttāvatyaḥ saṃhitā yairdvijottamaiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 5.1]
gṛhītāste 'pi cocyante paṇḍitaiḥ prācyasāmagāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 5.2]
lokākṣiḥ kuthumiścaiva kuṣīdī lāṅgalistathā | [ViPur, 3, 6 6.1]
pauṣpiñjiśiṣyāstadbhedaiḥ saṃhitā bahulīkṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 6.2]
hiraṇyanābhaśiṣyaśca caturviṃśatisaṃhitāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 7.1]
provāca kṛtināmāsau śiṣyebhyaḥ sumahāmatiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 7.2]
taiścāpi sāmavedo 'sau śākhābhirbahulīkṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 8.1]
atharvaṇām atho vakṣye saṃhitānāṃ samuccayam | [ViPur, 3, 6 8.2]
atharvavedaṃ sa muniḥ sumanturamitadyutiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 8.3]
śiṣyamadhyāpayāmāsa kabandhaṃ so 'pi taṃ dvidhā | [ViPur, 3, 6 9.1]
kṛtvā tu devadarśāya tathā pathyāya dattavān | [ViPur, 3, 6 9.2]
devadarśasya śiṣyāstu maudgo brahmabalistathā | [ViPur, 3, 6 10.1]
śaulkāyaniḥ pippalādastathānyo munisattama | [ViPur, 3, 6 10.2]
pathyasyāpi trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ kṛtā yairdvija saṃhitāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 11.1]
jājaliḥ kumudādiśca tṛtīyaḥ śaunako dvija | [ViPur, 3, 6 11.2]
śaunakastu dvidhā kṛtvā dadāvekāṃ tu babhrave | [ViPur, 3, 6 12.1]
dvitīyāṃ saṃhitāṃ prādātsaindhavāya ca saṃjñine | [ViPur, 3, 6 12.2]
saindhavānmuñjakeśaśca 'bhinadvedaṃ dvidhā punaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 13.1]
nakṣatrakalpo vedānāṃ saṃhitānāṃ tathaiva ca | [ViPur, 3, 6 13.2]
caturthaḥ syādāṅgirasaḥ śāntikalpaśca pañcamaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 14.1]
śreṣṭhāstvatharvaṇām ete saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 14.2]
ākhyānaiścāpyupākhyānairgāthābhiḥ kalpaśuddhibhiḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 15.1]
purāṇasaṃhitāṃ cakre purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 15.2]
prakhyāto vyāsaśiṣyo 'bhūtsūto vai romaharṣaṇaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 16.1]
purāṇasaṃhitāṃ tasmai dadau vyāso mahāmuniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 16.2]
sumatiścāgnivarcāśca mitrāyuḥ śāṃsapāyanaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 17.1]
akṛtavraṇo 'tha sāvarṇiḥ ṣaṭśiṣyāstasya cābhavan | [ViPur, 3, 6 17.2]
kāśyapaḥ saṃhitākartā sāvarṇiḥ śāṃśapāyanaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 18.1]
romaharṣaṇikā cānyā tisṝṇāṃ mūlasaṃhitā | [ViPur, 3, 6 18.2]
catuṣṭayenāpyetena saṃhitānām idaṃ mune | [ViPur, 3, 6 19.1]
ādyaṃ sarvapurāṇānāṃ purāṇaṃ brāhmamucyate | [ViPur, 3, 6 20.1]
aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni purāṇajñāḥ pracakṣate | [ViPur, 3, 6 20.2]
brāhmaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā | [ViPur, 3, 6 21.1]
tathānyaṃ nāradīyaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyaṃ ca saptamam | [ViPur, 3, 6 21.2]
āgneyamaṣṭamaṃ caiva bhaviṣyaṃ navamaṃ tathā | [ViPur, 3, 6 22.1]
daśamaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṅgamekādaśaṃ smṛtam | [ViPur, 3, 6 22.2]
vārāhaṃ dvādaśaṃ caiva skāndaṃ cātra trayodaśam | [ViPur, 3, 6 23.1]
caturdaśaṃ vāmanaṃ ca kaurmaṃ pañcadaśaṃ smṛtam | [ViPur, 3, 6 23.2]
mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍaṃ caiva brahmāṇḍaṃ ca tataḥ param | [ViPur, 3, 6 23.3]
sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca | [ViPur, 3, 6 24.1]
sarveṣveteṣu kathyante vaṃśānucaritaṃ ca yat | [ViPur, 3, 6 24.2]
yadetattava maitreya purāṇaṃ kathyate mayā | [ViPur, 3, 6 25.1]
etadvaiṣṇavasaṃjñaṃ vai pādmasya samanantaram | [ViPur, 3, 6 25.2]
sarge ca pratisarge ca vaṃśamanvantarādiṣu | [ViPur, 3, 6 26.1]
kathyate bhagavānviṣṇuraśeṣeṣveva sattama | [ViPur, 3, 6 26.2]
aṅgāni caturo vedā mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 27.1]
purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vidyā hyetāścaturdaśa | [ViPur, 3, 6 27.2]
āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāndharvaścaiva te trayaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 28.1]
arthaśāstraṃ caturthaṃ tu vidyā hyaṣṭādaśaiva tāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 28.2]
jñeyā brahmarṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ tebhyo devarṣayaḥ punaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 29.1]
rājarṣayaḥ punastebhya ṛṣiprakṛtayastrayaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 29.2]
iti śākhāḥ samākhyātāḥ śākhābhedāstathaiva ca | [ViPur, 3, 6 30.1]
kartāraścaiva śākhānāṃ bhedahetustathoditaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 30.2]
sarvamanvantareṣvevaṃ śākhābhedāḥ samāḥ smṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 6 31.1]
prājāpatyā śrutirnityā tadvikalpāstvime dvija | [ViPur, 3, 6 32.1]
etattavoditaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭo 'hamiha tvayā | [ViPur, 3, 6 33.1]
maitreya vedasambaddhaṃ kimanyatkathayāmi te | [ViPur, 3, 6 33.2]
{ViPur, 3, 7}
maitreya uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 7 1.1]
yathāvatkathitaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭo 'si mayā guro | [ViPur, 3, 7 1.2]
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ tvekaṃ tad bhavānprabravītu me | [ViPur, 3, 7 1.3]
saptadvīpāni pātālavīthyaśca sumahāmune | [ViPur, 3, 7 2.1]
sapta lokāśca ye 'ntaḥsthā brahmāṇḍasyāsya sarvataḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 2.2]
sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmaistathāsūkṣmaiḥ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraistathā | [ViPur, 3, 7 3.1]
sthūlaiḥ sthūlataraiścaitatsarvaṃ prāṇibhirāvṛtam | [ViPur, 3, 7 3.2]
aṅgulasyāṣṭabhāgo 'pi na so 'sti munisattama | [ViPur, 3, 7 4.1]
na santi prāṇino yatra karmabandhanibandhanāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 4.2]
sarve caite vaśaṃ yānti yamasya bhagavan kila | [ViPur, 3, 7 5.1]
āyuṣo 'nte tato yānti yātanā tatpracoditāḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 5.2]
yātanābhyaḥ paribhraṣṭā devādyāsvatha yoniṣu | [ViPur, 3, 7 6.1]
jantavaḥ parivartante śāstrāṇāmeṣa nirṇayaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 6.2]
so 'ham icchāmi tacchrotuṃ yamasya vaśavartinaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 7.1]
na bhavanti narā yena tatkarma kathayāmalam | [ViPur, 3, 7 7.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 7 8.1]
ayameva mune praśno nakulena mahātmanā | [ViPur, 3, 7 8.2]
pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ prāha bhīṣmo yattacchṛṇuṣva me | [ViPur, 3, 7 8.3]
bhīṣma uvāca | [ViPur, 3, 7 9.1]
purā mamāgato vatsa sakhā kāliṅgako dvijaḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 9.2]
māmuvāca sa pṛṣṭo vai mayā jātismaro muniḥ | [ViPur, 3, 7 9.3]
tenākhyātam idaṃ cedamitthaṃ caitadbhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 3, 7 10.1]
tathā ca tadabhūd vatsa yathoktaṃ tena dhīmatā | [ViPur, 3, 7 10.2]

tad asya vaṃśasyānupūrvīm aśeṣapāpaprakṣālanāya maitreya tāṃ śṛṇu | [ViPur, 4, 1 5.1]
tad yathā sakalajagatāmanādir ādibhūtaṛgyajuḥsāmādimayo bhagavadviṣṇumayasya brahmaṇo mūrtaṃ rūpaṃ hiraṇyagarbho brahmāṇḍato bhagavānprāgbabhūva | [ViPur, 4, 1 6.1]
brahmaṇaśca dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhajanmā dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ dakṣasyāditiraditervivasvān vivasvato manuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 7.1]
manor ikṣvākunṛgadhṛṣṭaśaryātinariṣyantaprāṃśunābhāganediṣṭakarūṣapṛṣadhrākhyā daśa putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 8.1]
iṣṭiṃ ca mitrāvaruṇayormanuḥ putrakāmaścakāra | [ViPur, 4, 1 9.1]
tatrāpahute hoturapacārādilā nāma kanyā babhūva | [ViPur, 4, 1 10.1]
saiva ca mitrāvaruṇayoḥ prasādātsudyumno nāma manoḥ putro maitreyāsīt | [ViPur, 4, 1 11.1]
punaś ceśvarakopātstrī satī somasūnorbudhasyāśramasamīpe babhrāma | [ViPur, 4, 1 12.1]
sānurāgaśca tasyāṃ budhaḥ purūravasam ātmajamutpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 1 13.1]
jāte ca tasmin amitatejobhiḥ paramarṣibhirṛṅmayo yajurmayaḥ sāmamayo 'tharvamayaḥ sarvamayo manomayo jñānamayo nakiṃcinmayo bhagavān yajñapuruṣasvarūpī sudyumnasya puṃstvamabhilaṣadbhiryathāvadiṣṭastatprasādāccāsāvilā punarapi sudyumno 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 14.1]
tasyāpyutkalagayavinatasaṃjñāstrayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 15.1]
sudyumnastu strīpūrvakatvādrājyabhāgaṃ na lebhe | [ViPur, 4, 1 16.1]
tatpitrā tu vasiṣṭhavacanātpratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma nagaraṃ sudyumnāya dattaṃ taccāsau purūravase prādāt | [ViPur, 4, 1 17.1]
pṛṣadhrastu manoḥ putro gurugovadhācchūdratvamagamat | [ViPur, 4, 1 18.1]
karūṣātkārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā mahābalaparākramā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 19.1]
nābhāgo nediṣṭaputrastu vaiśyatāmagamattasmādbhalandanaḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 20.1]
bhalandanād vatsaprir udārakīrtiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 21.1]
vatsapreḥ prāṃśur abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 22.1]
prajāniś ca prāṃśor eko 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 23.1]
tataś ca khanitrastasmāccakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuṣāccātibalaparākramo viṃśo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 24.1]
tato viviṃśastasmācca khaninetrastataścātivibhūtiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 25.1]
ativibhūterbhūribalaparākramaḥ karaṃdhamaḥ putro 'bhavattasmād apyavikṣir avikṣer apyavikṣito 'pyatibalaḥ putro marutto 'bhavadyasyemāvadyāpi ślokau gīyete | [ViPur, 4, 1 26.1]
maruttasya yathā yajñastathā kasyābhavad bhuvi | [ViPur, 4, 1 27.1]
sarvaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ yasya yajñavastv atiśobhanam | [ViPur, 4, 1 27.2]
amādyad indraḥ somena dakṣiṇābhir dvijātayaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 28.1]
marutaḥ pariveṣṭāraḥ sadasyāś ca divaukasaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 28.2]
maruttaś cakravartī nariṣyantanāmānaṃ putram avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 1 29.1]
tasmācca damaḥ damasya putro rājyavardhano jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 1 30.1]
rājyavardhanāt susuvṛddheḥ kevalaḥ kevalāt sudhṛtir abhūttataśca naraḥ tasmāccandraḥ tasmācca kevalaḥ kevalād bandhumān bandhumato vegavān vegavato budhaḥ tataśca tṛṇabinduḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 31.1]
tasyāpy ekā kanyā ilavilā nāma | [ViPur, 4, 1 32.1]
taṃ cālambusā nāma varāpsarās tṛṇabinduṃ bheje | [ViPur, 4, 1 33.1]
tasyām apy asya viśālo jajñe yaḥ purīṃ vaiśālīṃ nāma nirmame | [ViPur, 4, 1 34.1]
hemacandro viśālasya putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 35.1]
tasmāc ca sucandrastattanayo dhūmrāśvastasyāpi sṛñjayo 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 1 36.1]
sṛñjayāt sahadevaḥ tataḥ kṛśāśvo nāma putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 37.1]
somadattaḥ kṛśāśvājjajñe yo daśāśvamedhān ājahāra | [ViPur, 4, 1 38.1]
tatputraś ca janamejayaḥ janamejayāt sumatiḥ ete vaiśālikā bhūbhṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 39.1]
śloko 'py atra gīyate | [ViPur, 4, 1 40.1]
tṛṇabindoḥ prasādena sarve vaiśālikā nṛpāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 40.2]
dīrghāyuṣo mahātmāno vīryavanto 'tidhārmikāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 40.3]
śaryāteḥ kanyā sukanyā nāmābhavat yām upayeme cyavanaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 41.1]
ānartaś ca nāma dhārmikaḥ śaryātiputro 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 1 42.1]
ānartasyāpi revato nāma putro jajñe yo 'sāvānartaviṣayaṃ bubhuje purīṃ ca kuśasthalīm adhyuvāsa | [ViPur, 4, 1 43.1]
revatasyāpi raivataḥ putraḥ kakudmī nāma dharmātmā bhrātṛśatasya jyeṣṭho 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 1 44.1]
tasya ca revatī nāma kanyā tām ādāya sa tām ādāya kasyeyam arhatīti bhagavantam abjayoniṃ praṣṭuṃ brahmalokaṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 1 45.1]
tāvacca brahmaṇo 'ntike hāhāhūhūsaṃjñābhyāṃ gandharvābhyām atitānaṃ nāma divyaṃ gāndharvam agīyata | [ViPur, 4, 1 46.1]
tāvacca trimārgaparivartair anekayugaparivṛttitiṣṭhann api raivataḥ śṛṇvan muhūrtam iva mene | [ViPur, 4, 1 47.1]
gītāvasāne ca bhagavantam abjayoniṃ praṇamya raivataḥ kanyāyogyaṃ varam apṛcchat | [ViPur, 4, 1 48.1]
taṃ cāha bhagavān kathaya yo 'bhimatas te vara iti | [ViPur, 4, 1 49.1]
punaś ca praṇamya bhagavate tasmai yathābhimatān ātmanaḥ sa varān kathayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 1 50.1]
ka eṣāṃ bhagavato 'bhimato yasmai kanyām imāṃ prayacchāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 1 50.2]
tataḥ kiṃcidavanataśirāḥ sasmitaṃ bhagavān abjayonir āha | [ViPur, 4, 1 51.1]
ya ete bhavato 'bhimatā naiteṣāṃ sāṃprataṃ apatyāpatyasaṃtatir apy avanītale 'sti | [ViPur, 4, 1 52.1]
bahūni hi tavātraiva gāndharvaṃ śṛṇvataś caturyugānyatītāni | [ViPur, 4, 1 53.1]
sāmprataṃ hi bhū'ṣṭāviṃśatitamasya manoś caturyugam atītaprāyam āsanno hi tatra kaliḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 54.1]
anyasmai kanyāratnam idaṃ bhavataikākinā deyam | [ViPur, 4, 1 55.1]
bhavato 'pi mitramantribhṛtyakalatrabandhubalakośādayaḥ samastāḥ kālenaitenātyantam atītāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 56.1]
tataḥ punar utpannasādhvaso rājā bhagavantaṃ praṇamya papraccha | [ViPur, 4, 1 57.1]
bhagavann evam avasthite mayeyaṃ kasmai deyeti | [ViPur, 4, 1 58.1]
tataḥ sa bhagavān kiṃcidavanamrakandharaṃ kṛtāñjalibhūtaṃ sarvalokagurur abjayonir āha | [ViPur, 4, 1 59.1]
brahmovāca | [ViPur, 4, 1 60.1]
na hy ādimadhyāntam ajasya yasya vidmo vayaṃ sarvamayasya dhātuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 60.2]
na ca svarūpaṃ na paraṃ svabhāvaṃ na caiva sāraṃ parameśvarasya | [ViPur, 4, 1 60.3]
kalāmuhūrtādimayaś ca kālo na yadvibhūteḥ pariṇāmahetuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 61.1]
ajanmanāśasya samastamūrter anāmarūpasya sanātanasya | [ViPur, 4, 1 61.2]
yasya prasādād aham acyutasya bhūtaḥ prajāsṛṣṭikaro 'ntakārī | [ViPur, 4, 1 62.1]
krodhācca rudraḥ sthitihetubhūto yasmācca madhye puruṣaḥ parasmāt | [ViPur, 4, 1 62.2]
madrūpam āsthāya sṛjaty ajo yaḥ sthitau ca yo 'sau puruṣasvarūpī | [ViPur, 4, 1 63.1]
rudrasvarūpeṇa ca yo 'tti viśvaṃ dhatte tathānantavapuḥ samastam | [ViPur, 4, 1 63.2]
śakrādirūpī paripāti viśvam arkendurūpaś ca tamo hinasti | [ViPur, 4, 1 64.1]
pākāya yo 'gnitvam upetya lokān bibharti pṛthvīvapur avyayātmā | [ViPur, 4, 1 64.2]
ceṣṭāṃ karoti śvasanasvarūpī lokasya tṛptiṃ ca jalānnarūpī | [ViPur, 4, 1 65.1]
dadāti viśvasthitisaṃsthitas tu sarvāvakāśaṃ ca nabhaḥsvarūpī | [ViPur, 4, 1 65.2]
yaḥ sṛjyate sargakṛd ātmanaiva yaḥ pālyate pālayitā ca devaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 66.1]
viśvātmanā saṃhriyate 'ntakārī pṛthaktrayasyāsya ca yo 'vyayātmā | [ViPur, 4, 1 66.2]
yasmiñjagad yo jagad etad ādyo yaś cāśrito 'smiñjagati svayaṃbhūḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 67.1]
sa sarvabhūtaprabhavo dharitryāṃ svāṃśena viṣṇur nṛpate 'vatīrṇaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 67.2]
kuśasthalī yā tava bhūpa ramyā purī purābhūd amarāvatīva | [ViPur, 4, 1 68.1]
sā dvārakā saṃprati tatra cāste sa keśavāṃśo baladevanāmā | [ViPur, 4, 1 68.2]
tasmai tvam enāṃ tanayāṃ narendra prayaccha māyāmanujāya jāyām | [ViPur, 4, 1 69.1]
ślāghyo varo 'sau tanayā taveyaṃ strīratnabhūtā sadṛśo hi yogaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 69.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 1 70.1]
itīrito 'sau kamalodbhavena bhuvaṃ samāsādya patiḥ prajānām | [ViPur, 4, 1 70.2]
dadarśa hrasvān puruṣān aśeṣān alpaujasaḥ svalpavivekavīryān | [ViPur, 4, 1 70.3]
kuśasthalīṃ tāṃ ca purīm upetya dṛṣṭvānyarūpāṃ pradadau svakanyām | [ViPur, 4, 1 71.1]
sīradhvajāya sphaṭikācalābhavakṣaḥsthalāyātuladhīr narendraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 71.2]
uccapramāṇām iti tām avekṣya svalāṅgalāgreṇa ca tālaketuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 1 72.1]
vināmayāmāsa tataśca sāpi babhūva sadyo vanitā yathānyā | [ViPur, 4, 1 72.2]
tāṃ revatīṃ raivatabhūpakanyāṃ sīrāyudho 'sau vidhinopayeme | [ViPur, 4, 1 73.1]
dattvā ca kanyāṃ sa nṛpo jagāma himālayaṃ vai tapase dhṛtātmā | [ViPur, 4, 1 73.2]
{ViPur, 4, 2}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 1.1]
yāvacca brahmalokāt kakudmī raivato nābhyeti tāvat puṇyajanasaṃjñā rākṣasās tām asya purīṃ kuśasthalīṃ jaghnuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 1.2]
taccāsya bhrātṛśataṃ puṇyajanatrāsād diśo bheje | [ViPur, 4, 2 2.1]
tadanvayāś ca kṣatriyāḥ sarvadikṣvabhavan | [ViPur, 4, 2 3.1]
dhṛṣṭasyāpi dhārṣṭakaṃ kṣatram abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 4.1]
nabhagasyātmajo nābhāgasaṃjño 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 5.1]
tasyāpy ambarīṣaḥ ambarīṣasyāpi virūpo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 5.2]
virūpāt pṛṣadaśvo jajñe tataś ca rathītaraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 6.1]
atrāyaṃ ślokaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 7.1]
ete kṣatraprasūtā vai punaś cāṅgirasāḥ smṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 7.2]
rathītarāṇāṃ pravarāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 7.3]
kṣuvataśca manor ikṣvākur ghrāṇataḥ putro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 2 8.1]
tasya putraśatapravarā vikukṣinimidaṇḍākhyās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 9.1]
śakunipramukhāḥ pañcāśat putrāḥ uttarāpatharakṣitāro babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 9.2]
catvāriṃśad aṣṭau ca dakṣiṇāpathabhūpālāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 9.3]
sa cekṣvākur aṣṭakāyām utpādya śrāddhārhaṃ māṃsam ānayeti vikukṣim ājñāpayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 10.1]
sa tatheti gṛhītājño vanam abhyetyānekān mṛgān hatvātiśrānto 'tikṣutparīto vikukṣir ekaṃ śaśam abhakṣayat | [ViPur, 4, 2 10.2]
śeṣaṃ ca māṃsam ānīya pitre nivedayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 10.3]
ikṣvākukulācāryas vasiṣṭhaś coditaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 2 11.1]
alam anenāmedhyenāmiṣeṇa durātmanānena te putreṇaitan māṃsam upahataṃ yato 'nena śaśo bhakṣitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 11.2]
tataś cāsau vikukṣir guruṇaivam uktaḥ śaśādasaṃjñām avāpa pitrā ca parityaktaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 12.1]
pitary uparate cākhilām etāṃ pṛthvīṃ dharmataḥ śaśāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 13.1]
śaśādasya puraṃjayo nāma putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 14.1]
idaṃ cānyat | [ViPur, 4, 2 15.1]
purā hi tretāyāṃ devāsuram atīva bhīṣaṇaṃ yuddham āsīt | [ViPur, 4, 2 15.2]
tatra cātibalibhir asurair amarāḥ parājitā bhagavantaṃ viṣṇum ārādhayāṃcakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 15.3]
prasannaś ca devānām anādinidhanaḥ sakalajagatparāyaṇo nārāyaṇaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 2 16.1]
jñātam eva mayā yuṣmābhir yad abhilaṣitaṃ tadartham idaṃ śrūyatām | [ViPur, 4, 2 16.2]
puraṃjayo nāma śaśādasya ca rājarṣes tanayaḥ kṣatriyavaryas taccharīre 'ham aṃśena svayam evāvatīrya tān aśeṣān asurān nihaniṣyāmi tad bhavadbhiḥ puraṃjayo 'suravadhārthāya kāryodyogaḥ kārya iti | [ViPur, 4, 2 16.3]
etacca śrutvā praṇamya bhagavantaṃ viṣṇum amarāḥ puraṃjayasakāśam ājagmuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 16.4]
ūcuś cainaṃ bho bhoḥ kṣatriyavaryāsmābhir abhyarthitena bhavatāsmākam arātivadhodyatānāṃ sāhāyyaṃ kṛtam icchāmaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 17.1]
tad bhavatāsmākam abhyāgatānāṃ praṇayabhaṅgo na kārya ity uktaḥ puraṃjayaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 2 17.2]
sakalatrailokyanātho yo 'yaṃ yuṣmākam indraḥ śatakratur asya yady ahaṃ skandhārūḍho yuṣmadarātibhiḥ saha yotsye tadāhaṃ bhavatāṃ sahāyaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 17.3]
ityākarṇya samastadevair indreṇa ca bāḍham ity evaṃ samanvicchitam | [ViPur, 4, 2 17.4]
tataśca śatakrator vṛṣabharūpadhāriṇaḥ kakutstho 'tiharṣasamanvito bhagavataś carācaraguror acyutasya tejasāpyāyito devāsurasaṃgrāme samastān evāsurān nijaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 2 18.1]
yataś ca vṛṣabhakakutsthena rājñā niṣūditam asurabalam ataś cāsau kakutsthasaṃjñām avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 2 19.1]
kakutsthasyāpy anenāḥ putro 'bhūt pṛthur anenasaḥ pṛthor viśvagaś ca tasyāpi cāndro yuvanāśvaścāndrasya tasya yuvanāśvasya śrāvasto yaḥ purīṃ śrāvastīṃ niveśayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 20.1]
śrāvastasya bṛhadaśvastasyāpi kuvalayāśvo yo 'sāvuttaṅkasya maharṣer apakāriṇaṃ dhundhunāmānam asuraṃ vaiṣṇavena tejasāpyāyitaḥ putrasahasrair ekaviṃśatibhiḥ parivṛto jaghāna dhundhumārasaṃjñāṃ cāvāpa | [ViPur, 4, 2 21.1]
tasya ca samastā eva putrā dundumukhaniśvāsāgninā vipluṣṭā vineśuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 22.1]
dṛḍhāśvacandrāśvakapilāśvās trayaḥ kevalaṃ avaśeṣitāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 23.1]
dṛḍhāśvāddharyaśvaḥ tasmān nikumbho nikumbhāt saṃhitāśvaḥ tataś ca kṛśāśvaḥ tasmācca prasenajit tato yuvanāśvo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 24.1]
tasya cāputrasyātinirvedān munīnām āśramamaṇḍale nivasataḥ kṛpālubhis tair munibhir apatyotpādanāya iṣṭiḥ kṛtā | [ViPur, 4, 2 25.1]
tasyāṃ ca madhyamadhyarātrinivṛttāyāṃ mantrapūtajalapūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ vedimadhye niveśya te munayaḥ suṣupuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 25.2]
teṣu ca supteṣvatitṛṭparītaḥ sa bhūpālastam āśramaṃ viveśa | [ViPur, 4, 2 26.1]
suptāṃśca tānṛṣīn naivotthāpayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 27.1]
tacca kalaśajalam aparimeyamāhātmyaṃ mantrapūtaṃ papau | [ViPur, 4, 2 27.2]
prabuddhāśca ṛṣayaḥ papracchuḥ kenaitan mantrapūtaṃ vāri pītam | [ViPur, 4, 2 28.1]
atra hi pīte rājño yuvanāśvasya patnī mahābalaparākramaṃ putraṃ janayiṣyatīty ityākarṇya sa rājā ajānatā mayā pītam ityāha | [ViPur, 4, 2 29.1]
garbhaśca yuvanāśvasyodare abhavat krameṇa ca vavṛdhe | [ViPur, 4, 2 30.1]
prāptasamayaśca dakṣiṇakukṣim avanīpater nirbhidya niścakrāma sa cāsau rājā mamāra | [ViPur, 4, 2 31.1]
jāto nāmaiṣa kaṃ dhāsyatīti munayaḥ procuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 32.1]
athāgamya devarāḍ 'bravīt mām ayaṃ dhāsyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 2 33.1]
tato māndhātā nāmato 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 34.1]
vaktre cāsya pradeśinī devarājena nyastā tāṃ papau | [ViPur, 4, 2 34.2]
tāṃ cāmṛtasrāviṇīm āsvādyāhnaiva sa vyavardhata | [ViPur, 4, 2 34.3]
tatas tu māndhātā cakravartī saptadvīpāṃ mahīṃ bubhuje | [ViPur, 4, 2 35.1]
bhavati cātra ślokaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 36.1]
yāvat sūrya udeti sma yāvacca pratitiṣṭhati | [ViPur, 4, 2 36.2]
sarvaṃ tad yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate | [ViPur, 4, 2 36.3]
māndhātā śaśabindorduhitaraṃ bindumatīm upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 2 37.1]
purukutsam ambarīṣaṃ ca mucukundaṃ ca tasyāṃ putratrayam utpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 37.2]
pañcāśacca duhitarastasya nṛpater babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 38.1]
bahvṛcaśca saubharirnāma maharṣirantarjale dvādaśābdaṃ kālam uvāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 39.1]
tatra cāntarjale matsyaḥ saṃmado nāmātibahuprajo 'tipramāṇo mīnādhipatir āsīt | [ViPur, 4, 2 40.1]
tasya ca putrapautradauhitrāḥ pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'grataḥ vakṣaḥpucchaśirasāṃ copari bhramantastenaiva sahāharniśam atinirvṛtā remire | [ViPur, 4, 2 40.2]
sa cāpi tatsparśopacīyamānaharṣaprakarṣo bahuprakāraṃ tasya ṛṣeḥ paśyatastairātmajapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahānudivasaṃ bahuprakāraṃ reme | [ViPur, 4, 2 41.1]
athāntarjalāvasthitaḥ sa saubharirekāgratāsamādhānam apahāyānudinaṃ tat tasya matsyasyātmajapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahātiramaṇīyaṃ lalitam avekṣyācintayat | [ViPur, 4, 2 42.1]
aho dhanyo 'yam īdṛśam anabhimataṃ yonyantaram avāpyaibhir ātmajapautrādibhiḥ saha ramamāṇo 'tīvāsmākaṃ spṛhām utpādayati | [ViPur, 4, 2 42.2]
vayam apyevaṃ putrādibhiḥ saha ramiṣyāmaḥ ityevam abhisamīkṣya sa tasmād antarjalānniṣkramya saṃtānāya nirveṣṭukāmaḥ kanyārthaṃ māndhātāraṃ rājānam agacchat | [ViPur, 4, 2 42.3]
āgamanaśravaṇasamanantaraṃ cotthāya tena rājñā samyag arghādinā pūjitaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ saubhariruvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 43.1]
saubhariruvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 44.1]

saubhariruvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 48.1]

rājovāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 50.1]

bhagavadājñāsmanmanorathānām apyagocaravartinī kathamapyeṣā saṃjātā tad evam upasthite na vidmaḥ kiṃ kurma ityetan mayā cintyate ityabhihite ca tena bhūbhujā muniracintayat | [ViPur, 4, 2 50.3]
aho 'yam anyo 'smatpratyākhyānopāyo vṛddho 'yam anabhimataḥ strīṇāṃ kimuta kanyānām ityamunā saṃcintyaivam abhihitam evam astu tathā kariṣyāmīti saṃcintya māndhātāram uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 50.4]
yadyevaṃ tadādiśyatām asmākaṃ praveśāya kanyāntaḥpuravarṣavaraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 51.1]
yadi kanyaiva kācin mām abhilaṣati tadāhaṃ dārasaṃgrahaṃ kariṣyāmi anyathā cet tad alam asmākam etenātītakālārambhaṇenety uktvā virarāma | [ViPur, 4, 2 51.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 52.1]
tataśca māndhātrā muniśāpaśaṅkitena kanyāntaḥpuravarṣadharaḥ samājñaptaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 52.2]
kanyāntaḥpuraṃ praviśann eva bhagavān akhilasiddhagandharvamanuṣebhyo 'tiśayena kamanīyaṃ rūpam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 2 53.1]
praveśya ca tam ṛṣim antaḥpuravarṣavaras tāḥ kanyakāḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 2 54.1]
bhavatīnāṃ janayitā mahārājaḥ samājñāpayati | [ViPur, 4, 2 55.1]
ayam asmān brahmarṣiḥ kanyārthī samabhyāgato mayā cāsya pratijñātaṃ yadyasmatkanyakā kācid bhagavantaṃ varayati tat kanyāyāśchande nāhaṃ paripanthānaṃ kariṣyāmītyākarṇya sarvā eva tāḥ kanyāḥ sānurāgāḥ samanmathāḥ kareṇava ivebhayūthapatiṃ tam ṛṣim ahamahamikayā varayāṃbabhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 55.2]
ūcuśca alaṃ bhaginyo 'ham imaṃ vṛṇomi vṛto mayā naiṣa tavānurūpaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 56.1]

kṛtānurūpavivāhaśca maharṣiḥ sakalā eva tāḥ kanyāḥ svam āśramam anayat | [ViPur, 4, 2 60.1]
tatra cāśeṣaśilpiśilpapraṇetāraṃ dhātāram ivānyaṃ viśvakarmāṇam āhūya sakalakanyānām ekaikasyāḥ protphullapaṅkajāḥ kūjatkalahaṃsakāraṇḍavādivihaṃgamābhirāma jalāśayāḥ sopavanāḥ sāvakāśāḥ sādhuśayyāsanaparicchadāḥ prāsādāḥ kriyantām ityādideśa | [ViPur, 4, 2 61.1]

tato 'navaratabhakṣyabhojyalehyādyupabhogair āgatānugatabhṛtyādīn aharniśam aśeṣagṛheṣu tāḥ kṣitīśaduhitaro bhojayāmāsuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 64.1]
ekadā tu duhitṛsnehākṛṣṭahṛdayaḥ sa mahīpatir atiduḥkhitāstāḥ sukhitā veti vicintya tasya maharṣer āśramam upetya sphuradaṃśumālāṃ sphaṭikamayīṃ prāsādātiramyopavanajalāśayāṃ dadarśa | [ViPur, 4, 2 65.1]
praviśya caikaṃ prāsādam ātmajāṃ pariṣvajya kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ pravṛddhasnehanayanāmbugarbhanayano 'bravīt | [ViPur, 4, 2 66.1]
apyatra vatse bhavatyāḥ sukham uta kiṃcid asukham api te maharṣiḥ snehavān uta saṃsmaryate 'smadgṛhavāsasyety uktā tattanayā pitaram āha | [ViPur, 4, 2 67.1]
tātātiramaṇīyaḥ prāsādo 'trātimanojñam upavanam atikalavākyavihaṃgamābhirutāḥ protphullapadmākarā jalāśayāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 68.1]
mano'nukūlabhakṣyabhojyānulepanavastrabhūṣaṇādibhogopabhogā mṛdūni śayanāni sarvasaṃpatsamavetam etad gārhasthyam | [ViPur, 4, 2 68.2]
tathāpi kena vā janmabhūmir na smaryate | [ViPur, 4, 2 68.3]
tvatprasādād idam aśeṣam atiśobhanam | [ViPur, 4, 2 69.1]

mamaiva kevalam atiprītyā samīpavartī nānyāsām asmadbhaginīnām | [ViPur, 4, 2 70.2]
evaṃ ca mama sodaryo duḥkhitā ityevam atiduḥkhakāraṇam ityuktastayā dvitīyaṃ prāsādam upetya svatanayāṃ pariṣvajyopaviṣṭas tathaiva pṛṣṭavān | [ViPur, 4, 2 71.1]
tayāpi tathaiva sarvam etat prāsādādyupabhogasukhaṃ ākhyātaṃ mamaiva kevalam atiprītyā pārśvavartī nāsmadbhaginīnām ityevamādi śrutvā samastaprāsādeṣu rājā praviveśa tanayāṃ tathaivāpṛcchat | [ViPur, 4, 2 72.1]
sarvābhistābhir abhihitaḥ paritoṣavismayanirbharavivaśahṛdayo bhagavantaṃ saubharim ekāntāvasthitam upetya kṛtapūjo 'bravīt | [ViPur, 4, 2 73.1]
dṛṣṭaste bhagavan sumahān eṣa siddhiprabhāvo naivaṃvidham anyasya kasyacid asmābhir vibhūtivilasitam upalakṣitaṃ kiyad etad bhagavaṃs tapasaḥ phalam ityabhipūjya tam ṛṣiṃ tatraiva tena ṛṣivaryeṇa saha kiṃcit kālam abhimatopabhogaṃ bubhuje svapuraṃ ca jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 2 74.1]
kālena gacchatā tasya tāsu rājatanayāsu putraśataṃ sārdham abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 75.1]
anudinānurūḍhasnehaprasaraś ca sa tatrātīva mamatākṛṣṭahṛdayo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 76.1]
apyete 'smatputrāḥ kalabhāṣiṇaḥ padbhyāṃ gaccheyuḥ apyete yauvanino bhaveyuḥ api kṛtadārān etān paśyeyam apyeṣāṃ putrā bhaveyuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 77.1]
apyetatputrān putrasamanvitān paśyeyam evamādimanorathān anudinakālasaṃpattivṛttim apekṣyaitat saṃcintayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 2 77.2]
aho me mohasyātivistāraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 77.3]
manorathānāṃ na samāptir asti varṣāyutenāpi tathābdalakṣaiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 78.1]
pūrṇeṣu pūrṇeṣu punar navānāṃ utpattayaḥ santi manorathānām | [ViPur, 4, 2 78.2]
padbhyāṃ gatā yauvaninaśca jātā dāraiśca saṃyogam itāḥ prasūtāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 79.1]
dṛṣṭāḥ sutāstattanayaprasūtiṃ draṣṭuṃ punar vāñchati me 'ntarātmā | [ViPur, 4, 2 79.2]

niḥsaṅgatā muktipadaṃ yatīnāṃ saṅgād aśeṣāḥ prabhavanti doṣāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 86.1]
ārūḍhayogo 'pi nipātyate 'dhaḥ saṅgena yogī kim utālpasiddhiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 86.2]
ahaṃ cariṣyāmi tathātmano 'rthe parigrahagrāhagṛhītabuddhiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 2 87.1]
yathā hi bhūyaḥ parihīnadoṣo janasya duḥkhair bhavitā na duḥkhī | [ViPur, 4, 2 87.2]

tasminn aśeṣaujasi sarvarūpiṇyavyaktavispaṣṭatanāvanante | [ViPur, 4, 2 89.1]

yasmānna kiṃcit tam ahaṃ gurūṇāṃ paraṃ guruṃ saṃśrayam emi viṣṇum | [ViPur, 4, 2 90.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 2 91.1]
ityātmānam ātmanaivābhidhāyāsau saubharir apahāya putragṛhāsanaparicchadādikam aśeṣam arthajātaṃ sakalabhāryāsamaveto vanaṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 2 91.2]
tatrāpyanudinaṃ vaikhānasaniṣpādyam aśeṣaṃ kriyākalāpaṃ niṣpādya kṣapitasakalapāpaḥ paripakvamanovṛttir ātmanyagnīn samāropya bhikṣur abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 2 92.1]
