parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 3 1.1]
ato māṃdhātuḥ putrasaṃtatir abhidhīyate | [ViPur, 4, 3 1.2]
ambarīṣasya māṃdhātus tanayasya yuvanāśvaḥ putro 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 3 2.1]
tasmāddharīto yato 'ṅgirasaḥ hārītāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 3.1]
rasātale ca mauneyā nāma gandharvāḥ ṣaṭkoṭisaṃkhyās tair aśeṣāṇi nāgakulāny apahṛtapradhānaratnādhipatyāny akriyanta | [ViPur, 4, 3 4.1]
taiś ca gandharvavīryavidhūtair bhagavān aśeṣadeveśastavaśravaṇonmīlitonnidrapuṇḍarīkanayano jalaśayano nidrāvasānād vibuddhaḥ praṇipatyābhihitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 5.1]
bhagavann apyasmākam etebhyo gandharvebhyo bhayam upaśamam eṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 3 5.2]
āha bhagavān anādipuruṣaḥ puruṣottamo yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ purukutsanāmā putras tam aham anupraviśya tān aśeṣaduṣṭagandharvān upaśamaṃ nayiṣyāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 3 5.3]
ityākarṇya bhagavate kṛtapraṇāmāḥ punar nāgilokam āgatāḥ pannagapatayo narmadāṃ ca purukutsānayanāya codayāmāsuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 6.1]
sā cainaṃ rasātalaṃ nītavatī | [ViPur, 4, 3 7.1]
rasātalagataś cāsau bhagavattejasāpyāyitātmavīryaḥ sakalagandharvāñjaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 3 8.1]
punaśca svabhavanam ājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 3 8.2]
sakalapannagapatayaś ca narmadāyai varaṃ daduḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 9.1]
yas te 'nusmaraṇasamavetaṃ nāmagrahaṇaṃ kariṣyati na tasya sarpaviṣabhayaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 3 9.2]
atra ca ślokaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 10.1]
narmadāyai namaḥ prātar narmadāyai namo niśi | [ViPur, 4, 3 10.2]
namo 'stu narmade tubhyaṃ trāhi māṃ viṣasarpataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 10.3]
ityuccāryāharniśam andhakārapraveśe vā na sarpair daśyate na cāpi kṛtānusmaraṇabhujo viṣam api bhuktam upaghātāya bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 3 11.1]
purukutsāya saṃtativicchedo na bhavato bhaviṣyatītyuragapatayo varaṃ daduḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 12.1]
purukutso narmadāyāṃ trasadasyum ajījanat | [ViPur, 4, 3 13.1]
trasadasyutaḥ sambhūtastato 'naraṇyas taṃ rāvaṇo digvijaye nijaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 3 14.1]
anaraṇyasya pṛṣadaśvaḥ pṛṣadaśvasya haryaśvaḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 3 14.2]
tataśca vasumanās tasyāpi tridhanvā tridhanvanas trayyāruṇaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 14.3]
tasmātsatyavrato yo 'sau triśaṅkusaṃjñām avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 3 14.4]
caṇḍālatām upagataśca | [ViPur, 4, 3 14.5]
dvādaśavārṣikyām anāvṛṣṭyāṃ viśvāmitrakalatrāpatyapoṣaṇārthaṃ caṇḍālapratigrahapariharaṇāya jāhnavītīranyagrodhe mṛgamāṃsam anudinaṃ babandha | [ViPur, 4, 3 15.1]
parituṣṭena viśvāmitreṇa saśarīraḥ svargam āropitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 16.1]
triśaṅkor hariścandras tasmācca rohitāśvas tataśca harito haritasya cañcuś cañcorvijayavasudevau ruruko vijayād rurukasya vṛkaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 25.1]
tato vṛkasya bāhuḥ yo 'sau haihayatālajaṅghādibhiḥ parājito 'ntarvatnyā mahiṣyā saha vanaṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 3 26.1]
tasyāś ca sapatnyā garbhastambhanāya garo dattaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 27.1]
tenāsyā garbhaḥ saptavarṣāṇi jaṭhara eva tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 3 28.1]
sa ca bāhur vṛddhabhāvād aurvāśramasamīpe mamāra | [ViPur, 4, 3 29.1]
sā tasya bhāryā citāṃ kṛtvā tam āropyānumaraṇakṛtaniścayābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 3 30.1]
athaitām atītānāgatavartamānakālatrayavedī bhagavān aurvaḥ svāśramān nirgatyābravīt | [ViPur, 4, 3 31.1]
alam alam anenāsadgrāheṇākhilabhūmaṇḍalapatir ativīryaparākramo naikayajñakṛd arātipakṣakṣayakartā tavodare cakravartī tiṣṭhati | [ViPur, 4, 3 32.1]
naivam atisāhasādhyavasāyinī bhavatī bhavet yuktā sā tasmād anumaraṇanirbandhād virarāma | [ViPur, 4, 3 33.1]
tenaiva ca bhagavatā svāśramam ānītā | [ViPur, 4, 3 34.1]
tatra katipayadinābhyantare ca sahaiva tena gareṇātitejasvī bālako jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 3 35.1]
tasyaurvo jātakarmādikriyā niṣpādya sagara iti nāma cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 3 36.1]
kṛtopanayanaṃ cainam aurvo vedaśāstrāṇy astraṃ cāgneyaṃ bhārgavākhyam adhyāpayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 3 37.1]
utpannabuddhiś ca mātaram abravīt | [ViPur, 4, 3 38.1]
amba kathayātra vayaṃ kva tāto 'smākam ity evamādi pṛcchantaṃ mātā sarvam evāvocat | [ViPur, 4, 3 39.1]
tataś ca pitṛrājyāpaharaṇād amarṣito haihayatālajaṅghādivadhāya pratijñām akarot | [ViPur, 4, 3 40.1]
prāyaśaś ca haihayatālajaṅghāñ jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 3 41.1]
śakayavanakāmbhojapāradapaplavāḥ hanyamānās tatkulaguruṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 42.1]
athainān vasiṣṭho jīvanmṛtakān kṛtvā sagaram āha | [ViPur, 4, 3 43.1]
vatsālam ebhir jīvanmṛtakair anumṛtaiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 44.1]
ete ca mayaiva tvatpratijñāparipālanāya nijadharmadvijasaṅgaparityāgaṃ kāritāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 45.1]
tatheti tad guruvacanam abhinandya teṣāṃ veṣānyatvam akārayat | [ViPur, 4, 3 46.1]
yavanān muṇḍitaśiraso 'rdhamuṇḍitāñchakān pralambakeśān pāradān paplavāñśmaśrudharān niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārān etān anyāṃś ca kṣatriyāṃś cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 3 47.1]
ete cātmadharmaparityāgād brāhmaṇaiḥ parityaktā mlecchatāṃ yayuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 3 48.1]
sagaro 'pi svam adhiṣṭhānam āgamya askhalitacakraḥ saptadvīpavatīm imām urvīṃ praśaśāsa | [ViPur, 4, 3 49.1]
{ViPur, 4, 4}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 4 1.1]
kāśyapaduhitā sumatir vidarbharājatanayā keśinī ca dve bhārye sagarasyāstām | [ViPur, 4, 4 1.2]
tābhyāṃ cāpatyārtham aurvaḥ parameṇa samādhinārādhito varam adāt | [ViPur, 4, 4 2.1]
ekā vaṃśakaram ekaṃ putram aparā ṣaṣṭiṃ putrasahasrāṇāṃ janayiṣyatīti yasyā yad abhimataṃ tad icchayā gṛhyatām ityukte keśinyekaṃ varayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 4 3.1]
sumatiḥ putrasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ vavre | [ViPur, 4, 4 4.1]
tathetyukte alpair ahobhiḥ keśinī putram ekam asamañjasanāmānaṃ vaṃśakaram asūta | [ViPur, 4, 4 5.1]
kāśyapatanayāyāstu sumatyāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ putrasahasrāṇyabhavan | [ViPur, 4, 4 6.1]
tasmād asamañjasād aṃśumān nāma kumāro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 4 7.1]
sa tv asamañjaso bālo bālyād evāsadvṛtto 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 4 8.1]
pitā cāsyācintayad ayam atītabālyaḥ subuddhimān bhaviṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 4 9.1]
atha tatrāpi ca vayasyatīte asaccaritam enaṃ pitā tatyāja | [ViPur, 4, 4 10.1]
tānyapi ṣaṣṭiḥ putrasahasrāṇyasamañjasacaritam evānucakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 11.1]
tataścāsamañjasacaritānukāribhiḥ sāgarair apadhvastayajñaiḥ sanmārge jagati devāḥ sakalavidyāmayam asaṃspṛṣṭam aśeṣadoṣair bhagavataḥ puruṣottamasyāṃśabhūtaṃ kapilaṃ praṇamya tadartham ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 12.1]
bhagavann ebhiḥ sagaratanayair asamañjasacaritam anugamyate | [ViPur, 4, 4 13.1]
katham ebhir asadvṛttam anusaradbhir jagad bhaviṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 4 14.1]
atyārtajagatparitrāṇāya ca bhagavato 'tra śarīragrahaṇam ity ākarṇya bhagavān āhālpair eva dinair vinaṅkṣyantīti | [ViPur, 4, 4 15.1]
atrāntare ca sagaro hayamedham ārabhata | [ViPur, 4, 4 16.1]
tasya ca putrair adhiṣṭhitam asyāśvaṃ ko 'py apahṛtya bhuvo bilaṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 4 17.1]
tatas tattanayāś cāśvakhuragatinirbandhenāvanīm ekaiko yojanaṃ cakhnuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 18.1]
pātāle cāśvaṃ paribhramantaṃ tam avanīpatitanayās te dadṛśuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 19.1]
nātidūre 'vasthitaṃ ca bhagavantam apaghane śaratkāle 'rkam iva tejobhir avanatamūrdham adhaścāśeṣadiśaścodbhāsayamānaṃ hayahartāraṃ kapilarṣim apaśyan | [ViPur, 4, 4 20.1]
tataś codyatāyudhā durātmāno 'yam asmadapakārī yajñavighnakārī hanyatāṃ hayahartā hanyatām ity avocann abhyadhāvaṃś ca | [ViPur, 4, 4 21.1]
tatas tenāpi bhagavatā kiṃcidīṣatparivartitalocanenāvalokitāḥ svaśarīrasamutthenāgninā dahyamānā vineśuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 22.1]
sagaro 'pyavagamyāśvānusāri tat putrabalam aśeṣaṃ paramarṣiṇā kapilena tejasā dagdhaṃ tato 'ṃśumantam asamañjasaputram aśvānayanāya yuyoja | [ViPur, 4, 4 23.1]
sa tu sagaratanayakhātamārgeṇa kapilam upagamya bhaktinamras tadā tuṣṭāva | [ViPur, 4, 4 24.1]
athainaṃ bhagavān āha | [ViPur, 4, 4 25.1]
gacchainaṃ pitāmahāyāśvaṃ prāpaya varaṃ vṛṇīṣva ca putraka pautrāśca te svargād gaṅgāṃ bhuvam āneṣyanta iti | [ViPur, 4, 4 26.1]
athāṃśumān api svaryātānāṃ brahmadaṇḍahatānām asmatpitṝṇām asvargayogyānāṃ svargaprāptikaraṃ varam asmākaṃ prayaccheti pratyāha | [ViPur, 4, 4 27.1]
tad ākarṇya taṃ ca bhagavān āha uktam evaitan mayādya pautraste tridivād gaṅgāṃ bhuvam ānayiṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 4 28.1]
tadambhasā ca saṃspṛṣṭeṣvasthibhasmasu ete ca svargam ārokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 4 29.1]
bhagavadviṣṇupādāṅguṣṭhanirgatasya hi jalasyaitan māhātmyam | [ViPur, 4, 4 30.1]
yan na kevalam abhisaṃdhipūrvakaṃ snānādyupabhogeṣūpakārakam anabhisaṃdhitam apy asyāṃ pretaprāṇasyāsthicarmasnāyukeśādyupaspṛṣṭaṃ śarīrajam api patitaṃ sadyaḥ śarīriṇaṃ svargaṃ nayatīty uktaḥ praṇamya bhagavate 'śvam ādāya pitāmahayajñam ājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 4 31.1]
sagaro 'py aśvam āsādya taṃ yajñaṃ samāpayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 4 32.1]
sāgaraṃ cātmajaprītyā putratve kalpitavān | [ViPur, 4, 4 33.1]
tasyāṃśumato dilīpaḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 34.1]
dilīpasya bhagīrathaḥ yo 'sau gaṅgāṃ svargād ihānīya bhāgīrathīsaṃjñāṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 4 35.1]
bhagīrathāt suhotraḥ suhotrācchrutaḥ tasyāpi nābhāgaḥ tato 'mbarīṣaḥ tatputraḥ sindhudvīpaḥ sindhudvīpād ayutāyuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 36.1]
tatputraś ca ṛtuparṇaḥ yo 'sau nalasahāyo 'kṣahṛdayajño 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 4 37.1]
ṛtuparṇaputraḥ sarvakāmaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 38.1]
tattanayaḥ sudāsaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 39.1]
sudāsāt saudāso mitrasahanāmā | [ViPur, 4, 4 40.1]
sa cāṭavyāṃ mṛgayārthī paryaṭan vyāghradvayam apaśyat | [ViPur, 4, 4 41.1]
tābhyāṃ tad vanam apamṛgaṃ kṛtaṃ matvaikaṃ tayor bāṇena jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 4 42.1]
mriyamāṇaścāsāvatibhīṣaṇākṛtir atikarālavadano rākṣaso 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 4 43.1]
dvitīyo 'pi pratikriyāṃ te kariṣyāmīty uktvāntardhānaṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 4 44.1]
kālena gacchatā saudāso yajñam ayajat | [ViPur, 4, 4 45.1]
pariniṣṭhitayajñe ācārye vasiṣṭhe niṣkrānte tad rakṣo vasiṣṭharūpam āsthāya yajñāvasāne mama naramāṃsabhojanaṃ deyam iti tat saṃskriyatāṃ kṣaṇād āgamiṣyāmīty uktvā niṣkrāntaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 46.1]
bhūyaś ca sūdaveṣaṃ kṛtvā rājājñayā mānuṣaṃ māṃsaṃ saṃskṛtya rājñe nyavedayat | [ViPur, 4, 4 47.1]
asāv api hiraṇyapātre māṃsam ādāya vasiṣṭhāgamanapratīkṣo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 48.1]
āgatāya vasiṣṭhāya niveditavān | [ViPur, 4, 4 49.1]
sa cāpy acintayad aho 'sya rājño dauḥśīlyaṃ yenaitan māṃsam asmākaṃ prayacchati kim etad dravyajātam iti dhyānaparo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 50.1]
apaśyacca tan māṃsaṃ mānuṣam | [ViPur, 4, 4 51.1]
ataḥ krodhakaluṣīkṛtacetā rājani śāpam utsasarja | [ViPur, 4, 4 52.1]
yasmād abhojyam etad asmadvidhānāṃ tapasvinām avagacchann api bhavān mahyaṃ dadāti tasmāt tavaivātra lolupatā bhaviṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 4 53.1]
anantaraṃ ca tenāpi bhagavataivābhihito 'smīty ukte kiṃ kiṃ mayābhihitam iti muniḥ punar api samādhau tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 4 54.1]
samādhivijñānāvagatārthaś cānugrahaṃ tasmai cakāra nātyantikam etad dvādaśābdaṃ tava bhojanaṃ bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 4 55.1]
asāvapi pratigṛhyodakāñjaliṃ muniśāpapradānāyodyato bhagavann ayam asmadgurur nārhasyenaṃ kuladevatābhūtam ācāryaṃ śaptum iti madayantyā svapatnyā prasāditaḥ sasyāmbudarakṣaṇārthaṃ tacchāpāmbu norvyāṃ na cākāśe cikṣepa kiṃtu tenaiva svapadau siṣeca | [ViPur, 4, 4 56.1]
tena ca krodhāśritenāmbunā dagdhacchāyau tatpādau kalmāṣatām upagatau | [ViPur, 4, 4 57.1]
tataḥ sa kalmāṣapādasaṃjñām avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 4 57.2]
vasiṣṭhaśāpācca ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe kāle rākṣasasvabhāvam etyāṭavyāṃ paryaṭann anekaśo mānuṣān abhakṣayat | [ViPur, 4, 4 58.1]
ekadā tu kaṃcin munim ṛtukāle bhāryāsaṃgataṃ dadarśa | [ViPur, 4, 4 59.1]
tayośca tam atibhīṣaṇaṃ rākṣasasvarūpam avalokya trāsād dampatyoḥ pradhāvitayor brāhmaṇaṃ jagrāha | [ViPur, 4, 4 60.1]
tataḥ sā brāhmaṇī bahuśas tam abhiyācitavatī | [ViPur, 4, 4 61.1]
prasīdekṣvākukulatilakabhūtas tvaṃ mahārājo mitrasaho na rākṣasaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 62.1]
nārhasi strīdharmasukhābhijño mayyakṛtārthāyām asmadbhartāraṃ hantum ity evaṃ bahuprakāraṃ tasyāṃ vilapantyāṃ vyāghraḥ paśum ivāraṇye 'bhimataṃ taṃ brāhmaṇam abhakṣayat | [ViPur, 4, 4 63.1]
tataś cātikopasamanvitā brāhmaṇī taṃ rājānaṃ śaśāpa | [ViPur, 4, 4 64.1]
yasmād evaṃ mayy atṛptāyāṃ tvayāyaṃ matpatir bhakṣitaḥ tasmāt tvam api kāmopabhogapravṛtto 'ntaṃ prāpsyasīti | [ViPur, 4, 4 65.1]
śaptvā caiva sāgniṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 4 66.1]
tatas tasya dvādaśābdaparyaye vimuktaśāpasya strīviṣayābhilāṣiṇo madayantī taṃ smārayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 4 67.1]
tataḥ param asau strībhogaṃ tatyāja | [ViPur, 4, 4 68.1]
vasiṣṭhaścāputreṇa rājñā putrārtham abhyarthito madayantyāṃ garbhādhānaṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 4 69.1]
yadā ca sapta varṣāṇyasau garbheṇa jajñe tatastaṃ garbham aśmanā sā devī jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 4 70.1]
putraś cājāyata | [ViPur, 4, 4 71.1]
tasya cāśmaka ityeva nāmābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 72.1]
aśmasya mūlako nāma putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 73.1]
yo 'sau niḥkṣatre kṣmātale 'smin kriyamāṇe strībhir vivastrābhiḥ parivārya rakṣitaḥ tatas taṃ nārīkavacam udāharanti | [ViPur, 4, 4 74.1]
mūlakād daśarathas tasmād ilivilas tataśca viśvasahaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 75.1]
tasmāc ca khaṭvāṅgaḥ yo 'sau devāsurasaṃgrāme devair abhyarthito 'surāñ jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 4 76.1]
svarge ca kṛtapriyair devair varagrahaṇāya coditaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 4 77.1]
yady avaśyaṃ varo grāhyaḥ tanmamāyuḥ kathyatām iti | [ViPur, 4, 4 78.1]
anantaraṃ ca tairuktaṃ muhūrtam ekaṃ pramāṇaṃ tavāyurityukto 'thāskhalitagatinā vimānena laghimādiguṇo martyalokam āgamyedam āha | [ViPur, 4, 4 79.1]
yathā na brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sakāśād ātmāpi me priyataraḥ na ca svadharmollaṅghanaṃ mayā kadācid apy anuṣṭhitaṃ na ca sakaladevamānuṣapaśupakṣivṛkṣādikeṣvacyutavyatirekavatī dṛṣṭir mamābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 4 80.1]
tathā tam evaṃ munijanānusmṛtaṃ bhagavantam askhalitagatiḥ prāpayeyam ityaśeṣadevagurau bhagavaty anirdeśyavapuṣi sattāmātrātmanyātmānaṃ paramātmani vāsudevākhye yuyoja | [ViPur, 4, 4 80.2]
tatraiva ca layam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 4 80.3]
khaṭvāṅgād dīrghabāhuḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 81.1]
tato raghur abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 82.1]
tasmād apy ajaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 83.1]
ajād daśarathaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 84.1]
tasyāpi bhagavān abjanābho jagataḥ sthityartham ātmāṃśena rāmalakṣmaṇabharataśatrughnarūpeṇa caturdhā putratvam āyāsīt | [ViPur, 4, 4 85.1]
rāmo 'pi bāla eva viśvāmitrayāgarakṣaṇāya gacchaṃs tāṭakāṃ jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 4 86.1]
yajñe ca mārīcam iṣuvātāhataṃ samudre cikṣepa | [ViPur, 4, 4 87.1]
subāhupramukhāṃś ca kṣayam anayat | [ViPur, 4, 4 88.1]
darśanamātreṇāhalyām apāpāṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 4 89.1]
janakagṛhe ca māheśvaraṃ cāpam anāyāsena babhañja | [ViPur, 4, 4 90.1]
sītām ayonijāṃ janakarājatanayāṃ vīryaśulkāṃ lebhe | [ViPur, 4, 4 91.1]
sakalakṣatriyakṣayakāriṇam aśeṣahaihayakuladhūmaketubhūtaṃ ca paraśurāmam apāstavīryabalāvalepaṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 4 92.1]
pitṛvacanāc cāgaṇitarājyābhilāṣo bhrātṛbhāryāsameto vanaṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 4 93.1]
virādhakharadūṣaṇādīn kabandhavālinau ca nijaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 4 94.1]
baddhvā cāmbhonidhim aśeṣarākṣasakulakṣayaṃ kṛtvā daśānanāpahṛtāṃ bhāryāṃ tadvadhād apahṛtakalaṅkām apy analapraveśaśuddhām aśeṣadevasaṅghaiḥ stūyamānaśīlāṃ janakarājakanyām ayodhyām āninye | [ViPur, 4, 4 95.1]
tataś cābhiṣekamaṅgalaṃ maitreya varṣaśatenāpi vaktuṃ na śakyate saṃkṣepeṇa śrūyatām | [ViPur, 4, 4 96.1]
lakṣmaṇabharataśatrughnavibhīṣaṇasugrīvāṅgadajāmbavaddhanumatprabhṛtibhiḥ samutphullavadanaiś chattracāmarādiyutaiḥ sevyamāno dāśarathir brahmendrāgniyamanirṛtivaruṇavāyukubereśānaprabhṛtibhiḥ sarvāmarair vasiṣṭhavāmadevavālmīkimārkaṇḍeyaviśvāmitrabharadvājāgastyaprabhṛtibhir munivaraiḥ ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvaiḥ saṃstūyamāno nṛtyagītavādyādyakhilalokamaṅgalavādyair vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgabherīpaṭahaśaṅkhakāhalagomukhaprabhṛtibhiḥ sunādaiḥ samastabhūbhṛtāṃ madhye sakalalokarakṣārthaṃ yathocitam abhiṣikto dāśarathiḥ kosalendro raghukulatilako jānakīpriyo bhrātṛtrayapriyaḥ siṃhāsanagata ekādaśābdasahasraṃ rājyam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 4 97]
bharato 'pi gandharvaviṣayasādhanāya gacchan saṃgrāme gandharvakoṭīs tisro jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 4 98.1]
śatrughnenāpy amitabalaparākramo madhuputro lavaṇo nāma rākṣaso nihato mathurā ca niveśitā | [ViPur, 4, 4 99.1]
ityevamādi atibalaparākramavikramaṇair atiduṣṭasaṃhāriṇo 'śeṣasya jagato niṣpāditasthitayo rāmalakṣmaṇabharataśatrughnāḥ punar api divam ārūḍhāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 100.1]
ye 'pi teṣu bhagavadaṃśeṣvanurāgiṇaḥ kosalanagarajānapadās te 'pi tanmanasas tatsālokyatām avāpuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 101.1]
atiduṣṭasaṃhāriṇo rāmasya kuśalavau dvau putrau lakṣmaṇasyāṅgadacandraketū takṣapuṣkalau bharatasya subāhuśūrasenau śatrughnasya | [ViPur, 4, 4 102.1]
kuśasyātithir atither api niṣadhaḥ putro 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 4 103.1]
niṣadhasyāpyanalas tasmād api nabhāḥ nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkas tattanayaḥ kṣemadhanvā tasya ca devānīkas tasyāpy ahīnako 'hīnakasyāpi rurus tasya ca pāriyātrakaḥ pāriyātrād devalo devalād vaccalaḥ tasyāpy utkaḥ utkācca vajranābhas tasmācchaṅkhaṇas tasmādyuṣitāśvas tataśca viśvasaho jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 4 104.1]
tasmāddhiraṇyanābhaḥ yo mahāyogīśvarājjaimineḥ śiṣyād yājñavalkyādyogam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 4 105.1]
hiraṇyanābhasya putraḥ puṣyas tasmād dhruvasandhistataḥ sudarśanas tasmādagnivarṇas tataḥ śīghragas tasmādapi maruḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 4 106.1]
yo 'sau yogam āsthāyādyāpi kalāpagrāmam āśritya tiṣṭhati | [ViPur, 4, 4 107.1]
āgāmiyuge sūryavaṃśakṣatravrata āvartayitā bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 4 108.1]
tasyātmajaḥ praśuśrukas tasyāpi susaṃdhis tataś cāpyamarṣastasya ca sahasvāṃstataśca viśvabhavaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 4 109.1]
tasya bṛhadbalaḥ yo 'rjunatanayenābhimanyunā bhāratayuddhe kṣayam anīyata | [ViPur, 4, 4 110.1]
{ViPur, 4, 5}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 5 1.1]
ikṣvākutanayo yo 'sau nimir nāmnā sahasraṃ vatsaraṃ satram ārebhe | [ViPur, 4, 5 1.2]
vasiṣṭhaṃ ca hotāraṃ varayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 5 2.1]
tam āha vasiṣṭho 'ham indreṇa pañcavarṣaśatayāgārthaṃ prathamaṃ vṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 3.1]
tadanantaraṃ pratipālyatām āgatas tavāpi ṛtvik bhaviṣyāmītyukte sa pṛthivīpatir na kiṃcid uktavān | [ViPur, 4, 5 4.1]
vasiṣṭho 'py anena samanvicchitam ityamarapater yāgam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 5 5.1]
so 'pi tatkāla evānyair gautamādibhir yāgam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 5 6.1]
samāpte cāmarapater yāge tvarayā vasiṣṭho nimiyajñaṃ kariṣyāmīty ājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 5 7.1]
tatkarmakartṛtvaṃ ca gautamasya dṛṣṭvā svapate tasmai rājñe māṃ pratyākhyāyaiva tad anena gautamāya karmāntaraṃ samarpitaṃ yasmāt tasmād ayaṃ videho bhaviṣyatīti śāpaṃ dadau | [ViPur, 4, 5 8.1]
prabuddhaścāsāvavanipatir api prāha | [ViPur, 4, 5 9.1]
yasmānmām asaṃbhāṣyājñānata eva śayānasya śāpotsargam asau duṣṭaguruścakāra tasmāt tasyāpi dehaḥ patiṣyatīti śāpaṃ dattvā deham atyajat | [ViPur, 4, 5 10.1]
tacchāpācca mitrāvaruṇayostejasi vasiṣṭhasya cetaḥ praviṣṭam | [ViPur, 4, 5 11.1]
urvaśīdarśanād udbhūtabījaprapātayos tayoḥ sakāśād vasiṣṭho deham aparaṃ lebhe | [ViPur, 4, 5 12.1]
nimer api taccharīram atimanoharagandhatailādibhir upasaṃskriyamāṇaṃ naiva kledādikaṃ doṣam avāpa sadyo mṛta iva tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 5 13.1]
yajñasamāptau bhāgagrahaṇāya devān āgatān ṛtvija ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 14.1]
yajamānāya varo dīyatām iti | [ViPur, 4, 5 14.2]
devaiśca chandito 'sau nimir āha | [ViPur, 4, 5 15.1]
bhagavanto 'khilasaṃsāraduḥkhahantāraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 16.1]
na hy etādṛg anyad duḥkham asti yaccharīrātmanor viyoge bhavati | [ViPur, 4, 5 17.1]
tad aham icchāmi sakalalokalocaneṣu vastuṃ na punaḥ śarīragrahaṇaṃ kartum ityevam uktair devair asāv aśeṣabhūtānāṃ netreṣv avatāritaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 18.1]
tato bhūtāny unmeṣanimeṣaṃ cakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 19.1]
aputrasya ca tasya bhūbhujaḥ śarīram arājakabhīravo munayo 'raṇyā mamanthuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 20.1]
tatra ca kumāro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 5 21.1]
jananājjanakasaṃjñāṃ cāvāpa | [ViPur, 4, 5 22.1]
abhūd videho 'sya piteti vaidehaḥ mathanān mithir iti | [ViPur, 4, 5 23.1]
tasyodāvasuḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 5 24.1]
udāvasor nandivardhanas tataḥ suketuḥ tasmād devarātas tataśca bṛhadukthaḥ tasya ca mahāvīryas tasyāpi sudhṛtiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 25.1]
tataś ca dhṛṣṭaketur ajāyata | [ViPur, 4, 5 26.1]
dhṛṣṭaketor haryaśvas tasya ca manuḥ manoḥ pratikaḥ tasmātkṛtarathas tasya devamīḍhaḥ tasya ca vibudhaḥ vibudhasya mahādhṛtis tataśca kṛtarātaḥ tato mahāromā tasya svarṇaromā tatputro hrasvaromā hrasvaromṇaḥ sīradhvajo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 5 27.1]
tasya putrārthaṃ yajanabhuvaṃ kṛṣataḥ sīre sītā duhitā samutpannā | [ViPur, 4, 5 28.1]
sīradhvajasya bhrātā sāṅkāśyadhipatiḥ kuśadhvajanāmāsīt | [ViPur, 4, 5 29.1]
sīradhvajasyāpatyaṃ bhānumān bhānumataḥ śatadyumnaḥ tasya tu śuciḥ tasmāccorjanāmā putro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 5 30.1]
tasyāpi śatadhvajaḥ tataḥ kṛtiḥ kṛter añjanaḥ tatputraḥ kurujit tato 'riṣṭanemiḥ tasmācchrutāyuḥ śrutāyuṣaḥ supārśvaḥ tasmāt sṛñjayaḥ tataḥ kṣemāvī kṣemāvino 'nenāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 31.1]
tasmād bhaumarathaḥ tasya satyarathaḥ tasmādupaguḥ upagor upaguptaḥ tatputraḥ svāgatas tasya ca svānandaḥ tasmāc ca suvarcāḥ tasya ca supārśvaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 31.2]
tasyāpi subhāṣaḥ tasya suśrutaḥ tasmāt suśrutājjayaḥ tasya putro vijayaḥ vijayasya ṛtaḥ ṛtāt sunayaḥ sunayād vītahavyaḥ tasmād dhṛtiḥ dhṛter bahulāśvaḥ tasya putraḥ kṛtiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 31.3]
kṛtau saṃtiṣṭhaty ayaṃ janakavaṃśaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 32.1]
ityete maithilāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 5 33.1]
prāyeṇaite ātmavidyāśrayiṇo bhūpālā bhavanti | [ViPur, 4, 5 34.1]
{ViPur, 4, 6}
sūryasya bhagavan vaṃśaḥ kathito bhavatā mama | [ViPur, 4, 6 1.1]
somasya vaṃśe tvakhilāñśrotum icchāmi pārthivān | [ViPur, 4, 6 1.2]
kīrtyate sthirakīrtīnāṃ yeṣām adyāpi saṃtatiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 2.1]
prasādasumukhas tan me brahmann ākhyātum arhasi | [ViPur, 4, 6 2.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 6 3.1]
śrūyatāṃ muniśārdūla vaṃśaḥ prathitatejasaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 3.2]
somasyānukramāt khyātā yatrorvīpatayo 'bhavan | [ViPur, 4, 6 3.3]
ayaṃ hi vaṃśo 'tibalaparākramadyutiśīlaceṣṭāvadbhir atiguṇānvitair nahuṣayayātikārtavīryārjunādibhir bhūpālair alaṃkṛtaḥ tam ahaṃ kathayāmi śrūyatām | [ViPur, 4, 6 4.1]
akhilajagatsraṣṭur bhagavato nārāyaṇasya nābhisarojasamudbhavābjayoner brahmaṇaḥ putro 'triḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 5.1]
atreḥ somaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 6.1]
taṃ ca bhagavān abjayoniḥ aśeṣauṣadhīdvijanakṣatrāṇām ādhipatye 'bhyaṣecayat | [ViPur, 4, 6 7.1]
sa ca rājasūyam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 6 8.1]
tatprabhāvād atyutkṛṣṭādhipatyādhiṣṭhātṛtvāc cainaṃ mada āviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 6 9.1]
madāvalepāc ca sakaladevaguror bṛhaspates tārāṃ nāma patnīṃ jahāra | [ViPur, 4, 6 10.1]
bahuśaś ca bṛhaspaticoditena bhagavatā brahmaṇā codyamānaḥ sakalaiś ca devarṣibhir yācamāno 'pi na mumoca | [ViPur, 4, 6 11.1]
tasya candrasya ca bṛhaspater dveṣād uśanā pārṣṇigrāho 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 6 12.1]
aṅgirasaś ca sakāśād upalabdhavidyo bhagavān rudro bṛhaspateḥ sāhāyyam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 6 13.1]
yataś cośanā tato jambhakumbhādyāḥ samastā eva daityadānavanikāyā mahāntam udyamaṃ cakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 14.1]
bṛhaspater api sakaladevasainyayutaḥ sahāyaḥ śakro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 6 15.1]
evaṃ ca tayor atīvograsaṃgrāmas tārānimittas tārakāmayo nāmābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 6 16.1]
tataś ca samastaśastrāṇyasureṣu rudrapurogamā devā deveṣu cāśeṣadānavā mumucuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 17.1]
evaṃ devāsurāhavasaṃkṣobhakṣubdhahṛdayam aśeṣaṃ eva jagad brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 6 18.1]
tataś ca bhagavān abjayonir apyuśanasaṃ śaṃkaram asurān devāṃś ca nivārya bṛhaspataye tārām adāpayat | [ViPur, 4, 6 19.1]
tāṃ cāntaḥprasavām avalokya bṛhaspatir apyāha | [ViPur, 4, 6 20.1]
naiṣa mama kṣetre bhavatyānyasya suto dhāryaḥ samutsṛjainam alam alam atidhārṣṭyeneti | [ViPur, 4, 6 21.1]
sā ca tenaivam uktātipativratā bhartṛvacanānantaraṃ tam iṣīkāstambe garbham utsasarja | [ViPur, 4, 6 22.1]
sa cotsṛṣṭamātra evātitejasā devānāṃ tejāṃsyācikṣepa | [ViPur, 4, 6 23.1]
bṛhaspatim induṃ ca tasya kumārasyāticārutayā sābhilāṣau dṛṣṭvā devāḥ samutpannasaṃdehās tārāṃ papracchuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 24.1]
satyaṃ kathayāsmākam iti subhage somasyātha vā bṛhaspater ayaṃ putra iti | [ViPur, 4, 6 25.1]
evaṃ tair uktā sā tārā hriyā kiṃcin novāca | [ViPur, 4, 6 26.1]
bahuśo 'pyabhihitā yadāsau devebhyo nācacakṣe tataḥ sa kumāras tāṃ śaptum udyataḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 6 27.1]
duṣṭe 'mba kasmān mama tātaṃ nākhyāsi | [ViPur, 4, 6 28.1]
adyaiva te vyalīkalajjāvatyās tathā śāstim ahaṃ karomi | [ViPur, 4, 6 29.1]
yathā ca naivam adyāpyatimantharavacanā bhaviṣyasīti | [ViPur, 4, 6 30.1]
athāha bhagavān pitāmahaḥ taṃ kumāraṃ saṃnivārya svayam apṛcchat tāṃ tārām | [ViPur, 4, 6 31.1]
kathaya vatse kasyāyam ātmajaḥ somasya vā bṛhaspater vā ityuktā lajjamānāha somasyeti | [ViPur, 4, 6 32.1]
tataḥ prasphuraducchvasitāmalakapolakāntir bhagavān uḍupatiḥ kumāram āliṅgya sādhu sādhu vatsa prājño 'sīti budha iti tasya ca nāma cakre | [ViPur, 4, 6 33.1]
tad ākhyātam evaitat sa ca yathelāyām ātmajaṃ purūravasam utpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 6 34.1]
purūravās tvatidānaśīlo 'tiyajvātitejasvī yaṃ satyavādinam atirūpasvinaṃ manasvinaṃ mitrāvaruṇaśāpān mānuṣe loke mayā vastavyam iti kṛtamatir urvaśī dadarśa | [ViPur, 4, 6 35.1]
dṛṣṭamātre ca tasminn apahāya mānam aśeṣam apāsya svargasukhābhilāṣaṃ tanmanaskā bhūtvā tam evopatasthe | [ViPur, 4, 6 36.1]
so 'pi ca tām atiśayitasakalalokastrīkāntisaukumāryalāvaṇyagativilāsahāsādiguṇām avalokya tadāyattacittavṛttir babhūva | [ViPur, 4, 6 37.1]
ubhayam api tanmanaskam ananyadṛṣṭi parityaktasamastānyaprayojanam abhūt | [ViPur, 4, 6 38.1]
rājā tu prāgalbhyāt tām āha | [ViPur, 4, 6 39.1]
subhru tvām aham abhikāmo 'smi prasīdānurāgam udvahetyuktā lajjāvakhaṇḍitam urvaśī taṃ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 6 40.1]
bhavatvevaṃ yadi me samayaparipālanaṃ bhavān karotītyākhyāte punar api tām āha | [ViPur, 4, 6 41.1]
ākhyāhi me samayam iti | [ViPur, 4, 6 42.1]
atha pṛṣṭā punar apyabravīt | [ViPur, 4, 6 43.1]
śayanasamīpe mamoraṇakadvayaṃ putrabhūtaṃ nāpaneyam | [ViPur, 4, 6 44.1]
bhavāṃś ca mayā na nagno draṣṭavyaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 45.1]
ghṛtamātraṃ ca mamāhāra iti | [ViPur, 4, 6 46.1]
evam eveti bhūpatir apyāha | [ViPur, 4, 6 47.1]
tayā saha sa cāvanipatir alakāyāṃ caitrarathādivaneṣvamalapadmakhaṇḍeṣu mānasādisaraḥsvatiramaṇīyeṣu ramamāṇa ekaṣaṣṭivarṣāṇyanudinapravardhamānapramodo 'nayat | [ViPur, 4, 6 48.1]
urvaśī ca tadupabhogāt pratidinapravardhamānānurāgā amaralokavāse 'pi na spṛhāṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 6 49.1]
vinā corvaśyā suraloko 'psarasāṃ siddhagandharvāṇāṃ ca nātiramaṇīyo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 6 50.1]
tataścorvaśīpurūravasoḥ samayavid viśvāvasur gandharvasamaveto niśi śayanābhyāśād ekam uraṇakaṃ jahāra | [ViPur, 4, 6 51.1]
tasyākāśe nīyamānasyorvaśī śabdam aśṛṇot | [ViPur, 4, 6 52.1]
evam uvāca ca mamānāthāyāḥ putraḥ kenāpahriyate kaṃ śaraṇam upayāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 6 53.1]
tad ākarṇya rājā māṃ nagnaṃ devī vīkṣyatīti na yayau | [ViPur, 4, 6 54.1]
athānyam apyuraṇakam ādāya gandharvā yayuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 55.1]
tasyāpyapahriyamāṇasyākarṇya śabdam ākāśe punar apy anāthāsmy aham abhartṛkā kāpuruṣāśrayety ārtarāviṇī babhūva | [ViPur, 4, 6 56.1]
rājāpyamarṣavaśād andhakāram etad iti khaḍgam ādāya duṣṭa duṣṭa hato 'sīti vyāharann abhyadhāvat | [ViPur, 4, 6 57.1]
tāvac ca gandharvair apyatīvojjvalā vidyuj janitā | [ViPur, 4, 6 58.1]
tatprabhayā corvaśī rājānam apagatāmbaraṃ dṛṣṭvāpavṛttasamayā tatkṣaṇād evāpakrāntā | [ViPur, 4, 6 59.1]
parityajya tāvapyuraṇakau gandharvāḥ suralokam upagatāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 60.1]
rājāpi ca tau meṣāvādāyātihṛṣṭamanāḥ svaśayanam āyāto norvaśīṃ dadarśa | [ViPur, 4, 6 61.1]
tāṃ cāpaśyan vyapagatāmbara evonmattarūpo babhrāma | [ViPur, 4, 6 62.1]
kurukṣetre cāmbhojasarasyanyābhiś catasṛbhir apsarobhiḥ samavetām urvaśīṃ dadarśa | [ViPur, 4, 6 63.1]
tataś conmattarūpo jāye he tiṣṭha manasi dhīre tiṣṭha vacasi kapaṭike tiṣṭhetyevam anekaprakāraṃ sūktam avocat | [ViPur, 4, 6 64.1]
āha corvaśī | [ViPur, 4, 6 65.1]
mahārājālam anenāvivekaceṣṭitena | [ViPur, 4, 6 66.1]
antarvatnyaham abdānte bhavatātrāgantavyaṃ kumāras te bhaviṣyati ekāṃ ca niśām ahaṃ tvayā saha vatsyāmīty uktaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ svapuraṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 6 67.1]
tāsāṃ cāpsarasām ūrvaśī kathayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 6 68.1]
ayaṃ sa puruṣotkṛṣṭo yenāham etāvantaṃ kālam anurāgākṛṣṭamānasā sahoṣiteti | [ViPur, 4, 6 69.1]
evam uktās tāś cāpsarasa ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 70.1]
sādhu sādhvasya rūpam apyanena sahāsmākam api sarvakālam āsyā bhaved iti | [ViPur, 4, 6 71.1]
abde ca pūrṇe sa rājā tatrājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 6 72.1]
kumāraṃ cāyuṣam asmai corvaśī dadau | [ViPur, 4, 6 73.1]
dattvā caikāṃ niśāṃ tena rājñā sahoṣitvā pañcaputrotpattaye garbham avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 6 74.1]
uvāca cainaṃ rājānam asmatprītyā mahārājāya sarva eva gandharvā varadāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ vriyatāṃ ca vara iti | [ViPur, 4, 6 75.1]
āha ca rājā | [ViPur, 4, 6 76.1]
vijitasakalārātir avihatendriyasāmarthyo bandhumān amitabalakośo 'smi nānyad asmākam urvaśīsālokyāt prāptavyam asti tad aham anayā sahorvaśyā kālaṃ netum abhilaṣāmītyukte gandharvā rājñe 'gnisthālīṃ daduḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 77.1]
ūcuś cainam agnim āmnāyānusārī bhūtvā tridhā kṛtvorvaśīsalokatāmanoratham uddiśya samyag yajethāḥ tato 'vaśyam abhilaṣitam avāpsyatītyuktas tām agnisthālīm ādāya jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 6 78.1]
antar aṭavyām acintayat aho me 'tīva mūḍhatā kim aham akaravam | [ViPur, 4, 6 79.1]
vahnisthālī mayaiṣānītā norvaśīti | [ViPur, 4, 6 80.1]
athainām aṭavyām evāgnisthālīṃ tatyāja svapuraṃ ca jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 6 81.1]
vyatīte 'rdharātre vinidraś cācintayat | [ViPur, 4, 6 82.1]
mamorvaśīsālokyaprāptyartham agnisthālī gandharvair dattā sā ca mayāṭavyāṃ parityaktā | [ViPur, 4, 6 83.1]
tad ahaṃ tatra tadāharaṇāya yāsyāmītyutthāya tatrāpyupagato nāgnisthālīm apaśyat | [ViPur, 4, 6 84.1]
śamīgarbhaṃ cāśvattham agnisthālīsthāne dṛṣṭvācintayat | [ViPur, 4, 6 85.1]
mayātrāgnisthālī nikṣiptā sā cāśvatthaḥ śamīgarbho 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 6 86.1]
tad enam evāham agnirūpam ādāya svapuram abhigamyāraṇīṃ kṛtvā tadutpannāgner upāstiṃ kariṣyāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 6 87.1]
evam eva svapuram abhigamyāraṇiṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 6 88.1]
tatpramāṇaṃ cāṅgulaiḥ kurvan gāyatrīm apaṭhat | [ViPur, 4, 6 89.1]
paṭhataś cākṣarasaṃkhyānyevāṅgulānyaraṇyabhavat | [ViPur, 4, 6 90.1]
tatrāgniṃ nirmathyāgnitrayam āmnāyānusārī bhūtvā juhāva | [ViPur, 4, 6 91.1]
urvaśīsālokyaṃ phalam abhisaṃdhitavān | [ViPur, 4, 6 92.1]
tenaiva cāgnividhinā bahuvidhān yajñān iṣṭvā gāndharvalokān avāpyorvaśyā sahāviyogam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 6 93.1]
eko 'gnir ādāvabhavat ekena tvatra manvantare tredhā pravartitāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 6 94.1]
{ViPur, 4, 7}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 7 1.1]
tasyāpyāyur dhīmān amāvasur viśvāvasuḥ śrutāyuḥ śatāyur ayutāyur itisaṃjñāḥ ṣaṭ putrā abhavan | [ViPur, 4, 7 1.2]
tathāmāvasor bhīmanāmā putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 7 2.1]
bhīmasya kāñcanaḥ kāñcanāt suhotraḥ tasyāpi jahnuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 7 3.1]
yo 'sau yajñavāṭam akhilaṃ gaṅgāmbhasā plāvitam avalokya krodhasaṃraktalocano bhagavantaṃ yajñapuruṣam ātmani parameṇa samādhinā samāropyākhilam eva gaṅgām apibat | [ViPur, 4, 7 4.1]
athainaṃ devarṣayaḥ prasādayāmāsuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 7 5.1]
duhitṛtve cāsya gaṅgām anayan | [ViPur, 4, 7 6.1]
jahnoś ca sumantur nāma putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 7 7.1]
tasyāpy ajakas tato balākāśvas tasmāt kuśas tasyāpi kuśāmbukuśanābhādhūrtarajaso vasuś ceti catvāraḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 7 8.1]
teṣāṃ kuśāmbaḥ śakratulyo me putro bhaved iti tapaś cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 7 9.1]
taṃ cogratapasam avalokya mā bhavatv anyo 'smattulyo vīrya ity ātmanaivāsyendraḥ putratvam agacchat | [ViPur, 4, 7 10.1]
sa gādhir nāma putraḥ kauśiko 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 7 11.1]
gādhiś ca satyavatīṃ kanyām ajanayat | [ViPur, 4, 7 12.1]
tāṃ ca bhārgavaḥ ṛcīko vavre | [ViPur, 4, 7 13.1]
gādhir apy atiroṣaṇāyātivṛddhāya brāhmaṇāya dātum anicchann ekataḥ śyāmakarṇānām induvarcasām anilaraṃhasām aśvānāṃ sahasraṃ kanyāśulkam ayācata | [ViPur, 4, 7 14.1]
tenāpyṛṣiṇā varuṇasakāśād upalabhyāśvatīrthotpannaṃ tādṛśam aśvasahasraṃ dattam | [ViPur, 4, 7 15.1]
tatas tām ṛcīkaḥ kanyām upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 7 16.1]
ṛcīkaś ca tasyāś carum apatyārthaṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 7 17.1]
tatprasāditaś ca tanmātre kṣatravaraputrotpattaye carum aparaṃ sādhayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 7 18.1]
eṣa carur bhavatyā ayam aparaś carus tvanmātrā samyag upayojya ity uktvā vanaṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 7 19.1]
upayogakāle ca tāṃ mātā satyavatīm āha | [ViPur, 4, 7 20.1]
putri sarva evātmaputram atiguṇam abhilaṣati nātmajāyābhrātṛguṇeṣv atīvādṛto bhavatīti | [ViPur, 4, 7 21.1]
ato 'rhasi mamātmīyaṃ caruṃ dātuṃ madīyaṃ carum ātmanopayoktum | [ViPur, 4, 7 22.1]
matputreṇa hi sakalabhūmaṇḍalaparipālanaṃ kāryaṃ kiyad vā brāhmaṇasya balavīryasaṃpadety uktā sā svacaruṃ mātre dattavatī | [ViPur, 4, 7 23.1]
atha vanād āgatya satyavatīm ṛṣir apaśyat | [ViPur, 4, 7 24.1]
āha cainām atipāpe kim idam akāryaṃ bhavatyā kṛtam atiraudraṃ te vapur lakṣyate | [ViPur, 4, 7 25.1]
nūnaṃ tvayā tvanmātṛsātkṛtaś carur upayukto na yuktam etat | [ViPur, 4, 7 26.1]
mayā hi tatra carau sakalaiśvaryavīryaśauryabalasaṃpad āropitā tvadīyacarāvapy akhilaśāntijñānatitikṣādibrāhmaṇaguṇasaṃpat | [ViPur, 4, 7 27.1]
tacca viparītaṃ kurvantyās tavātiraudrāstradhāraṇapālananiṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyācāraḥ putro bhaviṣyati tasyāś copaśamarucir brāhmaṇācāra ity ākarṇyaiva sā tasya pādau jagrāha | [ViPur, 4, 7 28.1]
praṇipatya cainam āha | [ViPur, 4, 7 29.1]
bhagavan mayaitad ajñānād anuṣṭhitaṃ prasādaṃ me kuru maivaṃvidhaḥ putro bhavatu kāmam evaṃvidhaḥ pautro bhavatv ity ukte munir apy āha | [ViPur, 4, 7 30.1]
evam astv iti | [ViPur, 4, 7 31.1]
anantaraṃ ca sā jamadagnim ajījanat | [ViPur, 4, 7 32.1]
tanmātā ca viśvāmitraṃ janayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 7 33.1]
satyavaty api kauśikī nāma nady abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 7 34.1]
jamadagnir ikṣvākuvaṃśodbhavasya reṇos tanayāṃ reṇukām upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 7 35.1]
tasyāṃ cāśeṣakṣatrahantāraṃ paraśurāmasaṃjñaṃ bhagavataḥ sakalalokaguror nārāyaṇasyāṃśaṃ jamadagnir ajījanat | [ViPur, 4, 7 36.1]
viśvāmitraputras tu bhārgava eva śunaḥśepo devair dattaḥ tataś ca devarātanāmābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 7 37.1]
tataś cānye madhuśchandodhanañjayakṛtadevāṣṭakakacchapaharirākhyā viśvāmitraputrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 7 38.1]
teṣāṃ ca bahūni kauśikagotrāṇi ṛṣyantareṣu vivāhyany abhavan | [ViPur, 4, 7 39.1]
{ViPur, 4, 8}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 8 1.1]
purūravaso jyeṣṭhaḥ putro yas tvāyurnāmā sa rāhor duhitaram upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 8 1.2]
tasyāṃ ca pañca putrān utpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 8 2.1]
nahuṣakṣatravṛddharambharajisaṃjñās tathaivānenāḥ pañcamaḥ putro 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 8 3.1]
kṣatravṛddhāt suhotraḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 8 4.1]
kāśyapakāśagṛtsamadās trayas tasya putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 8 5.1]
gṛtsamadasya śaunakaś cāturvarṇyapravartayitābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 8 6.1]
kāśyasya kāśeyaḥ kāśīrājaḥ tasmād rāṣṭraḥ rāṣṭrasya dīrghatapāḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 8 7.1]
dhanvantaris tu dīrghatapasaḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 8 8.1]
sa hi saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇaḥ sakalasaṃbhūtiṣv aśeṣajñānavidā bhagavatā nārāyaṇena cātītasaṃbhūtau tasmai varo dattaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 8 9.1]
kāśīrājagotre 'vatīrya tvam aṣṭadhā samyag āyurvedaṃ kariṣyasi yajñabhāgabhug bhaviṣyasīti | [ViPur, 4, 8 10.1]
tasya ca dhanvantareḥ putraḥ ketumān ketumato bhīmarathaḥ tasyāpi divodāsaḥ tasyāpi pratardanaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 8 11.1]
sa ca bhadraśreṇyavaṃśavināśanād aśeṣaśatravo 'nena jitā iti śatrujid abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 8 12.1]
tena ca prītimatātmaputro vatsa vatsetyabhihito vatso 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 8 13.1]
satyaparatayā ṛtadhvajasaṃjñām avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 8 14.1]
tataś ca kuvalayanāmānam aśvaṃ lebhe tataḥ kuvalayāśva ity asyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ prathitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 8 15.1]
tasya ca vatsasya putro 'larkanāmābhavat yasyāyam adyāpi śloko gīyate | [ViPur, 4, 8 16]
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭivarṣaśatāni ca | [ViPur, 4, 8 17.1]
alarkādaparo nānyo bubhuje medinīṃ yuvā | [ViPur, 4, 8 17.2]
tasyāpy alarkasya sannatināmābhavad ātmajaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 8 18.1]
sannateḥ sunīthaḥ tasyāpi suketuḥ tasmāc ca dharmaketur jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 8 19.1]
tataś ca satyaketuḥ tasmād vibhuḥ tattanayaḥ suvibhuḥ tataś ca sukumāras tasyāpi dṛṣṭaketuḥ tataś ca vītihotraḥ tasmād bhārgaḥ bhārgasya bhārgabhūmiḥ tataś cāturvarṇyapravṛttir ityete kāśyapabhūbhṛtaḥ kathitāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 8 20.1]
rajes tu saṃtatiḥ śrūyatām | [ViPur, 4, 8 21.1]
{ViPur, 4, 9}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 9 1.1]
rajes tu pañca putraśatānyatulabalaparākramasārāṇyāsan | [ViPur, 4, 9 1.2]
devāsurasaṃgrāmārambhe ca parasparavadhepsavo devāś cāsurāś ca brahmāṇam upetya papracchuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 2.1]
bhagavann asmākam atra virodhe katamaḥ pakṣo jetā bhaviṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 9 3.1]
athāha bhagavān | [ViPur, 4, 9 4.1]
yeṣām arthe rajir ātmāttāyudho yotsyati tatpakṣo jeteti | [ViPur, 4, 9 5.1]
atha daityair upetya rajir ātmasāhāyyadānāyābhyarthitaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 9 6.1]
yotsye 'haṃ bhavatām arthe yady aham amarajayād bhavatām indro bhaviṣyāmīty ākarṇyaitat tair abhihitam | [ViPur, 4, 9 7.1]
na vayam anyathā vadiṣyāmo 'nyathā kariṣyāmo 'smākam indraḥ prahlādas tadartham evāyam udyama ity uktvā gateṣv asureṣu devair apy asāv avanipatir evam evoktas tenāpi ca tathaivokte devair indras tvaṃ bhaviṣyasīti samanvicchitam | [ViPur, 4, 9 8.1]
rajināpi devasainyasahāyenānekair mahāstrais tad aśeṣamahāsurabalaṃ niṣūditam | [ViPur, 4, 9 9.1]
atha jitāripakṣaś ca devendro rajicaraṇayugalam ātmanaḥ śirasā nipīḍyāha | [ViPur, 4, 9 10.1]
bhayatrāṇād annadānād bhavān asmatpitāśeṣalokānām uttamottamo bhavān yasyāhaṃ putras trilokendraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 11.1]
sa cāpi rājā prahasyāha | [ViPur, 4, 9 12.1]
evam astv evam astv anatikramaṇīyā hi vairipakṣād apy anekavidhacāṭuvākyagarbhā praṇatir ity uktvā svapuraṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 9 13.1]
śatakratur apīndratvaṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 9 14.1]
svaryāte tu rajau nāradarṣicoditā rajiputrāḥ śatakratum ātmapitṛputraṃ samācārād rājyaṃ yācitavantaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 15.1]
apradānena ca vijityendram atibalinaḥ svayam indratvaṃ cakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 16.1]
tataś ca bahutithe kāle hy atīte bṛhaspatim ekānte dṛṣṭvā apahṛtatrailokyayajñabhāgaḥ śatakratur uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 9 17.1]
badarīphalamātram apy arhasi mamāpyāyanāya puroḍāśakhaṇḍaṃ dātum ity ukto bṛhaspatir uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 9 18.1]
yady evaṃ tvayāhaṃ pūrvam eva coditaḥ syāṃ tan mayā tvadarthaṃ kim akartavyam ity alpair evāhobhis tvāṃ nijaṃ padaṃ prāpayiṣyāmīty abhidhāya teṣām anudinam abhicārakaṃ buddhimohāya śakrasya tejo'bhivṛddhaye juhāva | [ViPur, 4, 9 19.1]
te cāpi tena buddhimohenābhibhūyamānā brahmadviṣo dharmatyāgino vedavādaparāṅmukhā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 20.1]
tatas tān apetadharmācārān indro jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 9 21.1]
purohitāpyāyitatejāś ca śakro divam ākramat | [ViPur, 4, 9 22.1]
etad indrasya svapadacyavanād ārohaṇaṃ śrutvā puruṣaḥ svapadabhraṃśaṃ daurātmyaṃ ca nāpnoti | [ViPur, 4, 9 23.1]
rambhas tv anapatyo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 9 24.1]
kṣatravṛddhasutaḥ pratikṣatro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 9 25.1]
tatputraḥ sañjayaḥ tasyāpi jayaḥ tasyāpi vijayaḥ tasmāc ca jajñe kṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 26.1]
tasya ca haryadhanaḥ haryadhanasutaḥ sahadevaḥ tasmād adīnas tasya jayatsenaḥ tataś ca saṃkṛtiḥ tatputraḥ kṣatradharmā ity ete kṣatravṛddhasya vaṃśyāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 9 27.1]
tato nahuṣavaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmi | [ViPur, 4, 9 28.1]
{ViPur, 4, 10}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 10 1.1]
yatiyayātisaṃyātyāyātiviyātikṛtisaṃjñā nahuṣasya ṣaṭ putrā mahābalaparākramā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 1.2]
yatis tu rājyaṃ naicchat | [ViPur, 4, 10 2.1]
yayātis tu bhūbhṛd abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 10 3.1]
uśanasaś ca duhitaraṃ devayānīṃ vārṣaparvaṇīṃ ca śarmiṣṭhām upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 10 4.1]
atrānuvaṃśaśloko bhavati | [ViPur, 4, 10 5.1]
yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānī vyajāyata | [ViPur, 4, 10 6.1]
druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī | [ViPur, 4, 10 6.2]
kāvyaśāpāccākālenaiva yayātir jarām avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 10 7.1]
prasannaśukravacanāc ca svajarāṃ saṃkrāmayituṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ yadum uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 10 8.1]
vatsa tvanmātāmahaśāpād iyam akālenaiva jarā mamopasthitā tām ahaṃ tasyaivānugrahād bhavataḥ saṃcārayāmi | [ViPur, 4, 10 9.1]
ekaṃ varṣasahasram atṛpto 'smi viṣayeṣu tvadvayasā viṣayān ahaṃ bhoktum icchāmi | [ViPur, 4, 10 10.1]
nātra bhavatā pratyākhyānaṃ kartavyam ity uktaḥ sa yadur naicchat tāṃ jarām ādātum | [ViPur, 4, 10 11.1]
taṃ ca pitā śaśāpa tvatprasūtir na rājyārhā bhaviṣyatīti | [ViPur, 4, 10 12.1]
anantaraṃ ca durvasuṃ druhyum anuṃ ca pṛthivīpatir jarāgrahaṇārthaṃ svayauvanapradānāya cābhyarthayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 10 13.1]
tair apy ekaikena pratyākhyātas tāñchaśāpa | [ViPur, 4, 10 14.1]
atha śarmiṣṭhātanayam aśeṣakanīyāṃsaṃ pūruṃ tathaivāha | [ViPur, 4, 10 15.1]
sa cātipravaṇamatiḥ sabahumānaṃ pitaraṃ praṇamya mahāprasādo 'yam asmākam ity udāram abhidhāya jarāṃ jagrāha | [ViPur, 4, 10 16.1]
svakīyaṃ ca yauvanaṃ svapitre dadau | [ViPur, 4, 10 17.1]
so 'pi pauravaṃ yauvanam āsādya dharmāvirodhena yathākāmaṃ yathākālopapannaṃ yathotsāhaṃ viṣayāṃś cacāra | [ViPur, 4, 10 18.1]
samyak ca prajāpālanam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 10 19.1]
viśvācyā devayānyā ca sahopabhogaṃ bhuktvā kāmānām antaṃ prāpsyāmīty anudinaṃ tanmanasko babhūva | [ViPur, 4, 10 20.1]
anudinaṃ copabhogataḥ kāmān atiramyān mene | [ViPur, 4, 10 21.1]
tataś cainam agāyata | [ViPur, 4, 10 22.1]
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati | [ViPur, 4, 10 23.1]
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate | [ViPur, 4, 10 23.2]
yat pṛthivyāṃ vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ paśavaḥ striyaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 24.1]
ekasyāpi na paryāptaṃ tasmāt tṛṣṇāṃ parityajet | [ViPur, 4, 10 24.2]
yadā na kurute bhāvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam | [ViPur, 4, 10 25.1]
samadṛṣṭes tadā puṃsaḥ sarvāḥ sukhamayā diśaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 25.2]
yā dustyajā durmatibhir yā na jīryati jīryataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 26.1]
tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ saṃtyajet prājñaḥ sukhenaivābhipūryate | [ViPur, 4, 10 26.2]
jīryanti jīryataḥ keśā dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 27.1]
dhanāśā jīvitāśā ca jīryato 'pi na jīryataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 27.2]
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ me viṣayāsaktacetasaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 10 28.1]
tathāpy anudinaṃ tṛṣṇā mamaiteṣv eva jāyate | [ViPur, 4, 10 28.2]
tasmād etām ahaṃ tyaktvā brahmaṇy ādhāya mānasam | [ViPur, 4, 10 29.1]
nirdvandvo nirmamo bhūtvā cariṣyāmi mṛgaiḥ saha | [ViPur, 4, 10 29.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 10 30.1]
pūroḥ sakāśād ādāya jarāṃ dattvā ca yauvanam | [ViPur, 4, 10 30.2]
rājye 'bhiṣicya pūruṃ ca prayayau tapase vanam | [ViPur, 4, 10 30.3]
diśi dakṣiṇapūrvāyāṃ turvasuṃ praty athādiśat | [ViPur, 4, 10 31.1]
pratīcyāṃ ca tathā druhyuṃ dakṣiṇāyāṃ tato yadum | [ViPur, 4, 10 31.2]
udīcyāṃ ca tathaivānuṃ kṛtvā maṇḍalino nṛpān | [ViPur, 4, 10 32.1]
sarvapṛthvīpatiṃ pūruṃ so 'bhiṣicya yayau vanam | [ViPur, 4, 10 32.2]
{ViPur, 4, 11}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 11 1.1]
ataḥ paraṃ yayāteḥ prathamaputrasya yador vaṃśam ahaṃ kathayāmi | [ViPur, 4, 11 1.2]
yatrāśeṣalokanivāso manuṣyasiddhagandharvayakṣarākṣasaguhyakakiṃpuruṣāpsaroragavihagadaityadānavādityarudravasvaśvimaruddevarṣibhir mumukṣibhir dharmārthakāmamokṣārthibhiś ca tattatphalalābhāya sadābhiṣṭuto 'paricchedyamāhātmyāṃśena bhagavān anādinidhano viṣṇur avatatāra | [ViPur, 4, 11 2]
atra ślokaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 3.1]
yador vaṃśaṃ naraḥ śrutvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate | [ViPur, 4, 11 4.1]
yatrāvatīrṇaṃ viṣṇvākhyaṃ paraṃ brahma nirākṛti | [ViPur, 4, 11 4.2]
sahasrajitkroṣṭunalanahuṣasaṃjñāś catvāro yaduputrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 5.1]
sahasrajitputraḥ śatajit | [ViPur, 4, 11 6.1]
tasya haihayahehayaveṇuhayās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 7.1]
haihayaputro dharmaḥ tasyāpi dharmanetraḥ tataḥ kuntiḥ kunteḥ sahajit | [ViPur, 4, 11 8.1]
tattanayo mahiṣmān yo 'sau māhiṣmatīṃ purīṃ nirvāpayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 11 9.1]
tasmād bhadraśreṇyas tato durdamas tasmād dhanakaḥ dhanakasya kṛtavīryakṛtāgnikṛtadharmakṛtaujasaś catvāraḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 10.1]
kṛtavīryād arjunaḥ saptadvīpādhipatir bāhusahasro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 11 11.1]
yo 'sau bhagavadaṃśam atrikulaprasūtaṃ dattātreyākhyam ārādhya bāhusahasram adharmasevānivāraṇaṃ svadharmasevitvaṃ raṇe pṛthivījayaṃ dharmataś cānupālanam | [ViPur, 4, 11 12.1]
arātibhyo 'parājayam akhilajagatprakhyātapuruṣāc ca mṛtyum ity etān varān abhilaṣitavāṃllebhe ca | [ViPur, 4, 11 12.2]
teneyam aśeṣadvīpavatī pṛthivī samyak paripālitā | [ViPur, 4, 11 13.1]
daśa yajñasahasrāṇy asāv ayajat | [ViPur, 4, 11 14.1]
tasya ca śloko 'dyāpi gīyate | [ViPur, 4, 11 15.1]
na nūnaṃ kārtavīryasya gatiṃ yāsyanti pārthivāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 16.1]
yajñair dānais tapobhir vā praśrayeṇa śrutena ca | [ViPur, 4, 11 16.2]
anaṣṭadravyatā ca tasya rājye 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 11 17.1]
evaṃ ca pañcāśītivarṣasahasrāṇy avyāhatārogyaśrībalaparākramo rājyam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 11 18.1]
māhiṣmatyāṃ digvijayābhyāgato narmadājalāvagāhanakrīḍātipānamadākulenāyatnenaiva tenāśeṣadevadaityagandharveśajayodbhūtamadāvalepo 'pi rāvaṇaḥ paśur iva baddhvā svanagaraikānte sthāpitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 19.1]
yaś ca pañcāśītivarṣasahasropalakṣaṇakālāvasāne bhagavannārāyaṇāṃśena paraśurāmeṇopasaṃhṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 20.1]
tasya ca putraśatapradhānāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ śūraśūrasenavṛṣasenamadhujayadhvajasaṃjñāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 21.1]
jayadhvajāt tālajaṅghaḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 11 22.1]
tālajaṅghasya tālajaṅghākhyaṃ putraśatam āsīt | [ViPur, 4, 11 23.1]
eṣāṃ jyeṣṭho vītihotras tathānyo bharataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 24.1]
bharatād vṛṣaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 11 25.1]
vṛṣasya putro madhur abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 11 26.1]
tasyāpi vṛṣṇipramukhaṃ putraśatam āsīt | [ViPur, 4, 11 27.1]
yato vṛṣṇisaṃjñām etad gotram avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 11 28.1]
madhusaṃjñāhetuś ca madhur abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 11 29.1]
yādavāś ca yadunāmopalakṣaṇād iti | [ViPur, 4, 11 30.1]

parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 12 1.1]
kroṣṭos tu yaduputrasyātmajo dhvajinīvān | [ViPur, 4, 12 1.2]
tataś ca svātiḥ tato ruśaṅkuḥ ruśaṅkoś citrarathaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 2.1]
tattanayaḥ śaśibinduḥ caturdaśamahāratneśaś cakravarty abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 12 3.1]
tasya ca śatasahasraṃ patnīnām abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 12 4.1]
daśalakṣasaṃkhyāś ca putrāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 5.1]
teṣāṃ ca pṛthuśravāḥ pṛthukarmā pṛthukīrtiḥ pṛthuyaśāḥ pṛthujayaḥ pṛthudānaḥ ṣaṭ putrāḥ pradhānāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 6.1]
pṛthuśravasaś ca putraḥ pṛthutamaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 7.1]
tasmād uśanā yo vājimedhānāṃ śatam ājahāra | [ViPur, 4, 12 8.1]
tasya ca śitapur nāma putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 12 9.1]
tasyāpi rukmakavacas tataḥ parāvṛt | [ViPur, 4, 12 10.1]
tasya parāvṛto rukmeṣupṛthujyāmaghavalitaharitasaṃjñās tasya pañcātmajā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 11.1]
tasyāyam adyāpi jyāmaghasya śloko gīyate | [ViPur, 4, 12 12.1]
bhāryāvaśyās tu ye kecid bhaviṣyanty athavā mṛtāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 13.1]
teṣāṃ tu jyāmaghaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ śaibyāpatir abhūn nṛpaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 13.2]
aputrā tasya sā patnī śaibyā nāma tathāpy asau | [ViPur, 4, 12 14.1]
apatyakāmo 'pi bhayān nānyāṃ bhāryām avindata | [ViPur, 4, 12 14.2]
sa tvekadā prabhūtarathaturagagajasaṃmardātidāruṇe mahāhave yudhyamānaḥ sakalam evāricakram ajayat | [ViPur, 4, 12 15.1]
taccāricakram apāstaputrakalatrabandhubalakośaṃ svam adhiṣṭhānaṃ parityajya diśaḥ pratividrutam | [ViPur, 4, 12 16.1]
tasmiṃśca vidrute 'titrāsalolāyatalocanayugalaṃ trāhi trāhi māṃ tātāmba bhrātar ity ākulavilāpavidhuraṃ sa rājakanyāratnam adrākṣīt | [ViPur, 4, 12 17.1]
taddarśanāc ca tasyām anurāgānugatāntarātmā sa nṛpo 'cintayat | [ViPur, 4, 12 18.1]
sādhv idaṃ mamāpatyarahitasya vandhyābhartuḥ sāmprataṃ vidhināpatyakāraṇaṃ kanyāratnam upapāditam | [ViPur, 4, 12 19.1]
tad etat samudvahāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 12 20.1]
athavaināṃ syandanam āropya svam adhiṣṭhānaṃ nayāmi | [ViPur, 4, 12 21.1]
tayaiva devyā śaibyayāham anujñātaḥ samudvahāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 12 22.1]
athaināṃ ratham āropya svanagaram agacchat | [ViPur, 4, 12 23.1]
vijayinaṃ ca rājānam aśeṣapaurabhṛtyaparijanāmātyasametā śaibyā draṣṭum adhiṣṭhānadvāram āgatā | [ViPur, 4, 12 24.1]
sā cāvalokya rājñaḥ savyapārśvavartinīṃ kanyām īṣadudbhūtāmarṣasphuradadharapallavā rājānam avocat | [ViPur, 4, 12 25.1]
aticapalacittātra syandane keyam āropiteti | [ViPur, 4, 12 26.1]
asāvapyanālocitottaravacano 'tibhayāt tām āha snuṣā mameyam iti | [ViPur, 4, 12 27.1]
athainaṃ śaibyovāca | [ViPur, 4, 12 28.1]
nāhaṃ prasūtā putreṇa nānyā patnyabhavat tava | [ViPur, 4, 12 29.1]
snuṣāsaṃbandhatā hy eṣā katamena sutena te | [ViPur, 4, 12 29.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 12 30.1]
ity ātmerṣyākopakaluṣitavacanamuṣitaviveko bhayād duruktaparihārārtham idam avanīpatir āha | [ViPur, 4, 12 30.2]
yas te janiṣyaty ātmajas tasyeyam anāgatasyaiva bhāryā nirūpitety ākarṇyodbhūtamṛduhāsā tathety āha | [ViPur, 4, 12 31.1]
praviveśa ca rājñā sahādhiṣṭhānam | [ViPur, 4, 12 32.1]
anantaraṃ cātiśuddhalagnahorāṃśakāvayavoktakṛtaputrajanmalābhaguṇād vayasaḥ pariṇāmam upagatāpi śaibyā svalpair evāhobhir garbham avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 12 33.1]
kālena ca kumāram ajījanat | [ViPur, 4, 12 34.1]
tasya ca vidarbha iti pitā nāma cakre | [ViPur, 4, 12 35.1]
sa ca tāṃ snuṣām upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 12 36.1]
tasyāṃ cāsau krathakaiśikasaṃjñau putrāv ajanayat | [ViPur, 4, 12 37.1]
punaś ca tṛtīyaṃ romapādasaṃjñaṃ putram ajījanad yo nāradād avāptajñānavān bhaviṣyati iti | [ViPur, 4, 12 38.1]
romapādād babhruḥ babhror dhṛtiḥ dhṛteḥ kaiśikaḥ kaiśikasyāpi cediḥ putro 'bhavat yasya saṃtatau caidyā bhūpālāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 39.1]
krathasya snuṣāputrasya kuntir abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 12 40.1]
kunter dhṛṣṭiḥ dhṛṣṭer nidhṛtiḥ nidhṛter daśārhas tataś ca vyomaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 41.1]
tasyāpi jīmūtaḥ tataś ca vikṛtiḥ tataś ca bhīmarathaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 41.2]
tasmān navarathaḥ tasyāpi daśarathaḥ tataś ca śakuniḥ tattanayaḥ karambhiḥ karambher devarāto 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 12 41.3]
tasmād devakṣatraḥ tasyāpi madhuḥ madhoḥ kumāravaṃśaḥ kumāravaṃśād anuḥ anoḥ purumitraḥ pṛthivīpatir abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 12 42.1]
tataś cāṃśus tasmācca satvataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 43.1]
satvatād ete sātvatāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 12 44.1]
ityetāṃ jyāmaghasya saṃtatiṃ samyak śraddhāsamanvitaḥ śrutvā pumān maitreya svapāpaiḥ pramucyate | [ViPur, 4, 12 45.1]
{ViPur, 4, 13}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 13 1.1]
bhajanabhajamānadivyāndhakadevāvṛdhamahābhojavṛṣṇisaṃjñāḥ satvatasya putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 1.2]
bhajamānasya nimikṛkaṇavṛṣṇayas tathānye dvaimātrāḥ śatajitsahasrajidayutajitsaṃjñās trayaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 2.1]
devāvṛdhasyāpi babhruḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 13 3.1]
tayoś cāyaṃ śloko gīyate | [ViPur, 4, 13 4.1]
yathaiva śṛṇumo dūrāt saṃpaśyāmastathāntikāt | [ViPur, 4, 13 5.1]
babhruḥ śreṣṭho manuṣyāṇāṃ devair devāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 5.2]
puruṣāḥ ṣaṭ ca ṣaṣṭiś ca ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi cāṣṭa ca | [ViPur, 4, 13 6.1]
ye 'mṛtatvam anuprāptā babhror devāvṛdhād api | [ViPur, 4, 13 6.2]
mahābhojas tvatidharmātmā tasyānvaye bhojāḥ mṛttikāvarapuranivāsino mārtikāvarā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 7.1]
vṛṣṇeḥ sumitro yudhājicca putrāvabhūtām | [ViPur, 4, 13 8.1]
tataś cānamitraḥ tathānamitrān nighnaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 9.1]
nighnasya prasenasatrājitau | [ViPur, 4, 13 10.1]
tasya ca satrājito bhagavān ādityaḥ sakhābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 13 11.1]
ekadā tv ambhonidhitīrasaṃśrayaḥ sūryaṃ satrājit tuṣṭāva tanmanaskatayā ca bhāsvān abhiṣṭūyamāno 'gratas tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 13 12.1]
tatas tv aspaṣṭamūrtidharaṃ cainam ālokya satrājit sūryam āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 13.1]
yathaiva vyomni vahnipiṇḍopamaṃ tvām aham apaśyaṃ tathaivādyāgrato gatam apy atra bhagavatā kiṃcin na prasādīkṛtaṃ viśeṣam upalakṣayāmīty evam ukte bhagavatā sūryeṇa nijakaṇṭhād unmucya syamantakaṃ nāma mahāmaṇivaram avatāryaikānte nyastam | [ViPur, 4, 13 14.1]
tatas tam ātāmrojjvalaṃ hrasvavapuṣam īṣadāpiṅgalanayanam ādityam adrākṣīt | [ViPur, 4, 13 15.1]
kṛtapraṇipātastavādikaṃ ca satrājitam āha bhagavān ādityaḥ sahasradīdhitiḥ varam asmatto 'bhimataṃ vṛṇīṣveti | [ViPur, 4, 13 16.1]
sa ca tad eva maṇiratnam ayācata | [ViPur, 4, 13 17.1]
sa cāpi tasmai tad dattvā dīdhitipatir viyati svadhiṣṇyam āruroha | [ViPur, 4, 13 18.1]
satrājito 'py amalamaṇiratnasanāthakaṇṭhatayā sūrya iva tejobhir aśeṣadigantarāṇy udbhāsayan dvārakāṃ viveśa | [ViPur, 4, 13 19.1]
dvārakāvāsī janas tu tam āyāntam avekṣya bhagavantam ādipuruṣaṃ puruṣottamam avanibhārāvataraṇāyāṃśena mānuṣarūpadhāriṇaṃ praṇipatyāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 20.1]
bhagavan bhavantaṃ draṣṭuṃ nūnam ayam āditya āyātīty ukto bhagavān uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 13 21.1]
bhagavān nāyam ādityaḥ satrājito yam ādityadattasyamantakākhyaṃ mahāmaṇiratnaṃ bibhrad atropayāti | [ViPur, 4, 13 22.1]
tad enaṃ visrabdhāḥ paśyatety uktās te tathā eva dadṛśuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 23.1]
sa ca taṃ syamantakamaṇim ātmaniveśane cakre | [ViPur, 4, 13 24.1]
pratidinaṃ tan maṇiratnam aṣṭau kanakabhārān sravati | [ViPur, 4, 13 25.1]
tatprabhāvāc ca sakalasyaiva rāṣṭrasyopasargānāvṛṣṭivyālāgnito yad durbhikṣādibhayaṃ na bhavati | [ViPur, 4, 13 26.1]
acyuto 'pi tad divyaṃ ratnam ugrasenasya bhūpater yogyam etad iti lipsāṃ cakre | [ViPur, 4, 13 27.1]
gotrabhedabhayācchakto 'pi na jahāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 28.1]
satrājid apy acyuto mām etad yācayiṣyatīty avagamya ratnalobhād bhrātre prasenāya tad ratnam adāt | [ViPur, 4, 13 29.1]
tacca śucinā dhriyamāṇam aśeṣam eva suvarṇasravādikaṃ guṇajātam utpādayati anyathā dhārayantam eva hantīty ajānann asāvapi prasenas tena kaṇṭhasaktena syamantakenāśvam āruhyāṭavyāṃ mṛgayām agacchat | [ViPur, 4, 13 30.1]
tatra ca siṃhād vadham avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 13 31.1]
sāśvaṃ ca taṃ nihatya siṃho 'py amalamaṇiratnam āsyāgreṇādāya gantum abhyudyataḥ ṛkṣādhipatinā jāmbavatā dṛṣṭo ghātitaś ca | [ViPur, 4, 13 32.1]
jāmbavān apy amalamaṇiratnam ādāya svabilaṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 13 33.1]
sukumārasaṃjñāya bālakāya ca krīḍanakam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 13 34.1]
anāgacchati tasmin prasene kṛṣṇo maṇiratnam abhilaṣitavān sa ca prāptavān nūnam etad asya karmety akhila eva yadulokaḥ parasparaṃ karṇa ākarṇyākathayat | [ViPur, 4, 13 35.1]
viditalokāpavādavṛttāntaś ca bhagavān sarvayadusainyaparivāraparivṛtaḥ prasenāśvapadavīm anusasāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 36.1]
dadarśa cāśvasamavetaṃ prasenaṃ siṃhena vinihatam | [ViPur, 4, 13 37.1]
akhilajanamadhye siṃhapadadarśanakṛtapariśuddhiḥ siṃhapadam anusasāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 38.1]
ṛkṣapatinihataṃ ca siṃham apyalpe bhūmibhāge dṛṣṭvā tataś ca tadratnagauravād ṛkṣasyāpi padānyanuyayau | [ViPur, 4, 13 39.1]
giritaṭe ca sakalam eva tad yadusainyam avasthāpya tatpadānusārī ṛkṣabilaṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 13 40.1]
antaḥpraviṣṭaś ca dhātryāḥ sukumārakam ullālayantyā vāṇīṃ śuśrāva | [ViPur, 4, 13 41.1]
siṃhaḥ prasenam avadhīt siṃho jāmbavatā hataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 42.1]
sukumāraka mā rodīs tava hy eṣa syamantakaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 42.2]
ityākarṇyopalabdhasyamantako 'ntaḥpraviṣṭaḥ kumārakrīḍanakīkṛtaṃ ca dhātryā haste tejobhir jājvalyamānaṃ syamantakaṃ dadarśa | [ViPur, 4, 13 42.3]
taṃ ca syamantakābhilaṣitacakṣuṣam apūrvapuruṣam āgataṃ samavekṣya dhātrī trāhi trāhīti vyājahāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 43.1]
tadārtaravaśravaṇānantaraṃ cāmarṣapūrṇahṛdayaḥ sa jāmbavān ājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 13 44.1]
tayoś ca parasparam uddhatāmarṣayor yuddham ekaviṃśatidinānyabhavat | [ViPur, 4, 13 45.1]
te ca yadusainikās tatra saptāṣṭa dināni tanniṣkrāntim udīkṣamāṇās tasthuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 46.1]
aniṣkramaṇe ca madhuripur asāv avaśyam atra bile 'tyantaṃ nāśam avāpto bhaviṣyaty anyathā tasya jīvataḥ katham etāvanti dināni śatrujaye vyākṣepo bhaviṣyatīti kṛtādhyavasāyā dvārakām āgamya hataḥ kṛṣṇa iti kathayāmāsuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 47.1]
tadbāndhavāś ca tatkālocitam akhilam uttarakriyākalāpaṃ cakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 48.1]
tataś cāsya yudhyamānasyātiśraddhādattaviśiṣṭopapātrayuktānnatoyādinā śrīkṛṣṇasya balaprāṇapuṣṭir abhūt | [ViPur, 4, 13 49.1]
itarasyānudinam atigurupuruṣabhedyamānasya atiniṣṭhuraprahārapātapīḍitākhilāvayavasya nirāhāratayā balahānir abhūt | [ViPur, 4, 13 50.1]
nirjitaś ca bhagavatā jāmbavān praṇipatya vyājahāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 51.1]
surāsuragandharvayakṣarākṣasādibhir apy akhilair bhavān na jetuṃ śakyaḥ kim utāvanigocarair alpavīryair narair narāvayavabhūtaiś ca tiryagyonyanusṛtibhiḥ kiṃ punar asmadvidhair avaśyaṃ bhavatāsmatsvāminā rāmeṇeva nārāyaṇasya sakalajagatparāyaṇasyāṃśena bhagavatā bhavitavyam ity uktas tasmai bhagavān akhilāvanibhārāvataraṇārtham avataraṇam ācacakṣe | [ViPur, 4, 13 52]
prītyabhivyañjitakaratalasparśanena cainam apagatayuddhakhedaṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 53.1]
sa ca praṇipatya punar apy enaṃ prasādya jāmbavatīṃ nāma kanyāṃ gṛhāgatāyārghyabhūtāṃ grāhayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 13 54.1]
syamantakamaṇiratnam api praṇipatya tasmai pradadau | [ViPur, 4, 13 55.1]
acyuto 'py atipraṇatāt tasmād agrāhyam api tan maṇiratnam ātmasaṃśodhanāya jagrāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 56.1]
saha jāmbavatyā sa dvārakām ājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 13 57.1]
bhagavadāgamanodbhūtaharṣotkarṣasya dvārakāvāsijanasya kṛṣṇāvalokanāt tatkṣaṇam evātipariṇatavayaso 'pi navayauvanam ivābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 13 58.1]
diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti sakalayādavāḥ striyaś ca sabhājayāmāsuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 59.1]
bhagavān api yathānubhūtam aśeṣaṃ yādavasamāje yathāvad ācacakṣe | [ViPur, 4, 13 60.1]
syamantakaṃ ca satrājitāya dattvā mithyābhiśastipariśuddhim avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 13 61.1]
jāmbavatīṃ cāntaḥpure niveśayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 13 62.1]
satrājito 'pi mayāsyābhūtamalinam āropitam iti jātasaṃtrāsāt svasutāṃ satyabhāmāṃ bhagavate bhāryārthaṃ dadau | [ViPur, 4, 13 63.1]
tāṃ cākrūrakṛtavarmaśatadhanvapramukhā yādavāḥ prāg varayāṃbabhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 64.1]
tatas tatpradānād avajñātam evātmānaṃ manyamānāḥ satrājite vairānubandhaṃ cakruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 65.1]
akrūrakṛtavarmapramukhāś ca śatadhanvānam ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 66.1]
ayam atīva durātmā satrājito yo 'smābhir bhavatā ca prārthito 'py ātmajām asmān bhavantaṃ cāvigaṇayya kṛṣṇāya dattavān | [ViPur, 4, 13 67.1]
tad alam anena jīvatā ghātayitvainaṃ tan mahāratnaṃ syamantakākhyaṃ tvayā kiṃ na gṛhyate vayam abhyupapatsyāmo yady acyutas tavopari vairānubandhaṃ kariṣyatīty evam uktas tathety asāvapyāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 68]
jatugṛhadagdhānāṃ pāṇḍutanayānāṃ viditaparamārtho 'pi bhagavān duryodhanaprayatnaśaithilyakaraṇārthaṃ pārthānukūlyakaraṇāya vāraṇāvataṃ gataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 69.1]
gate ca tasmin suptam eva satrājitaṃ śatadhanvā jaghāna maṇiratnaṃ cādadāt | [ViPur, 4, 13 70.1]
pitṛvadhāmarṣapūrṇā ca satyabhāmā śīghraṃ syandanam ārūḍhā vāraṇāvataṃ gatvā bhagavate 'haṃ pratipāditety akṣāntimatā śatadhanvanāsmatpitā vyāpāditaḥ tacca syamantakamaṇiratnam apahṛtaṃ yasyāvabhāsanenāpahṛtatimiraṃ trailokyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 13 71.1]
tad iyaṃ tvadīyāpahāsanā tad ālocya yad atra yuktaṃ tat kriyatām iti kṛṣṇam āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 72.1]
tayā caivam uktaḥ parituṣṭāntaḥkaraṇo 'pi kṛṣṇaḥ satyabhāmām amarṣatāmranayanaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 73.1]
satye satyaṃ mamaivaiṣāpahāsanā nāham etāṃ tasya durātmanaḥ sahiṣye | [ViPur, 4, 13 74.1]
na hyanullaṅghya parapādapaṃ tatkṛtanīḍāśrayiṇo vihaṃgamā vadhyante | [ViPur, 4, 13 75.1]
tad alam amunāsmatpurataḥ śokapreritavākyaparikareṇety uktvā dvārakām abhyetyaikānte baladevaṃ vāsudevaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 75.2]
mṛgayāgataṃ prasenam aṭavyāṃ mṛgapatir jaghāna | [ViPur, 4, 13 76.1]
satrājito 'py adhunā śatadhanvanā nidhanaṃ prāpitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 77.1]
tadubhayavināśāttanmaṇiratnam āvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 13 78.1]
tad uttiṣṭhāruhyatāṃ rathaḥ śatadhanvanidhanāyodyamaṃ kurvityabhihitas tatheti samanvicchitavān | [ViPur, 4, 13 79.1]
kṛtodyamau ca tāvubhāvupalabhya śatadhanvā kṛtavarmāṇam upetya pārṣṇipūraṇakarmanimittam acodayat | [ViPur, 4, 13 80.1]
āha cainaṃ kṛtavarmā | [ViPur, 4, 13 81.1]
nāhaṃ baladevavāsudevābhyāṃ saha virodhāyālam ityuktaścākrūram acodayat | [ViPur, 4, 13 82.1]
asāvapy āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 83.1]
na hi kaścid bhagavatā pādaprahāraparikampitajagattrayeṇa suraripuvanitāvaidhavyakāriṇā prabalaripucakrāpratihatacakreṇa cakriṇā madamuditanayanāvalokanākhilaniśātanenātiguruvairivāraṇāpakarṣaṇāvikṛtamahimorusīreṇa sīriṇā ca saha sakalajagadvandyānām amaravarāṇām api yoddhuṃ samarthaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 84.1]
kim utāhaṃ tadanyaḥ śaraṇam abhilaṣyatām ityuktaḥ śatadhanur āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 85.1]
yady asmatparitrāṇāsamarthaṃ bhavān ātmānam adhigacchati tad ayam asmattas tāvan maṇiḥ saṃgṛhya rakṣyatām iti | [ViPur, 4, 13 86.1]
evam uktaḥ so 'py āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 87.1]
yady antyāyām apyavasthāyāṃ na kasmaicid bhavān kathayiṣyati tad aham etaṃ grahīṣyāmīti | [ViPur, 4, 13 88.1]
tathetyukte cākrūras tan maṇiratnaṃ jagrāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 89.1]
śatadhanur apy atulavegāṃ śatayojanavāhinīṃ vaḍavām āruhyāpakrāntaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 90.1]
śaibyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakāśvacatuṣṭayayuktarathasthitau baladevavāsudevau tam anuprayātau | [ViPur, 4, 13 91.1]
sā ca vaḍavā śatayojanapramāṇamārgam atītā punar api vāhyamānā mithilāvanoddeśe prāṇān utsasarja | [ViPur, 4, 13 92.1]
śatadhanur api tāṃ parityajya padātir evādravat | [ViPur, 4, 13 93.1]
kṛṣṇo 'pi balabhadram āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 94.1]
tāvad atra syandane bhavatā stheyam aham enam adhamācāraṃ padātir eva padātim anugamya yāvad ghātayāmi | [ViPur, 4, 13 95.1]
atra hi bhūbhāge dṛṣṭadoṣāḥ sabhayā ato naite 'śvā bhavatemaṃ bhūmibhāgam ullaṅghanīyāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 95.2]
tathety uktvā baladevo ratha eva tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 13 96.1]
kṛṣṇo 'pi dvikrośamātraṃ bhūmibhāgam anusṛtya dūrasthitasyaiva cakraṃ kṣiptvā śatadhanuṣaḥ śiraś cicheda | [ViPur, 4, 13 97.1]
taccharīrāmbarādiṣu ca bahuprakāram anvicchann api syamantakamaṇiṃ nāvāpa yadā tadopagamya balabhadram āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 98.1]
vṛthaivāsmābhiḥ śatadhanur ghātitaḥ na prāptam akhilajagatsārabhūtaṃ tan mahāratnaṃ syamantakākhyam ity ākarṇyodbhūtakopo baladevo vāsudevam āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 99.1]
dhik tvāṃ yas tvam evam arthalipsur etacca te bhrātṛtvān mayā kṣāntaṃ tad ayaṃ panthāḥ svecchayā gamyatāṃ | [ViPur, 4, 13 100.1]
na me dvārakayā na tvayā na cāśeṣabandhubhiḥ kāryam alam alam ebhir mamāgrato 'līkaśapathair ity ākṣipya tatkathāṃ kathaṃcit prasādyamāno 'pi na tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 13 100.2]
sa videhapurīṃ praviveśa | [ViPur, 4, 13 101.1]
janakarājaś cārghyapūrvakam enaṃ gṛhaṃ praveśayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 13 102.1]
sa tatraiva ca tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 13 103.1]
vāsudevo 'pi dvārakām ājagāma | [ViPur, 4, 13 104.1]
yāvacca janakarājagṛhe balabhadro 'vatasthe tāvad dhārtarāṣṭro duryodhanas tatsakāśād gadāśikṣām aśikṣayat | [ViPur, 4, 13 105.1]
varṣatrayānte ca babhrūgrasenaprabhṛtibhir yādavair na tad ratnaṃ kṛṣṇenāpahṛtam iti kṛtāvagatibhir videhanagarīṃ gatvā baladevaḥ saṃpratyāyya dvārakām ānītaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 106.1]
akrūro 'py uttamamaṇisamudbhūtasuvarṇena bhagavaddhyānaparo 'navarataṃ yajñān iyāja | [ViPur, 4, 13 107.1]
savanagatau hi kṣatriyavaiśyau nighnan brahmahā bhavatīty evaṃprakāraṃ dīkṣākavacaṃ praviṣṭa eva tasthau | [ViPur, 4, 13 108.1]
dviṣaṣṭivarṣāṇy evaṃ tanmaṇiprabhāvāt tatropasargadurbhikṣamārikāmaraṇādikaṃ nābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 13 109.1]
athākrūrapakṣīyair bhojaiḥ śatrughne sātvatasya prapautre vyāpādite bhojaiḥ sahākrūro dvārakām apahāyāpakrāntaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 110.1]
tadapakrāntidinād ārabhya tatropasargadurbhikṣavyālānāvṛṣṭimārikādyupadravā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 111.1]
atha yādavā balabhadrograsenasamavetā mantram amantrayan | [ViPur, 4, 13 112.1]
bhagavān uragāriketanaḥ kim idam ekadaiva pracuropadravāgamanam etad ālocyatām ityukte 'ndhakanāmā yaduvṛddhaḥ prāha | [ViPur, 4, 13 113.1]
asyākrūrasya pitṛśvaphalko yatra yatrābhūt tatra tatra durbhikṣamārikānāvṛṣṭyādikaṃ nābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 13 114.1]
kāśīrājasya viṣaye tvanāvṛṣṭyā ca śvaphalko nītaḥ tataś ca tatkṣaṇād devo vavarṣa | [ViPur, 4, 13 115.1]
kāśīrājapatnyāś ca garbhe kanyāratnaṃ pūrvam āsīt | [ViPur, 4, 13 116.1]
sā ca kanyā pūrṇe 'pi prasūtikāle naiva niścakrāma | [ViPur, 4, 13 117.1]
evaṃ ca tasya garbhasya dvādaśa varṣāṇy aniṣkrāmato yayuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 118.1]
kāśīrājaś ca tām ātmajāṃ garbhasthām āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 119.1]
putri kasmān na jāyase niṣkramyatām āsyaṃ te draṣṭum icchāmi etāṃ ca mātaraṃ kim iti ciraṃ kleśayiṣyasīty uktā garbhasthaiva vyājahāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 120.1]
tāta yady ekaikāṃ gāṃ dine dine brāhmaṇāya prayacchasi tad aham anyais tribhir varṣair asmād garbhāt tato 'vaśyaṃ niṣkramiṣyāmītyetad vacanam ākarṇya rājā dine dine brāhmaṇāya gāṃ prādāt | [ViPur, 4, 13 121.1]
sāpi tāvatā kālena jātā | [ViPur, 4, 13 122.1]
tatas tasyāḥ pitā gāndinīti nāma cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 123.1]
tāṃ ca gāndinīṃ kanyāṃ śvaphalkāyopakāriṇe gṛham āgatāyārghyabhūtāṃ prādāt | [ViPur, 4, 13 124.1]
tasyām ayam akrūraḥ śvaphalkājjajñe | [ViPur, 4, 13 125.1]
tasyaivaṃguṇamithunād utpattiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 126.1]
tat katham asminn apakrānte atra durbhikṣamārikādyupadravā na bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 13 127.1]
tad ayam atrānīyatām alam atiguṇavaty aparādhānveṣaṇeneti yaduvṛddhasyāndhakasyaitad vacanam ākarṇya keśavograsenabalabhadrapurogamair yadubhiḥ kṛtāparādhatitikṣubhir abhayaṃ dattvā śvaphalkaputraḥ svapuram ānītaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 128.1]
tatra cāgatamātra eva tasya syamantakamaṇeḥ prabhāvād anāvṛṣṭimārikādurbhikṣavyālādyupadravopaśamā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 129.1]
kṛṣṇaś cintayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 13 130.1]
svalpam etat kāraṇaṃ yad ayaṃ gāndinyāṃ śvaphalkenākrūro janitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 131.1]
sumahāṃś cāyam anāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣamārikādyupadravapratiṣedhakārī prabhāvaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 132.1]
tan nūnam asya sakāśe sa mahāmaṇiḥ syamantakākhyas tiṣṭhati | [ViPur, 4, 13 133.1]
tasya hy evaṃvidhāḥ prabhāvāḥ śrūyante | [ViPur, 4, 13 134.1]
ayam api ca yajñād anantaram anyat kratvantaraṃ tasyānantaram anyad yajñāntaraṃ cājasram avicchinnaṃ yajatīti | [ViPur, 4, 13 135.1]
analpopādānaṃ cāsyāsaṃśayam atrāsau maṇivaras tiṣṭhatīti kṛtādhyavasāyo 'nyat prayojanam uddiśya sakalayādavasamājam ātmagṛha evācīkarat | [ViPur, 4, 13 136.1]
tatra copaviṣṭeṣv akhileṣu yaduṣu pūrvaṃ prayojanam upanyasya paryavasite ca tasmin prasaṅgāntaraparihāsakathām akrūreṇa kṛtvā janārdanas tam akrūram āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 137.1]
dānapate jānīma eva vayaṃ yathā śatadhanvanā tad idam akhilajagatsārabhūtaṃ syamantakaṃ ratnaṃ bhavataḥ samarpitaṃ | [ViPur, 4, 13 138.1]
tad aśeṣarāṣṭropakārakaṃ bhavatsakāśe tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhatu sarva eva vayaṃ tatprabhāvaphalabhujaḥ kiṃtveṣa balabhadro 'smān āśaṅkitavāṃs tad asmatprītaye darśayasvety abhidhāya joṣaṃ sthite bhagavati vāsudeve saratnaḥ so 'cintayat | [ViPur, 4, 13 138.2]
kim atrānuṣṭheyam anyathā ced bravīmy ahaṃ tat kevalāmbaratirodhānam anviṣyanto ratnam ete drakṣyanti ativirodho na kṣama iti saṃcintya tam akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtaṃ nārāyaṇam āhākrūraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 139.1]
bhagavan mamaitat syamantakaratnaṃ śatadhanuṣā samarpitam apagate ca tasminn adya śvaḥ paraśvo vā bhagavān yācayiṣyatīti kṛtamatir atikṛcchreṇaitāvantaṃ kālam adhārayam | [ViPur, 4, 13 140.1]
tasya ca dhāraṇakleśenāham aśeṣopabhogeṣv asaṅgimānaso na vedmi svasukhakalām api | [ViPur, 4, 13 141.1]

tad idaṃ syamantakaratnaṃ gṛhyatām icchayā yasyābhimataṃ tasya samarpyatām | [ViPur, 4, 13 143.1]

muktamātre ca tasminn atikāntyā tad akhilam āsthānam uddyotitam | [ViPur, 4, 13 146.1]
athāhākrūraḥ sa eṣa maṇiḥ śatadhanvanāsmākaṃ samarpitaḥ yasyāyaṃ sa enaṃ gṛhṇātu iti | [ViPur, 4, 13 147.1]
tam ālokya sarvayādavānāṃ sādhu sādhv iti vismitamanasāṃ vāco 'śrūyanta | [ViPur, 4, 13 148.1]
tam ālokyātīva balabhadro mamāyam acyutenaiva sāmānyaḥ samanvicchita iti kṛtaspṛho 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 13 149.1]
mamaivāyaṃ pitṛdhanam ity atīva ca satyabhāmāpi spṛhayāṃcakāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 150.1]
balasatyāvalokanāt kṛṣṇo 'py ātmānaṃ gocakrāntarāvasthitam iva mene | [ViPur, 4, 13 151.1]
sakalayādavasamakṣaṃ cākrūram āha | [ViPur, 4, 13 152.1]
etaddhi maṇiratnam ātmasaṃśodhanāya eteṣāṃ yadūnāṃ mayā darśitam etacca mama balabhadrasya ca sāmānyaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ caitat satyabhāmāyā nānyasyaitat | [ViPur, 4, 13 153.1]
etacca sarvakālaṃ śucinā brahmacaryādiguṇavatā dhriyamāṇam aśeṣarāṣṭrasyopakārakam aśucinā dhriyamāṇam ādhāram eva hanti | [ViPur, 4, 13 154.1]
ato 'ham asya ṣoḍaśastrīsahasraparigrahād asamartho dhāraṇe katham etat satyabhāmā svīkaroti | [ViPur, 4, 13 155.1]
āryabalabhadreṇāpi madirāpānādyaśeṣopabhogaparityāgaḥ kāryaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 156.1]
tad alaṃ yaduloko 'yaṃ balabhadraḥ ahaṃ ca satyā ca tvāṃ dānapate prārthayāmaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 157.1]
tad bhavān eva dhārayituṃ samarthaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 13 158.1]
tvaddhṛtaṃ cāsya rāṣṭrasyopakārakaṃ tad bhavān aśeṣarāṣṭranimittam etat pūrvavad dhārayatvanyan na vaktavyam ity ukto dānapatis tathety āha jagrāha ca tan mahāratnam | [ViPur, 4, 13 159.1]
tataḥ prabhṛtyakrūraḥ prakaṭenaiva tenātijājvalyamānenātmakaṇṭhāvasaktenāditya ivāṃśumālī cacāra | [ViPur, 4, 13 160.1]
ityetad bhagavato mithyābhiśastikṣālanaṃ yaḥ smarati na tasya kadācid alpāpi mithyābhiśastir bhavati avyāhatākhilendriyaścākhilapāpamokṣam avāpnoti | [ViPur, 4, 13 161.1]

parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 14 1.1]
anamitrasya putraḥ śinir nāmābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 1.2]

ityete śaineyāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 4.1]

śvaphalkasyānyaḥ kanīyāṃś citrako nāma bhrātā | [ViPur, 4, 14 6.1]
śvaphalkād akrūro gāndinyām abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 7.1]
tathopamadguḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 8.1]
upamadgor mṛdāmṛdaviśvārimejayagirikṣatropakṣatraśataghnārimardanadharmadṛgdṛṣṭadharmagandhamojavāhaprativāhākhyāḥ putrāḥ sutārākhyā kanyā ca | [ViPur, 4, 14 9.1]
devavān upadevaś cākrūraputrau | [ViPur, 4, 14 10.1]

anor ānakadundubhiḥ tataś cābhijit abhijitaḥ punarvasuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 14.1]

āhukasya devakograsenau dvau putrau | [ViPur, 4, 14 16.1]

tāś ca sarvā vasudeva upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 14 19.1]
ugrasenasyāpi kaṃsanyagrodhasunāmānakāhvaśaṅkusubhūmirāṣṭrapālayuddhatuṣṭisutuṣṭimatsaṃjñāḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 20.1]
kaṃsākaṃsavatīsutanūrāṣṭrapālikāhvāśca ugrasenasya tanūjāḥ kanyāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 21.1]
bhajamānāc ca vidūrathaḥ putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 22.1]

devagarbhasyāpi śūraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 25.1]
śūrasyāpi māriṣā nāma patny abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 26.1]
tasyāṃ cāsau daśa putrān ajanayad vasudevapūrvān | [ViPur, 4, 14 27.1]
vasudevasya jātamātrasyaiva tadgṛhe bhagavadaṃśāvatāram avyāhatadṛṣṭyā paśyadbhir devair divyānakadundubhayo vāditāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 28.1]
tataś cāsāv ānakadundubhisaṃjñām avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 14 29.1]
tasya ca devabhāgadevaśravāṣṭakakakuccakravatsadhārakasṛñjayaśyāmaśamikagaṇḍūṣasaṃjñā nava bhrātaro 'bhavan | [ViPur, 4, 14 30.1]

śūrasya kuntir nāma sakhābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 32.1]
tasmai cāputrāya pṛthām ātmajāṃ vidhinā śūro dattavān | [ViPur, 4, 14 33.1]
tāṃ ca pāṇḍur uvāha | [ViPur, 4, 14 34.1]

pūrvam evānūḍhāyāś ca bhagavatā bhāsvatā kānīnaḥ karṇo nāma putro 'janyata | [ViPur, 4, 14 36.1]
tasyāś ca sapatnī mādrī nāmābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 14 37.1]
tasyāṃ ca nāsatyadasrābhyāṃ nakulasahadevau pāṇḍoḥ putrau janitau | [ViPur, 4, 14 38.1]
śrutadevāṃ tu vṛddhadharmā nāma kārūṣa upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 14 39.1]
tasyāṃ ca dantavakro nāma mahāsuro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 14 40.1]
śrutakīrtim api kekayarājā upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 14 41.1]
tasyāṃ ca saṃtardanādayaḥ kaikeyāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 42.1]
rājādhidevyām āvantyau vindānuvindau jajñāte | [ViPur, 4, 14 43.1]
śrutaśravasam api cedirājo damaghoṣanāmopayeme | [ViPur, 4, 14 44.1]
tasyāṃ ca śiśupālam utpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 14 45.1]
sa vā pūrvam apy udāravikramo daityānām ādipuruṣo hiraṇyakaśipur abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 46.1]
yaś ca bhagavatā sakalalokaguruṇā nārasiṃhena ghātitaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 47.1]
punar api akṣayavīryaśauryasaṃpatparākramaguṇaḥ samākrāntasakalatrailokeśvaraprabhāvo daśānano nāmābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 14 48.1]
bahukālopabhuktabhagavatsakāśāvāptaśarīrapātodbhavapuṇyaphalo bhagavatā rāghavarūpiṇā so 'pi nidhanam upapāditaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 14 49.1]
punaś cedirājasya damaghoṣasyātmajaḥ śiśupālanāmābhavat | [ViPur, 4, 14 50.1]
śiśupālatve 'pi bhagavato bhūbhārāvatāraṇāyāvatīrṇāṃśasya puṇḍarīkanayanākhyasyopari dveṣānubandham atitarāṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 14 51.1]
bhagavatā ca sa nidhanam upānītas tatraiva paramātmabhūte manasa ekāgratayā sāyujyam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 14 52.1]
bhagavān yadi prasanno yathābhilaṣitaṃ dadāti tathā aprasanno 'pi nighnan divyam anupamaṃ sthānaṃ prayacchati | [ViPur, 4, 14 53.1]
{ViPur, 4, 15}
maitreya uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 15 1.1]
hiraṇyakaśiputve ca rāvaṇatve ca viṣṇunā | [ViPur, 4, 15 1.2]
avāpa nihato bhogān aprāpyān amarair api | [ViPur, 4, 15 1.3]
na layaṃ tatra tenaiva nihataḥ sa kathaṃ punaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 2.1]
samprāptaḥ śiśupālatve sāyujyaṃ śāśvate harau | [ViPur, 4, 15 2.2]
etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ vara | [ViPur, 4, 15 3.1]
kautūhalapareṇaitat pṛṣṭo me vaktum arhasi | [ViPur, 4, 15 3.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 15 4.1]
daityeśvarasya vadhāyākhilalokotpattisthitivināśakāriṇā pūrvaṃ tanugrahaṇaṃ kurvatā nṛsiṃharūpam āviṣkṛtam | [ViPur, 4, 15 4.2]
tatra ca hiraṇyakaśiporviṣṇurayamityetanna manasyabhūt | [ViPur, 4, 15 5.1]
niratiśayapuṇyasamudbhūtam etat sattvajātam iti | [ViPur, 4, 15 6.1]
rajodrekapreritaikāgramatis tadbhāvanāyogāt tato 'vāptavadhahaitukīṃ niratiśayām evākhilatrailokyādhikyakāriṇīṃ daśānanatve bhogasaṃpadam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 15 7.1]
na tu sa tasminn anādinidhane parabrahmabhūte bhagavaty anālambini kṛte manasas tallayam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 15 8.1]
evaṃ daśānanatve 'py anaṅgaparādhīnatayā jānakīsamāsaktacetasā bhagavatā dāśarathirūpadhāriṇā hatasya tadrūpadarśanam evāsīt nāyam acyuta ityāsaktirvipadyato 'ntaḥkaraṇe mānuṣabuddhir eva kevalam asyābhūt | [ViPur, 4, 15 9.1]
punar apy acyutavinipātamātraphalam akhilabhūmaṇḍalaślāghyacedirājakule janma avyāhataiśvaryaṃ śiśupālatve 'py avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 15 10.1]
tatra tv akhilānām eva sa bhagavannāmnāṃ tvaṃkārakāraṇam abhavat | [ViPur, 4, 15 11.1]
tataś ca tatkālakṛtānāṃ teṣām aśeṣāṇām evācyutanāmnām anavaratam anekajanmasu vardhitavidveṣānubandhicitto vinindanasaṃtarjanādiṣūccāraṇam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 15 12.1]
tac ca rūpam utphullapadmadalāmalākṣim atyujjvalapītavastradhāryamalakirīṭakeyūrahārakaṭakādiśobhitam udāracaturbāhuśaṅkhacakragadādharam atiprarūḍhavairānubhāvād aṭanabhojanasnānāsanaśayanādiṣv aśeṣāvasthāntareṣu nānyatropayayāvasya cetasaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 13]
tatas tam evākrośeṣūccārayaṃstam eva hṛdayena dhārayann ātmavadhāya yāvad bhagavaddhastacakrāṃśumālojjvalam akṣayatejaḥsvarūpaṃ brahmabhūtam apagatadveṣādidoṣaṃ bhagavantam adrākṣīt | [ViPur, 4, 15 14.1]
tāvac ca bhagavaccakreṇāśu vyāpāditas tatsmaraṇadagdhākhilāghasaṃcayo bhagavatāntam upanītas tasminn eva layam upayayau | [ViPur, 4, 15 15.1]
etat tavākhilaṃ mayābhihitam | [ViPur, 4, 15 16.1]
ayaṃ hi bhagavān kīrtitaś ca saṃsmṛtaś ca dveṣānubandhenāpi akhilasurāsurādidurlabhaṃ phalaṃ prayacchati kimuta samyag bhaktimatām iti | [ViPur, 4, 15 17.1]
vasudevasya tv ānakadundubheḥ pauravīrohiṇīmadirābhadrādevakīpramukhā bahvyaḥ patnyo 'bhavan | [ViPur, 4, 15 18.1]
balabhadraśaṭhasāraṇadurmadādīn putrān rohiṇyām ānakadundubhir utpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 15 19.1]
baladevo 'pi revatyāṃ viśaṭholmukau putrāv ajanayat | [ViPur, 4, 15 20.1]
sārṣṭimārṣṭiśiśusatyasatyadhṛtipramukhāḥ sāraṇātmajāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 21.1]
bhadrāśvabhadrabāhudurdamabhūtādyāḥ rohiṇyāḥ kulajāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 22.1]
nandopanandakṛtakādyā madirāyās tanayāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 23.1]
bhadrāyāś copanidhigadādyāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 24.1]
vaiśālyāṃ ca kauśikam ekam evājanayat | [ViPur, 4, 15 25.1]
ānakadundubher devakyām api kīrtimatsuṣeṇodāyubhadrasenarjadāsabhadradevākhyāḥ ṣaṭ putrā jajñire | [ViPur, 4, 15 26.1]
tāṃśca sarvān eva kaṃso ghātitavān | [ViPur, 4, 15 27.1]
anantaraṃ ca saptamaṃ garbham ardharātre bhagavatprahitā yoganidrā rohiṇyā jaṭharam ākṛṣya nītavatī | [ViPur, 4, 15 28.1]
karṣaṇāccāsāvapi saṃkarṣaṇākhyām agamat | [ViPur, 4, 15 29.1]
tataś ca sakalajaganmahātarumūlabhūto bhūtabhaviṣyadādisakalasurāsuramunijanamanasām apyagocaro 'bjabhavapramukhair analamukhaiḥ praṇamyāvanibhāraharaṇāya prasādito bhagavān anādimadhyanidhano devakīgarbham avatatāra vāsudevaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 30.1]
tatprasādavivardhamānorumahimā ca yoganidrā nandagopapatnyā yaśodāyā garbham adhiṣṭhitavatī | [ViPur, 4, 15 31.1]
suprasannādityacandrādigraham avyālādibhayaṃ svasthamānasam akhilam evaitajjagad apāstādharmam abhavat tasmiṃś ca puṇḍarīkanayane jāyamāne | [ViPur, 4, 15 32.1]
jātena ca tenākhilam evaitat sanmārgavarti jagad akriyata | [ViPur, 4, 15 33.1]
bhagavato 'py atra martyaloke 'vatīrṇasya ṣoḍaśasahasrāṇy ekottaraśatādhikāni bhāryāṇām abhavan | [ViPur, 4, 15 34.1]
tāsāṃ ca rukmiṇīsatyabhāmājāmbavatīcāruhāsinīpramukhā hyaṣṭau patnyaḥ pradhānā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 35.1]
tāsu cāṣṭāvayutāni lakṣaṃ ca putrāṇāṃ bhagavān akhilamūrtir anādimān ajanayat | [ViPur, 4, 15 36.1]
teṣāṃ ca pradyumnacārudeṣṇasāmbādayaḥ trayodaśa pradhānāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 37.1]
pradyumno 'pi rukmiṇas tanayāṃ rukmavatīṃ nāmopayeme | [ViPur, 4, 15 38.1]
tasyām aniruddho jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 15 39.1]
aniruddho 'pi rukmiṇa eva pautrīṃ subhadrāṃ nāmopayeme | [ViPur, 4, 15 40.1]
tasyām asya vajro jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 15 41.1]
vajrasya pratibāhuḥ tasyāpi sucāruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 42.1]
evam anekaśatasahasrapuruṣasaṃkhyasya yadukulasya putrasaṃkhyā varṣaśatair api vaktuṃ na śakyate | [ViPur, 4, 15 43.1]
yato hi ślokāvimāvatra caritārthau | [ViPur, 4, 15 44.1]
tisraḥ koṭyaḥ sahasrāṇām aṣṭāśītiśatāni ca | [ViPur, 4, 15 45.1]
kumārāṇāṃ gṛhācāryāś cāpayogyāsu ye ratāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 45.2]
saṃkhyānaṃ yādavānāṃ kaḥ kariṣyati mahātmanām | [ViPur, 4, 15 46.1]

avatīrṇāḥ kulaśataṃ yatraikābhyadhikaṃ dvija | [ViPur, 4, 15 48.2]

nideśasthāyinas tasya babhūvuḥ sarvayādavāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 15 49.2]

parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 19 1.1]
