divodāsasya putro mitrāyuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 69.1]
mitrāyoś cyavano nāma rājā | [ViPur, 4, 19 70.1]
cyavanāt sudāsaḥ sudāsāt saudāsaḥ saudāsāt sahadevas tasyāpi somakaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 71.1]
somakājjantuḥ putraśatajyeṣṭho 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 19 72.1]
teṣāṃ yavīyān pṛṣataḥ pṛṣatād drupadas tasmācca dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato dhṛṣṭaketuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 73.1]
ajamīḍhasyānyo ṛkṣanāmā putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 19 74.1]
tasya saṃvaraṇaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 75.1]
saṃvaraṇāt kuruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 76.1]
ya idaṃ dharmakṣetraṃ kurukṣetraṃ cakāra | [ViPur, 4, 19 77.1]
sudhanurjahnuparīkṣitpramukhāḥ kuroḥ putrāḥ babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 78.1]
sudhanuṣaḥ putraḥ suhotras tasmāccyavanaḥ cyavanāt kṛtakaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 79.1]
tataś coparicaro vasuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 80.1]
bṛhadrathapratyagrakuśāmbakucelamātsyapramukhāḥ vasoḥ putrāḥ saptājāyanta | [ViPur, 4, 19 81.1]
bṛhadrathāt kuśāgraḥ kuśāgrād vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣabhāt puṣpavān tasmāt satyahitaḥ tasmāt sudhanvā tasya ca jatuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 82.1]
bṛhadrathāccānyaḥ śakaladvayajanmā jarayā saṃdhito jarāsaṃdhanāmā | [ViPur, 4, 19 83.1]
tasmāt sahadevaḥ sahadevāt somapas tataś ca śrutiśravāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 84.1]
ity ete mayā māgadhā bhūpālāḥ kathitāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 19 85.1]
{ViPur, 4, 20}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 20 1.1]
parīkṣitaś ca janamejayaśrutasenograsenabhīmasenāś catvāraḥ putrāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 1.2]
jahnos tu suratho nāmātmajo babhūva | [ViPur, 4, 20 2.1]
tasyāpi vidūrathaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 3.1]
tasmāt sārvabhaumaḥ sārvabhaumājjayatsenas tasmādārādhitas tataścāyutāyur ayutāyor akrodhanaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 4.1]
tasmād devātithiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 5.1]
tataś ca ṛkṣo 'nyo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 20 6.1]
ṛkṣād bhīmasenas tataś ca dilīpaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 7.1]
dilīpāt pratīpaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 8.1]
tasyāpi devāpiśaṃtanubāhlīkasaṃjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 9.1]
devāpir bāla evāraṇyaṃ viveśa | [ViPur, 4, 20 10.1]
śaṃtanus tu mahīpālo 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 20 11.1]
ayaṃ ca tasya ślokaḥ pṛthivyāṃ gīyate | [ViPur, 4, 20 12.1]
yaṃ yaṃ karābhyāṃ spṛśati jīrṇaṃ yauvanam eti saḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 13.1]
śāntiṃ cāpnoti yenāgryāṃ karmaṇā tena śāṃtanuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 13.2]
tasya ca śaṃtano rāṣṭre dvādaśavarṣāṇi devo na vavarṣa | [ViPur, 4, 20 14.1]
tataś cāśeṣarāṣṭravināśam avekṣyāsau rājā brāhmaṇān apṛcchat kasmād asmākaṃ rāṣṭre devo na varṣati ko mamāparādha iti | [ViPur, 4, 20 15.1]
tataś ca tam ūcur brāhmaṇāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 16.1]
agrajasya te hīyam avanis tvayā saṃbhujyate ataḥ parivettā tvam ity uktaḥ sa rājā punas tān apṛcchat | [ViPur, 4, 20 17.1]
kiṃ mayātra vidheyam iti | [ViPur, 4, 20 18.1]
tatas te punar apy ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 19.1]
yāvad devāpir na patanādibhir doṣair abhibhūyate tāvad etat tasyārhaṃ rājyam | [ViPur, 4, 20 20.1]
tad alam etena tu tasmai dīyatām ity ukte tasya mantripravareṇāśmarāviṇā tatrāraṇye tapasvino vedavādavirodhavaktāraḥ prayuktāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 21.1]
tair asyāpy atiṛjumater mahīpatiputrasya buddhir vedavādavirodhamārgānusāriṇy akriyata | [ViPur, 4, 20 22.1]
rājā ca śaṃtanur dvijavacanotpannaparidevanaśokas tān brāhmaṇān agrataḥ kṛtvāgrajasya pradānāyāraṇyaṃ jagāma | [ViPur, 4, 20 23.1]
tadāśramam upagatāś ca tam avanatam avanīpatiputraṃ devāpim upatasthuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 24.1]
te brāhmaṇā vedavādānubandhīni vacāṃsi rājyam agrajena kartavyam ity arthavanti tam ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 25.1]
asāv api devāpir vedavādavirodhayuktidūṣitam anekaprakāraṃ tān āha | [ViPur, 4, 20 26.1]
tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ śaṃtanum ūcuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 27.1]
āgaccha he rājann alam atrātinirbandhena praśānta evāsāv anāvṛṣṭidoṣaḥ patito 'yam anādikālam abhihitavedavacanadūṣaṇoccāraṇāt | [ViPur, 4, 20 28.1]
patite cāgraje naiva te parivettṛtvaṃ bhavatīty uktaḥ śaṃtanuḥ svapuram āgamya rājyam akarot | [ViPur, 4, 20 29.1]
vedavādavirodhavacanoccāraṇadūṣite ca tasmin devāpau tiṣṭhaty api jyeṣṭhabhrātary akhilasya niṣpattaye vavarṣa bhagavān parjanyaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 30.1]
bāhlīkāt somadattaḥ putro 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 20 31.1]
somadattasyāpi bhūribhūriśravaśalyasaṃjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 32.1]
śaṃtanor apy amaranadyāṃ jāhnavyām udārakīrtir aśeṣaśāstrārthavid bhīṣmaḥ putro 'bhūt | [ViPur, 4, 20 33.1]
satyavatyāṃ ca citrāṅgadavicitravīryau dvau putrāv utpādayāmāsa śaṃtanuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 34.1]
citrāṅgadas tu bāla eva citrāṅgadenaiva gandharveṇāhave nihataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 35.1]
vicitravīryo 'pi kāśīrājatanaye ambāmbālike upayeme | [ViPur, 4, 20 36.1]
tadupabhogātikhedāc ca yakṣmaṇā gṛhītaḥ sa pañcatvam agamat | [ViPur, 4, 20 37.1]
satyavatīniyogāc ca matputraḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano mātur vacanam anatikramaṇīyam iti kṛtvā vicitravīryakṣetre dhṛtarāṣṭrapāṇḍū tatprahitabhujiṣyāyāṃ viduraṃ cotpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 20 38.1]
dhṛtarāṣṭro 'pi gāndhāryāṃ duryodhanaduḥśāsanapradhānaṃ putraśatam utpādayāmāsa | [ViPur, 4, 20 39.1]
pāṇḍor apyaraṇye mṛgayāyām ṛṣiśāpopahataprajājananasāmarthyasya dharmavāyuśakrair yudhiṣṭhirabhīmasenārjunāḥ kuntyāṃ nakulasahadevau cāśvibhyāṃ mādryāṃ pañca putrāḥ samutpāditāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 40.1]
teṣāṃ ca draupadyāṃ pañcaiva putrā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 20 41.1]
yudhiṣṭhirāt prativindhyaḥ bhīmasenācchrutasenaḥ śrutakīrtir arjunācchrutānīko nakulācchrutakarmā sahadevāt | [ViPur, 4, 20 42.1]
anye ca pāṇḍavānām ātmajās tad yathā | [ViPur, 4, 20 43.1]
yaudheyī yudhiṣṭhirād devakaṃ putram avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 20 44.1]
hiḍimbā ghaṭotkacaṃ bhīmasenāt putraṃ lebhe | [ViPur, 4, 20 45.1]
kāśī ca bhīmasenād eva sarvagaṃ sutam avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 20 46.1]
sahadevācca vijayī suhotraṃ putram avāpa | [ViPur, 4, 20 47.1]
reṇumatyāṃ ca nakulo 'pi niramitram ajījanat | [ViPur, 4, 20 48.1]
arjunasyāpy ulūpyāṃ nāgakanyāyām irāvān nāma putro 'bhavat | [ViPur, 4, 20 49.1]
maṇipurapatiputryāṃ putrikādharmeṇa babhruvāhanaṃ nāma putram arjuno 'janayat | [ViPur, 4, 20 50.1]
subhadrāyāṃ cārbhakatve 'pi yo 'sāv atibalaparākramaḥ samastārātirathajetā so 'bhimanyur ajāyata | [ViPur, 4, 20 51.1]
abhimanyor uttarāyāṃ parikṣīṇeṣu kuruṣv aśvatthāmaprayuktabrahmāstreṇa garbha eva bhasmīkṛto bhagavataḥ sakalasurāsuravanditacaraṇayugalasyātmecchayā kāraṇamānuṣarūpadhāriṇo 'nubhāvāt punar jīvitam avāpya parīkṣij jajñe | [ViPur, 4, 20 52.1]
yo 'yaṃ sāmpratam etad bhūmaṇḍalam akhaṇḍitāyatidharmeṇa pālayatīti | [ViPur, 4, 20 53.1]
{ViPur, 4, 21}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 21 1.1]
ataḥ paraṃ bhaviṣyān ahaṃ bhūpālān kīrtayiṣyāmi | [ViPur, 4, 21 1.2]
yo 'yaṃ sāmpratam avanīpatiḥ parīkṣit tasyāpi janamejayaśrutasenograsenabhīmasenāś catvāraḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 21 2.1]
janamejayasyāpi śatānīko bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 21 3.1]
yo 'sau yājñavalkyād vedam adhītya kṛpād astrāṇyavāpya viṣamaviṣayaviraktacittavṛttiś ca śaunakopadeśād ātmajñānapravīṇaḥ paraṃ nirvāṇam avāpsyati | [ViPur, 4, 21 4.1]
śatānīkād aśvamedhadatto bhavitā | [ViPur, 4, 21 5.1]
tasmād apy adhisīmakṛṣṇaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 6.1]
adhisīmakṛṣṇānnicaknuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 7.1]
yo gaṅgayāpahṛte hastinapure kauśāmbyāṃ nivatsyati | [ViPur, 4, 21 8.1]
tasyāpy uṣṇaḥ putro bhavitā | [ViPur, 4, 21 9.1]
uṣṇād vicitrarathaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 10.1]
tataḥ śucirathaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 11.1]
tasmād vṛṣṇimāṃs tataḥ suṣeṇas tasyāpi sunīthaḥ sunīthān nṛpacakṣus tasmād api sukhibalas tasya ca pāriplavas tataś ca sunayas tasyāpi medhāvī | [ViPur, 4, 21 12.1]
medhāvino ripuñjayas tato 'rvas tasmācca tigmas tasmād bṛhadrathaḥ bṛhadrathād vasudāsaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 13.1]
tato 'paraḥ śatānīkaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 14.1]
tasmāccodayana udayanād vihīnaras tataśca daṇḍapāṇis tato nimittaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 15.1]
tasmācca kṣemakaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 16.1]
atrāyaṃ ślokaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 17.1]
brahmakṣatrasya yo yonir vaṃśo rājarṣisatkṛtaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 21 18.1]
kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ sa saṃsthāṃ prāpsyate kalau | [ViPur, 4, 21 18.2]
iti | [ViPur, 4, 21 18.3]
{ViPur, 4, 22}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 22 1.1]
ataścekṣvākavo bhaviṣyāḥ pārthivāḥ kathyante | [ViPur, 4, 22 1.2]
bṛhadbalasya putro bṛhatkṣaṇaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 22 2.1]

{ViPur, 4, 23}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 23 1.1]

atra hi vaṃśe mahābalaparākramā jarāsaṃdhapradhānā babhūvuḥ | [ViPur, 4, 23 2.1]

{ViPur, 4, 24}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 4, 24 1.1]
yo 'yaṃ ripuñjayo nāma bārhadratho 'ntyaḥ tasyāmātyo muniko nāma bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 1.2]
sa cainaṃ svāminaṃ hatvā svaputraṃ pradyotanāmānam abhiṣekṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 2.1]
tasyāpi balākanāmā putro bhavitā | [ViPur, 4, 24 3.1]
tataś ca viśākhayūpaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 4.1]
tatputro janakaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 5.1]
tasya ca nandivardhanaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 6.1]
tato nandī | [ViPur, 4, 24 7.1]
ity ete 'ṣṭatriṃśaduttaram aṣṭaśataṃ pañca pradyotāḥ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 8.1]
tataś ca śiśunābhaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 9.1]
tatputraḥ kākavarṇo bhavitā | [ViPur, 4, 24 10.1]
tasya ca putraḥ kṣemadharmā | [ViPur, 4, 24 11.1]
tasyāpi kṣataujāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 12.1]
tatputro vidhisāraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 13.1]
tataś cājātaśatruḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 14.1]
tasmād arbhakaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 15.1]
tasmāccodayanaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 16.1]
tasmād api nandivardhanaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 17.1]
tato mahānandī | [ViPur, 4, 24 18.1]
ity ete śaiśanābhā bhūpālās trīṇi varṣaśatāni dviṣaṣṭyadhikāni bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 19.1]
mahānandinas tataḥ śūdrāgarbhodbhavo 'tilubdho 'tibalo mahāpadmanāmā nandaḥ paraśurāma ivāparo 'khilakṣatrāntakārī bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 20.1]
tataḥ prabhṛti śūdrā bhūpālā bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 21.1]
sa caikacchattrām anullaṅghitaśāsano mahāpadmaḥ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyate | [ViPur, 4, 24 22.1]
tasyāpy aṣṭau sutāḥ sumālyādyā bhavitāraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 23.1]
tasya mahāpadmasyānu pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 24.1]
mahāpadmaputrāś caikaṃ varṣaśatam avanīpatayo bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 25.1]
tataś ca nava caitān nandān kauṭilyo brāhmaṇaḥ samuddhariṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 26.1]
teṣām abhāve mauryāḥ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 27.1]
kauṭilya eva candraguptam utpannaṃ rājye 'bhiṣekṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 28.1]
tasyāpi putro bindusāro bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 29.1]
tasyāpy aśokavardhanas tataḥ suyaśās tataś ca daśarathas tataś ca samyutas tataḥ śāliśūkas tasmāt somaśarmā tasyāpi somaśarmaṇaḥ śatadhanvā | [ViPur, 4, 24 30.1]
tasyānu bṛhadrathanāmā bhavitā | [ViPur, 4, 24 31.1]
evam ete mauryā daśa bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti abdaśataṃ saptatriṃśaduttaram | [ViPur, 4, 24 32.1]
teṣām ante pṛthivīṃ daśa śuṅgā bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 33.1]
puṣyamitraḥ senāpatiḥ svāminaṃ hatvā rājyaṃ kariṣyati tasyātmajo 'gnimitraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 34.1]
tasmāt sujyeṣṭhas tato vasumitras tasmād apy udaṅkas tataḥ pulindakas tato ghoṣavasus tasmād api vajramitras tato bhāgavataḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 35.1]
tasmād devabhūtiḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 36.1]
ityete śuṅgā dvādaśottaraṃ varṣaśataṃ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 37.1]
tataḥ kaṇvān eṣā bhūr yāsyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 38.1]
devabhūtiṃ tu śuṅgarājānaṃ vyasaninaṃ tasyaivāmātyaḥ kaṇvo vasudevanāmā taṃ nihatya svayam avanīṃ bhokṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 39.1]
tasya putro bhūmitras tasyāpi nārāyaṇaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 40.1]
nārāyaṇātmajaḥ suśarmā | [ViPur, 4, 24 41.1]
ete kāṇvāyanāścatvāraḥ pañcacatvāriṃśad varṣāṇi bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 42.1]
suśarmāṇaṃ tu kāṇvaṃ tadbhṛtyo balipucchakanāmā hatvāndhrajātīyo vasudhāṃ bhokṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 43.1]
tataś ca kṛṣṇanāmā tadbhrātā pṛthivīpatir bhaviṣyati | [ViPur, 4, 24 44.1]
tasyāpi putraḥ śāntakarṇis tasyāpi pūrṇotsaṅgas tatputraḥ śātakarṇis tasmācca lambodaras tasmācca pilakas tato meghasvātis tataḥ paṭumān | [ViPur, 4, 24 45.1]
tataś cāriṣṭakarmā tato hālāhalaḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 46.1]
hālāhalāt palalakas tataḥ pulindasenas tataḥ sundaras tataḥ śātakarṇis tataḥ śivasvātis tataś ca gomatiputras tatputro 'limān | [ViPur, 4, 24 47.1]
tasyāpi śāntakarṇis tataḥ śivaśritas tataś ca śivaskandhas tasmād api yajñaśrīs tato dviyajñas tasmāccandraśrīḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 48.1]
tasmāt pulomāpi hi | [ViPur, 4, 24 49.1]
evam ete triṃśaccatvāryabdaśatāni ṣaṭpañcāśadadhikāni pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 50.1]
āndhrabhṛtyāḥ saptābhīraprabhṛtayo daśa gardabhinaś ca bhūbhujo bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 51.1]
tataḥ ṣoḍaśa bhūpatayo bhavitāraḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 52.1]
tataś cāṣṭau yavanāś caturdaśa turuṣkārā muṇḍāśca trayodaśa ekādaśa maunā ete vai pṛthivīpatayaḥ pṛthivīṃ daśavarṣaśatāni navatyadhikāni bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 53.1]
tataś ca maunā ekādaśa bhūpatayo 'bdaśatāni trīṇi pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 54.1]
teṣūtsanneṣu kaiṅkilā yavanā bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanty amūrdhābhiṣiktāḥ | [ViPur, 4, 24 55.1]
teṣām apatyaṃ vindhyaśaktis tataḥ purañjayas tasmād rāmacandras tasmāddharmavarmā tato vaṅgas tato 'bhūnnandanas tataḥ sunandī tadbhrātā nandiyaśāḥ śukraḥ pravīra ete varṣaśataṃ ṣaḍ varṣāṇi bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti | [ViPur, 4, 24 56.1]

{ViPur, 5, 23}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 5, 23 1.1]

{ViPur, 5, 32}

dharmo yathābhirucitair anuṣṭhānair anuṣṭhitaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 1 15.2]

suvarṇamaṇiratnādau vastre copakṣayaṃ gate | [ViPur, 6, 1 17.1]

{ViPur, 6, 2}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 2 1.1]
vyāsaś cāha mahābuddhir yad atraiva hi vastuni | [ViPur, 6, 2 1.2]
tacchrūyatāṃ mahābhāga gadato mama tattvataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 1.3]
kasmin kāle 'lpako dharmo dadāti sumahat phalam | [ViPur, 6, 2 2.1]
munīnām apy abhūd vādaḥ kaiś cāsau kriyate sukham | [ViPur, 6, 2 2.2]
saṃdehanirṇayārthāya vedavyāsaṃ mahāmunim | [ViPur, 6, 2 3.1]
yayus te saṃśayaṃ praṣṭuṃ maitreya munipuṃgavāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 3.2]
dadṛśus te muniṃ tatra jāhnavīsalile dvija | [ViPur, 6, 2 4.1]
vedavyāsaṃ mahābhāgam ardhasnātaṃ sutaṃ mama | [ViPur, 6, 2 4.2]
snānāvasānaṃ te tasya pratīkṣanto maharṣayaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 5.1]
tasthus taṭe mahānadyās taruṣaṇḍam upāśritāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 5.2]
magno 'tha jāhnavītoyād utthāyāha suto mama | [ViPur, 6, 2 6.1]
vyāsaḥ sādhuḥ kaliḥ sādhur ity evaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ vacaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 6.2]
teṣāṃ munīnāṃ bhūyaś ca mamajja sa nadījale | [ViPur, 6, 2 6.3]
utthāya sādhu sādhv iti śūdra dhanyo 'si cābravīt | [ViPur, 6, 2 7.1]
nimagnaś ca samutthāya punaḥ prāha mahāmuniḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 8.1]
yoṣitaḥ sādhu dhanyās tās tābhyo dhanyataro 'sti kaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 8.2]
tataḥ snātvā yathānyāyam ācāntaṃ taṃ kṛtakriyam | [ViPur, 6, 2 9.1]
upatasthur mahābhāgā munayas te sutaṃ mama | [ViPur, 6, 2 9.2]
kṛtasaṃvandanāṃś cāha kṛtāsanaparigrahān | [ViPur, 6, 2 10.1]
kimartham āgatā yūyam iti satyavatīsutaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 10.2]
tam ūcuḥ saṃśayaṃ praṣṭuṃ bhavantaṃ vayam āgatāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 11.1]
alaṃ tenāstu tāvan naḥ kathyatām aparaṃ tvayā | [ViPur, 6, 2 11.2]
kaliḥ sādhv iti yat proktaṃ śūdraḥ sādhv iti yoṣitaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 12.1]
yaccāha bhagavān sādhu dhanyāś ceti punaḥ punaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 12.2]
tat sarvaṃ śrotum icchāmo na ced guhyaṃ mahāmune | [ViPur, 6, 2 13.1]
tat kathyatāṃ tato hṛtsthaṃ pṛcchāmas tvāṃ prayojanam | [ViPur, 6, 2 13.2]
ity ukto munibhir vyāsaḥ prahasyedam athābravīt | [ViPur, 6, 2 14.1]
śrūyatāṃ bho muniśreṣṭhā yad uktaṃ sādhu sādhv iti | [ViPur, 6, 2 14.2]
yat kṛte daśabhir varṣais tretāyāṃ hāyanena tat | [ViPur, 6, 2 15.1]
dvāpare tacca māsena ahorātreṇa tat kalau | [ViPur, 6, 2 15.2]
tapaso brahmacaryasya japādeś ca phalaṃ dvijāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 16.1]
prāpnoti puruṣas tena kaliḥ sādhv iti bhāṣitam | [ViPur, 6, 2 16.2]
dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñais tretāyāṃ dvāpare 'rcayan | [ViPur, 6, 2 17.1]
yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṃkīrtya keśavam | [ViPur, 6, 2 17.2]
dharmotkarṣam atīvātra prāpnoti puruṣaḥ kalau | [ViPur, 6, 2 18.1]
svalpāyāsena dharmajñās tena tuṣṭo 'smy ahaṃ kaleḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 18.2]
vratacaryopahāraiś ca grāhyo vedo dvijātibhiḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 19.1]
tataḥ svadharmasamprāptair yaṣṭavyaṃ vidhivad dhanaiḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 19.2]
vṛthā kathā vṛthā bhojyaṃ vṛthejyā ca dvijanmanām | [ViPur, 6, 2 20.1]
patanāya tathā bhāvyaṃ tais tu saṃyamibhiḥ sadā | [ViPur, 6, 2 20.2]
asamyakkaraṇe doṣas teṣāṃ sarveṣu vastuṣu | [ViPur, 6, 2 21.1]
bhojyapeyādikaṃ caiṣāṃ necchāprāptikaraṃ dvijāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 21.2]
pāratantryaṃ samasteṣu teṣāṃ kāryeṣu vai tataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 22.1]
jayanti te nijāṃllokān kleśena mahatā dvijāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 22.2]
dvijaśuśrūṣayaivaiṣa pākayajñādhikāravān | [ViPur, 6, 2 23.1]
nijāñjayati vai lokāñśūdro dhanyataras tataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 23.2]
bhakṣyābhakṣyeṣu nāsyāsti peyāpeyeṣu vai yataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 24.1]
niyamo muniśārdūlās tenāsau sādhv itīritam | [ViPur, 6, 2 24.2]
svadharmasyāvirodhena narair labdhaṃ dhanaṃ sadā | [ViPur, 6, 2 25.1]
pratipādyaṃ ca pātreṣu yaṣṭavyaṃ ca yathāvidhi | [ViPur, 6, 2 25.2]
tasyārjane mahān kleśaḥ pālane ca dvijottamāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 26.1]
tathāsadviniyogāya vijñeyaṃ gahanaṃ nṛṇām | [ViPur, 6, 2 26.2]
ebhir anyais tathā kleśaiḥ puruṣo dvijasattamāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 27.1]
nijāñjayati vai lokān prājāpatyādikān kramāt | [ViPur, 6, 2 27.2]
yoṣicchuśrūṣaṇaṃ bhartuḥ karmaṇā manasā girā | [ViPur, 6, 2 28.1]
kurvatī samavāpnoti tatsālokyaṃ yato dvijāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 28.2]
nātikleśena mahatā tān eva puruṣo yathā | [ViPur, 6, 2 29.1]
tṛtīyaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ tena mayā sādhv iti yoṣitām | [ViPur, 6, 2 29.2]
etad vaḥ kathitaṃ viprā yannimittam ihāgatāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 30.1]
tat pṛcchata yathākāmaṃ ahaṃ vakṣyāmi vaḥ sphuṭam | [ViPur, 6, 2 30.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 2 31.1]
tatas te munayaḥ procur yat praṣṭavyaṃ mahāmune | [ViPur, 6, 2 31.2]
anyasminn eva tat praśne yathāvat kathitaṃ tvayā | [ViPur, 6, 2 31.3]
tataḥ prahasya tān prāha kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 32.1]
vismayotphullanayanāṃs tāpasāṃs tān upāgatān | [ViPur, 6, 2 32.2]
mayaiṣa bhavatāṃ praśno jñāto divyena cakṣuṣā | [ViPur, 6, 2 33.1]
tato hi vaḥ prasaṅgena sādhu sādhv iti bhāṣitam | [ViPur, 6, 2 33.2]
svalpena hi prayatnena dharmaḥ sidhyati vai kalau | [ViPur, 6, 2 34.1]
narair ātmaguṇāmbhobhiḥ kṣālitākhilakilbiṣaiḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 34.2]
śūdraiś ca dvijaśuśrūṣātatparair munisattamāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 35.1]
tathā strībhir anāyāsāt patiśuśrūṣayaiva hi | [ViPur, 6, 2 35.2]
tatas tritayam apy etan mama dhanyatamaṃ matam | [ViPur, 6, 2 36.1]
dharmasaṃsādhane kleśo dvijātīnāṃ kṛtādiṣu | [ViPur, 6, 2 36.2]
bhavadbhir yad abhipretaṃ tad etat kathitaṃ mayā | [ViPur, 6, 2 37.1]
apṛṣṭenāpi dharmajñāḥ kim anyat kriyatāṃ dvijāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 37.2]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 2 38.1]
tataḥ sampūjya te vyāsaṃ praśaśaṃsuḥ punaḥ punaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 38.2]
yathāgataṃ dvijā jagmur vyāsoktikṣatasaṃśayāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 2 38.3]
bhavato 'pi mahābhāga rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā | [ViPur, 6, 2 39.1]

{ViPur, 6, 3}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 3 1.1]

naimittikaḥ prākṛtikas tathaivātyantiko mataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 1.3]
brāhmo naimittikas teṣāṃ kalpānte pratisaṃcaraḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 2.1]
ātyantikaś ca mokṣākhyaḥ prākṛto dviparārdhikaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 2.2]
maitreya uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 3 3.1]
parārdhasaṃkhyāṃ bhagavan mamācakṣva yayā tu saḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 3.2]
dviguṇīkṛtayā jñeyaḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 3.3]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 3 4.1]
sthānāt sthānaṃ daśaguṇam ekasmād gaṇyate dvija | [ViPur, 6, 3 4.2]
tato 'ṣṭādaśame bhāge parārdham abhidhīyate | [ViPur, 6, 3 4.3]
parārdhadviguṇaṃ yat tu prākṛtaḥ sa layo dvija | [ViPur, 6, 3 5.1]
tadāvyakte 'khilaṃ vyaktaṃ svahetau layam eti vai | [ViPur, 6, 3 5.2]
nimeṣo mānuṣo yo 'yaṃ mātrāmātrapramāṇataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 6.1]

nāḍikā tu pramāṇena kalā daśa ca pañca ca | [ViPur, 6, 3 7.1]
unmānenāmbhasaḥ sā tu palāny ardhatrayodaśa | [ViPur, 6, 3 8.1]

ahorātraṃ muhūrtās tu triṃśan māso dinais tathā | [ViPur, 6, 3 9.2]
māsair dvādaśabhir varṣam ahorātraṃ tu tad divi | [ViPur, 6, 3 10.1]
tribhir varṣaśatair varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭyā caivāsuradviṣām | [ViPur, 6, 3 10.2]
tais tu dvādaśasāhasraiś caturyugam udāhṛtam | [ViPur, 6, 3 11.1]
caturyugasahasraṃ tu kathyate brahmaṇo dinam | [ViPur, 6, 3 11.2]
sa kalpas tatra manavaś caturdaśa mahāmune | [ViPur, 6, 3 12.1]
tadante caiva maitreya brāhmo naimittiko layaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 12.2]
tasya svarūpam atyugraṃ maitreya gadato mama | [ViPur, 6, 3 13.1]
śṛṇuṣva prākṛtaṃ bhūyas tava vakṣyāmy ahaṃ layam | [ViPur, 6, 3 13.2]
caturyugasahasrānte kṣīṇaprāye mahītale | [ViPur, 6, 3 14.1]
anāvṛṣṭir atīvogrā jāyate śatavārṣikī | [ViPur, 6, 3 14.2]
tato yāny alpasārāṇi tāni sattvāny aśeṣataḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 15.1]
kṣayaṃ yānti muniśreṣṭha pārthivāny anupīḍanāt | [ViPur, 6, 3 15.2]
tataḥ sa bhagavān kṛṣṇo rudrarūpadharo 'vyayaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 16.1]
kṣayāya yatate kartum ātmasthāḥ sakalāḥ prajāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 16.2]
tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇur bhānoḥ saptasu raśmiṣu | [ViPur, 6, 3 17.1]
sthitaḥ pibaty aśeṣāṇi jalāni munisattama | [ViPur, 6, 3 17.2]
pītvāmbhāṃsi samastāni prāṇibhūmigatāni vai | [ViPur, 6, 3 18.1]
śoṣaṃ nayati maitreya samastaṃ pṛthivītalam | [ViPur, 6, 3 18.2]
samudrān saritaḥ śailān śailaprasravaṇāni ca | [ViPur, 6, 3 19.1]
pātāleṣu ca yat toyaṃ tat sarvaṃ nayati kṣayam | [ViPur, 6, 3 19.2]
tatas tasyānubhāvena toyāhāropabṛṃhitāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 20.1]
ta eva raśmayaḥ sapta jāyante sapta bhāskarāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 20.2]
adhaś cordhvaṃ ca te dīptās tataḥ sapta divākarāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 21.1]
dahanty aśeṣaṃ trailokyaṃ sapātālatalaṃ dvija | [ViPur, 6, 3 21.2]
dahyamānaṃ tu tair dīptais trailokyaṃ dvija bhāskaraiḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 22.1]
sādrinadyarṇavābhogaṃ niḥsneham abhijāyate | [ViPur, 6, 3 22.2]
tato nirdagdhavṛkṣāmbu trailokyam akhilaṃ dvija | [ViPur, 6, 3 23.1]
bhavaty eṣā ca vasudhā kūrmapṛṣṭhopamākṛtiḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 23.2]
tataḥ kālāgnirudro 'sau bhūtvā sarvaharo hariḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 24.1]
śeṣāhiśvāsasambhūtaḥ pātālāni dahaty adhaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 24.2]

bhūmim abhyetya sakalaṃ babhasti vasudhātalam | [ViPur, 6, 3 25.2]
bhuvarlokaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ svarlokaṃ ca sudāruṇaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 26.1]
jvālāmālāmahāvartas tatraiva parivartate | [ViPur, 6, 3 26.2]

jvālāvartaparīvāram upakṣīṇacarācaram | [ViPur, 6, 3 27.2]
tatas tāpaparītās tu lokadvayanivāsinaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 28.1]
kṛtādhikārā gacchanti maharlokaṃ mahāmune | [ViPur, 6, 3 28.2]

gacchanti janalokaṃ te daśāvṛttyā paraiṣiṇaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 29.2]
tato dagdhvā jagat sarvaṃ rudrarūpī janārdanaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 30.1]
mukhaniśvāsajān meghān karoti munisattama | [ViPur, 6, 3 30.2]
tato gajakulaprakhyās taḍidvanto ninādinaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 31.1]
uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakā ghanāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 31.2]
kecin nīlotpalaśyāmāḥ kecit kumudasaṃnibhāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 32.1]
dhūmravarṇā ghanāḥ kecit kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ | [ViPur, 6, 3 32.2]
kecid rāsabhavarṇābhā lākṣārasanibhās tathā | [ViPur, 6, 3 33.1]
kecid vaiḍūryasaṃkāśā indranīlanibhāḥ kvacit | [ViPur, 6, 3 33.2]

{ViPur, 6, 4}
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 4 1.1]

{ViPur, 6, 5}

janakāya purā yogaṃ tathāhaṃ kathayāmi te | [ViPur, 6, 6 5.3]
maitreya uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 6 6.1]
khāṇḍikyaḥ ko 'bhavad brahman ko vā keśidhvajo 'bhavat | [ViPur, 6, 6 6.2]
kathaṃ tayoś ca saṃvādo yogasaṃbandhavān abhūt | [ViPur, 6, 6 6.3]
parāśara uvāca | [ViPur, 6, 6 7.1]
dharmadhvajo vai janakas tasya putro 'mitadhvajaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 6 7.2]
kṛtadhvajaś ca nāmnāsīt sadādhyātmaratir nṛpaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 6 7.3]

putro 'mitadhvajasyāpi khāṇḍikyajanako 'bhavat | [ViPur, 6, 6 8.2]

yajñair yajñavido yajanti satataṃ yajñeśvaraṃ karmiṇo yaṃ yaṃ brahmamayaṃ parāparaparaṃ dhyāyanti ca jñāninaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 8 57.1]
yaṃ samprāpya na jāyate na mriyate no vardhate hīyate naivāsan na ca sad bhavaty ati tataḥ kiṃ vā hareḥ śrūyatām | [ViPur, 6, 8 57.2]
kavyaṃ yaḥ pitṛrūpadhṛg vidhihutaṃ havyaṃ ca bhuṅkte vibhur devatve bhagavān anādinidhanaḥ svāhāsvadhāsaṃjñitaḥ | [ViPur, 6, 8 58.1]
yasmin brahmaṇi sarvaśaktinilaye mānāni no mānināṃ niṣṭhāyai prabhavanti hanti kaluṣaṃ śrotraṃ sa yāto hariḥ | [ViPur, 6, 8 58.2]
nānto 'sti yasya na ca yasya samudbhavo 'sti vṛddhir na yasya pariṇāmavivarjitasya | [ViPur, 6, 8 59.1]
nāpakṣayaṃ ca samupaity avikalpavastu yas taṃ nato 'smi puruṣottamam īśam īḍyam | [ViPur, 6, 8 59.2]
tasyaiva yo 'nuguṇabhug bahudhaika eva śuddho 'py aśuddha iva mūrtivibhāgabhedaiḥ | [ViPur, 6, 8 60.1]
jñānānvitaḥ sakalatattvavibhūtikartā tasmai nato 'smi puruṣāya sadāvyayāya | [ViPur, 6, 8 60.2]
jñānapravṛttiniyamaikyamayāya puṃso bhogapradānapaṭave triguṇātmakāya | [ViPur, 6, 8 61.1]
avyākṛtāya bhavabhāvanakāraṇāya vande svarūpabhavanāya sadājarāya | [ViPur, 6, 8 61.2]
vyomānilāgnijalabhūracanāmayāya śabdādibhogyaviṣayopanayakṣamāya | [ViPur, 6, 8 62.1]
puṃsaḥ samastakaraṇair upakārakāya vyaktāya sūkṣmavimalāya sadā nato 'smi | [ViPur, 6, 8 62.2]
iti vividham ajasya yasya rūpaṃ prakṛtiparātmamayaṃ sanātanasya | [ViPur, 6, 8 63.1]
pradiśatu bhagavān aśeṣapuṃsāṃ harir apajanmajarādikāṃ sa siddhim | [ViPur, 6, 8 63.2]
